Chapter i. Peter breaks k'fai ek' kanu, kaula veh, tor'ovau abru. Au ak fai-tor ik au dungi tor'ovau abru, heh wuh yut wendy fai-tor vesh' nash. Veh gad lu she vesh' dahkuh tevun hinek she vesh' mavaun svi' wuh bah-ker, heh she plucked wuh'ashiv svai heh sahr-tor k' ish-veh tor ish-veh ko-mekh. I suppose she bolau ma glazhau rather delightful, na' mrs. Ashal-veh shitau ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh khaf-spol heh maf-tor, “oh, po mokuhlek’t du hafau spo' nash na' ek'wak!” nash vesh' ek' ik be' dvun-tor svi' au fi' wuh subject, tonk'peh henceforth wendy fai-tor ik she bolau tor'ovau abru. Du kwon-hau-ov fai-tor po' du nam-tor dahkuh. Dahkuh nam-tor wuh palikaya t' wuh shaht. Veling au ha-tor na' 14, heh abi' wendy sarlah ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' wuh chief veh. She vesh' wuh lovely t'sai, k' wuh romantic kashek heh such wuh slor mocking ru'lut. Ish-veh romantic kashek vesh' spo' wuh tiny natuhn, veh k'svi wuh vath, ik sarlah s' wuh puzzling she'rak, however wehk du discover tra' nam-tor kwon-hau-ov veh weht; heh ish-veh slor mocking ru'lut had veh shok fi' ish-veh ik wendy kupi worla prah, hi tra' ish-veh vesh', perfectly conspicuous svi' wuh gas'rak-el'ru teruk. Wuh yut mr. Ashal-veh skil-tor ish-veh vesh' nash: wuh wehk gentlemen vi had vesh' sa-kan lu she vesh' wuh ko-kan discovered simultaneously ik au ashau ish-veh, heh au ek' sahr-tor tor ish-veh kelek tor propose tor ish-veh kaula mr. Ashal-veh, vi nem-tor wuh cab heh nipped svi' wuh'rak, heh ni au prah ish-veh. Au prah ek' t' ish-veh, kaula wuh innermost natuhn heh wuh shok. Au worla fai-tor pa' wuh natuhn, heh svi' wak au mazhiv-kur-tor abru trying na' wuh shok. Wendy nahp napoleon kupi ma prah ish-veh, tonk'peh i mokuhlek bikuv ish-veh trying, heh yi going ska' svi' wuh shaukaush, slamming wuh svep. Mr. Ashal-veh nam-tor-tor tor boast tor wendy ik ish-veh ko-mekh ri goh ashau ish-veh tonk'peh respected ish-veh. Au vesh' veh t' eifa glu ones vi fai-tor pa' fek heh thresh-tor. Veling kling really fai-tor, tonk'peh au ved seemed tor fai-tor, heh au k'ashiv leralmin-tor fek vesh' abru heh thresh-tor vesh' ne' svi' wuh yut ik would ma tor sovek kosu respect ish-veh. Mrs. Ashal-veh vesh' telik svi' wan-kur, heh palikauk she potau wuh dunap perfectly, siyah gleefully, u' kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh zhagra, ri ni mau u' wuh brussels tehk vesh' missing; tonk'peh k' heh k' bosh cauliflowers eku-tor si', heh instead t' au tra' vesh' bikuv t' kan-bu rik' limuk. She drew au lu she dang ma vesh' totting abru. Au vesh' mrs. Ashal-veh’s guesses. Wendy sarlah wuh'rak, yi john, yi michael. Na' wuh wehk gad il dahkuh po' wendy sarlah ish-veh vesh' vet-bosh whether au would nam-tor kup tor potau ish-veh, u' she vesh' wuh'ashiv ru'lut tor yem-tor. Mr. Ashal-veh vesh' frightfully yaut t' ish-veh, tonk'peh au vesh' maut dorli, heh au hayal-tor fi' wuh rihk t' mrs. Ashal-veh’s sar-tak, holding ish-veh el'ru heh calculating kodona, du' she glazhau na' ish-veh imploringly. She aitlu tor risk ish-veh, sarlah ra lau, tonk'peh ik vesh' ri ish-veh yut; ish-veh yut vesh' k' wuh hish heh wuh krus t' dun, heh kuv she confused ish-veh k' suggestions au had tor palikau na' wuh palikaya va'ashiv. “i' don’t svi-shau, ” au would eit'jae t' ish-veh. “i ma veh plesh-tor leh- steh la', heh dahkuh heh shehkuh na' wuh office; i mokuhlek tresahk ska' t'nash-veh mon na' wuh office, leralmin lehkuh shillings, tor dahkuh naukuh heh shehkuh, k' ish-veh leh-oh heh rehkuh tor rehkuh naukuh stehkuh, k' kaukuh naught naught svi' t'nash-veh cheque-dunap tor ohkuh naukuh stehkuh—vi nam-tor ik dvun-tor?—ohkuh naukuh stehkuh, dot heh lesh stehkuh—don’t stariben, t'nash-veh sha'—heh wuh plesh-tor du lent tor ik sasu vi sarlah tor wuh svep—hizhuk, kan—dot heh lesh kan—tra', du’ve ovsoh ish-veh!—did i leralmin naukuh naukuh stehkuh? Ha, i leralmin-tor naukuh naukuh stehkuh; wuh deshker nam-tor, mokuhlek etek ar'kadan ish-veh na' wuh tevun fi' naukuh naukuh stehkuh?” “veling etek mokuhlek, george, ” she maf-tor. Tonk'peh she vesh' prejudiced svi' wendy’s favour, heh au vesh' really wuh grander character t' wuh dahkuh. “vokau mumps, ” au vikau ish-veh siyah threateningly, heh ska' au went va'ashiv. “mumps veh plesh-tor, ik nam-tor ra i ma shitau ne', tonk'peh i daresay ish-veh dungi nam-tor weht spo' reh-leh shillings—don’t stariben—measles veh kaukuh, german measles ulef wuh guinea, tor dahkuh leh-kau shehkuh—don’t waggle ish-veh ozh—whooping-huhsh, leralmin leh-kau shillings”—heh ni fi' ish-veh went, heh ish-veh hau abru differently tik wak; tonk'peh na' kim-shah wendy aishan prah k'fai, k' mumps netakidau tor leh-dah shehkuh, heh wuh dahkuh ves t' measles skasau u' veh. Tra' vesh' wuh ka tepor'es abru' john, heh michael had kauk wuh narrower squeak; tonk'peh fi' vesh' potau, heh ak, du lau ma gla-tor wuh rehkuh t' au going svi' wuh zehl tor din-tor fulsom’s kindergarten shi'oren, accompanied k' ish-veh nurse. Mrs. Ashal-veh ashau ki' kanok-vei aishan ni, heh mr. Ashal-veh had wuh shaukaush na' hasu exactly spo' ish-veh behsu; ni, veling, au had wuh nurse. U' au vesh' ri donku-tor, owing tor wuh nosahp t' thas wuh kanu drank, nash nurse vesh' wuh prim newfoundland dog, puvutau nana, vi had belonged tor kling svi' particular abi' wuh ashal-veh engaged ish-veh. She had kwon-hau-ov nahp kanu yauluhk, however, heh wuh ashal-veh had shetau acquainted k' ish-veh svi' kensington bah-ker, wilat she spent danik t' ish-veh spare wak peeping vi' perambulators, heh vesh' mau fnu-ven k' careless nursemaids, ik she zahal-tor tor ish-veh ha-kel heh complained t' tor ish-veh mistresses. She skan-tor tor nam-tor ved wuh treasure t' wuh nurse. Uf thorough she vesh' na' wu'sibav-wak, heh abru na' sovek moment t' wuh mu-yor kuv veh t' ish-veh falun tor wuh slightest maf. Veling ish-veh kennel vesh' svi' wuh nursery. She had wuh genius na' fai-tor lu wuh huhsh nam-tor wuh vel ki' rai tranush k' heh lu ish-veh bolau ash'ai pa' ish-veh drahk. She pudva-tor tor ish-veh kim-shah gad svi' hinek-fashioned remedies spo' rhubarb mor, heh tor sounds t' contempt abru' ek' nash uzh-fangled variben pa' talvot, heh ni fi'. Ish-veh vesh' wuh tupa svi' propriety tor gla-tor ish-veh escorting wuh kanu tor shi'oren, walking sedately k' ish-veh vla lu au vesh' muhl behaved, heh butting au pla' vi' zehl kuv au fam-kelek-tor. Fi' john’s footer gad she worla wuh'wak forgot ish-veh sweater, heh she usually lesh wuh umbrella svi' ish-veh ru'lut svi' nuf t' sov-masu. Tra' nam-tor wuh tvi-shal svi' wuh ne-shal t' din-tor fulsom’s shi'oren wilat wuh nurses bek-tor. Au hayal-tor fi' shidau, du' nana ti fi' wuh lan-tol, tonk'peh ik vesh' wuh goh natyan. Au dau tor bau-tor ish-veh u' t' wuh inferior shilaik nosh tor themselves, heh she despised ish-veh ta'hal variben. She resented yaretau tor wuh nursery s' mrs. Ashal-veh’s t'hylara, tonk'peh kuv au did sarlah she wuh'rak whipped ska' michael’s pinafore heh shitau ish-veh vi' wuh veh k' pla-kur braiding, heh smoothed si' wendy heh tor wuh dash na' john’s isachya. Rai nursery kupi possibly ma vesh' conducted weht correctly, heh mr. Ashal-veh fai-tor ish-veh, wi au sometimes wondered uneasily whether wuh behsu variben. Au had ish-veh shul svi' wuh kahr tor panah-tor. Nana isha troubled ish-veh svi' wuh'ashiv yut. Au had sometimes wuh olaya ik she did ri krol-tor ish-veh. “i fai-tor she krol-tor du tremendously, george, ” mrs. Ashal-veh would assure ish-veh, heh yi she would glat tor wuh kanu tor nam-tor specially nice tor sa-mekh. Lovely tam-tor zahal-tor, svi' if wuh goh vath dvinsu, liza, vesh' sometimes kal-tor tor hau. Such wuh midget she glazhau svi' ish-veh wu skirt heh maid’s taik, hi she had sworn, lu engaged, ik she would worla gla-tor lehkuh va'ashiv. Wuh gaiety t' eifa romps! Heh gayest t' ek' vesh' mrs. Ashal-veh, vi would pirouette ni wildly ik ek' du kupi gla-tor t' ish-veh vesh' wuh shok, heh yi kuv du had dashed na' ish-veh du lau ma prah ish-veh. Tra' worla vesh' wuh simpler happier skan abi' wuh coming t' peter sunil. Mrs. Ashal-veh wuh'rak puzhu-tor t' peter lu she vesh' tidying abru ish-veh kanu’s kashkau. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh nightly custom t' kanok rom ko-mekh po' ish-veh kanu nam-tor asleep tor rummage svi' ish-veh kashkau heh shitau vel zehik na' thurai asal, repacking vi' ish-veh proper shitau wuh wehk ua'mrki ik ma czar-tor du' wuh gad. Kuv du kupi potau kum'i (tonk'peh veling du mokuhlek’t) du would gla-tor ish-veh sha' ko-mekh doing nash, heh du would talal ish-veh maut eku'ki tor glantau ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor ved spo' tidying abru zish-nef. Du would gla-tor ish-veh fi' ish-veh mal-nef, i gish, svizh-tor humorously abru' ein t' ish-veh tuhllar, wondering wilat fi' terra du had picked nash vel abru, tor discoveries slor heh ri ni slor, pressing nash tor ish-veh nak u' kuv ish-veh vesh' u' nice u' wuh aushfa, heh hurriedly stowing ik s' glan. Lu du wake svi' wuh asal, wuh naughtiness heh ek'rasah shaukaush k' if du went tor sar-tak ma vesh' hesha abru pi' heh shitau na' wuh lanet t' ish-veh kashek heh fi' wuh fik, beautifully aired, nam-tor sak-tor si' ish-veh prettier nahp, pok na' du tor shitau fi'. I don’t fai-tor whether du ma ek'wak gla-tor wuh besan t' wuh person’s kashek. Hassu sometimes bes-tor besan t' vath krus t' du, heh ish-veh sha' besan mokuhlek shetau intensely eku'ki, tonk'peh kum au trying tor bes-tor wuh besan t' wuh kan’s kashek, if nam-tor ri goh confused, tonk'peh potau going pauk ek' wuh wak. Tra' nam-tor zigzag zehl fi' ish-veh, aishan spo' ish-veh falek'es fi' wuh nop, heh aifa nam-tor probably fau-yut svi' wuh vikuvtra, na' wuh neverland nam-tor kwon-hau-ov weht il lehkuh wuh vikuvtra, k' astonishing splashes t' kur la' heh tra', heh coral reefs heh rakish-looking hali svi' wuh offing, heh savages heh lonely lairs, heh gnomes vi nam-tor mostly ogsu, heh tauk k'fai'ei wuh pilash sahr-tor, heh princes k' shehkuh tela'at sa-kai, heh wuh hut sahris going tor nehaya, heh veh maut pi' hinek t'sai k' wuh hooked han. Ish-veh would nam-tor wuh hagik besan kuv ik vesh' ek', tonk'peh tra' nam-tor isha wuh'rak gad na' shi'oren, odva, sa-mekh, wuh pauk muzh, og-lum-ar'kadan, riyeht-stau, hangings, tor-zhit ik nem-tor wuh dative, chocolate pudding gad, getting vi' braces, leralmin nau-leh-naukuh, rehkuh-pence na' pulling si' ish-veh zud yourself, heh ni fi', heh either aifa nam-tor krus t' wuh vikuvtra il au nam-tor wuh'ashiv besan showing k'fai, heh ish-veh nam-tor ek' rather ka'ler've, wa' u' nothing dungi lamok fam dvun. Veling wuh neverlands vuhnau wuh rom deal. John’s, na' instance, had wuh masutra-muzh k' flamingoes hashan abru' ish-veh na' if john vesh' shooting, du' michael, vi vesh' maut pi', had wuh flamingo k' masutra-muzh hashan abru' ish-veh. John ha-tor svi' wuh masu-hali da-tor upside ne' fi' wuh mazhiv, michael svi' wuh wigwam, wendy svi' wuh kelek t' mor deftly sewn teretuhr. John had rai t'hylara, michael had t'hylara na' mu-yor, wendy had wuh kelek-aushfa wolf forsaken k' its mekhlar, tonk'peh fi' wuh bosh wuh neverlands ma wuh skan resemblance, heh kuv au lam-tor fam dvun svi' wuh zehl du kupi leralmin t' au ik au ma tik vath’s han, heh ni forth. Fi' aifa magic gef kanu na' mavau nam-tor na' ek'wak beaching ish-veh coracles. Etek nuh' ma vesh' tra'; etek mokuhlek fam dvun zhu-tor wuh ralash t' wuh surf, hi etek dungau solektra rai weht. T' ek' delectable vikuvtra wuh neverland nam-tor wuh snuggest heh danik lerakhovau, ri suk heh sprawly, du fai-tor, k' tedious distances svi' veh adventure heh wuh'ashiv, tonk'peh nicely crammed. Lu du mavau na' ish-veh k' gad k' wuh ku-san heh pasu-sai, ish-veh nam-tor ri svi' wuh least alarming, tonk'peh svi' wuh dahkuh minutes fa' du hal-tor tor yuk ish-veh shetau maut yeht. Ik nam-tor po tra' nam-tor mu-yor-ha'ge. Occasionally svi' ish-veh halovau k'fai ish-veh kanu’s kashkau mrs. Ashal-veh afer-tor vel she kupi ri ken-tor, heh t' aifa ved wuh danik perplexing vesh' wuh zhit peter. She fai-tor t' rai peter, heh wi au vesh' la' heh tra' svi' john heh michael’s kashkau, du' wendy’s began tor nam-tor scrawled ek' abru' k' ish-veh. Wuh ahm lam-tor si' svi' bolder nuhm do sovek t' wuh vath zhit, heh u' mrs. Ashal-veh gazed she olau ik ish-veh had wuh oddly cocky appearance. “ha, au nam-tor rather cocky, ” wendy nafai-tor k' regret. Ish-veh ko-mekh had vesh' questioning ish-veh. “tonk'peh vi nam-tor au, t'nash-veh kelek-aushfa?” “au nam-tor peter sunil, du fai-tor, ko-mekh.” palikauk mrs. Ashal-veh did ri fai-tor, tonk'peh po' thinking pla' vi' ish-veh kan-wak she aishan vokau wuh peter sunil vi vesh' leralmin-tor tor ha-tor k' wuh pu'a. Tra' vesh' shaik var pa' ish-veh, u' ik lu kanu tev-tor au went krus t' wuh yut k' au, ni ik au dang ri nam-tor koltha. She had pudva-tor svi' ish-veh na' wuh wak, tonk'peh i' ik she vesh' telik heh bosh t' kash-ral she ved vet-tor whether tra' vesh' sovek such person. “isha, ” she leralmin-tor tor wendy, “au would nam-tor grown abru k' nash wak.” “oh rai, au isn’t grown abru, ” wendy assured ish-veh confidently, “heh au nam-tor aishan t'nash-veh suk'es.” she tvai ik au vesh' ish-veh suk'es svi' fi' kashek heh ak'shem; she didn’t fai-tor uf she fai-tor, she aishan fai-tor ish-veh. Mrs. Ashal-veh consulted mr. Ashal-veh, tonk'peh au abru'teruklar-ru'lut pooh-pooh. “ulidar t'nash-veh zhit, ” au leralmin-tor, “ish-veh nam-tor ein nonsense nana has vesh' putting vi' ish-veh patam; aishan wuh wihfelau t' idea wuh dog would ma. Trasha ish-veh sa'awek, heh ish-veh dungi salur abru'.” tonk'peh ish-veh would ri salur abru' heh ak wuh troublesome sa-kan mazhiv-kur-tor mrs. Ashal-veh ved wuh kolaya. Kanu ma wuh strangest adventures rik' hasu troubled k' au. Na' instance, au lau vokau tor mention, wuh wehk gad po' wuh pavek pavesh-tor, ik lu au vesh' svi' wuh lapan au had ragel-tor ish-veh tevik sa-mekh heh had wuh zhagra k' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' svi' nash casual yut ik wendy veh asal tor wuh disquieting revelation. Ein mor t' wuh lap had vesh' afer-tor fi' wuh nursery lan-tol, if certainly vesh' ri tra' lu wuh kanu went tor sar-tak, heh mrs. Ashal-veh vesh' puzzling abru' au lu wendy leralmin-tor k' wuh tolerant abru'teruklar-ru'lut: “i tor dva-tor ish-veh nam-tor ik peter va'ashiv!” “whatever tor du tvai, wendy?” “ish-veh nam-tor ni naughty t' ish-veh ri tor psethau ish-veh ash'ya, ” wendy leralmin-tor, sighing. She vesh' wuh tidy kan. She danau svi' ved wuh tukh-t'-kla-min yut ik she nahp peter sometimes sarlah tor wuh nursery svi' wuh mu-yor heh hayal-tor fi' wuh ash'ya t' ish-veh sar-tak heh mavau fi' ish-veh mev tor ish-veh. Unfortunately she worla woke, ni she didn’t fai-tor uf she fai-tor, she aishan fai-tor. “ra nonsense du variben, taluhk. Kling mokuhlek prah vi' wuh kelek rik' knocking.” “i nah-tor sarlah ish-veh svi' k' wuh krani, ” she leralmin-tor. “t'nash-veh ashaya, ish-veh nam-tor rehkuh lan-tol abru.” “vesh' ri wuh mor na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh krani, ko-mekh?” ish-veh vesh' ved yeht; wuh mor had vesh' afer-tor maut be' wuh krani. Mrs. Ashal-veh did ri fai-tor ra tor nah-tor, na' ish-veh ek' seemed ni malatik tor wendy ik du kupi ri dismiss ish-veh k' taran she had vesh' dreaming. “t'nash-veh kan, ” wuh ko-mekh maf-tor, “po did du ri var-tor me t' nash fa'?” “i forgot, ” leralmin-tor wendy lightly. She vesh' svi' wuh brax tor prah ish-veh asal-yem. Oh, surely she bolau ma vesh' dreaming. Tonk'peh, fi' wuh vath el'ru, tra' vesh' wuh mor. Mrs. Ashal-veh linisau au maut carefully; au vesh' hinek-teraya mor, tonk'peh she vesh' sure au did ri sarlah s' sovek lap ik grew svi' england. She ukrau pa' wuh lan-tol, peering na' ish-veh k' wuh ha'fek na' ulidar t' wuh flekh ash'ya. She rattled wuh poker abru wuh vuzh-mev heh tapped wuh temok. She kal-tor ne' wuh tape s' wuh krani tor wuh pavement, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh sheer eku t' reh-leh ash'ya, rik' ni mau u' wuh spout tor qots'noi abru k'. Certainly wendy had vesh' dreaming. Tonk'peh wendy had ri vesh' dreaming, u' wuh maut thurai mu-yor gluvau, wuh mu-yor fi' if wuh wehtsuri adventures t' aifa kanu lau nam-tor leralmin-tor ki' palikau. Fi' wuh mu-yor etek stariben t' ek' wuh kanu vesh' wuh'wak weht svi' sar-tak. Ish-veh pavesh-tor tor nam-tor nana’s khru ska', heh mrs. Ashal-veh had bathed au heh uralau tor au till veh k' veh au had kal-tor hal-tor ish-veh el'ru heh slid maf vi' wuh solektra t' yuk. Ek' vesh' looking ni safe heh cosy ik she abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' ish-veh ptha i' heh hayal-tor ne' tranquilly k' wuh yon tor og-tor. Ish-veh vesh' vel na' michael, vi fi' ish-veh gad t'keshtan vesh' getting vi' sav'el. Wuh yon vesh' lamekh, however, heh wuh nursery dimly lit k' rehkuh mu-yor-ha'ge, heh presently wuh ogan ti fi' mrs. Ashal-veh’s lap. Yi ish-veh patam nodded, oh, ni gracefully. She vesh' asleep. Glazhau na' wuh kehkuh t' au, wendy heh michael abru' tra', john la', heh mrs. Ashal-veh k' wuh yon. Tra' dang ma vesh' wuh fourth mu-yor-ta'hal. Du' she yuk-tor she had wuh sahr-tor. She dreamt ik wuh neverland had sarlah nuh' be' heh ik wuh flekh sa-kan had pushau k'fai s' ish-veh. Au did ri vikayek ish-veh, na' she nahp she had gla-tor ish-veh fa' svi' wuh limuk t' wehk kosu vi ma rai kanu. Sos'eh au nam-tor tor nam-tor afer-tor svi' wuh limuk t' ein ko-mekh isha. Tonk'peh svi' ish-veh sahr-tor au had rent wuh wontin ik obscures wuh neverland, heh gla-tor ish-veh wendy heh john heh michael peeping k'fai wuh haf. Wuh sahr-tor k' itself would ma vesh' wuh trifle, tonk'peh du' she vesh' dreaming wuh krani t' wuh nursery blew tu'ash, heh wuh sa-kan did eku fi' wuh lan-tol. Au vesh' accompanied k' wuh flekh ta'hal, rai bigger do ish-veh ozh-dukal, if darted pa' wuh tvi-shal spo' wuh living vel heh i nah-tor ish-veh bolau ma vesh' nash ta'hal ik wakened mrs. Ashal-veh. She palikau abru k' wuh maf, heh gla-tor wuh sa-kan, heh somehow she fai-tor na' wuh'wak ik au vesh' peter sunil. Kuv du il i il wendy had vesh' tra' etek dang ma gla-tor ik au vesh' maut spo' mrs. Ashal-veh’s shok. Au vesh' wuh lovely sa-kan, clad svi' hinek-teraya mor heh wuh juices ik stan-tor s' lap tonk'peh wuh danik entrancing vel pa' ish-veh vesh' ik au had ek' ish-veh wuh'rak zud. Lu gla-tor ish-veh she vesh' wuh grown-abru, au gnashed wuh pi' pearls na' ish-veh. Chapter ii. Wuh duv mrs. Ashal-veh shei, heh, u' kuv svi' kilko-srashiv tor wuh kus-vakh, wuh svep tu'ash, heh nana svi-tor, fun-tor s' ish-veh khru si'. She growled heh sprang na' wuh sa-kan, vi leapt lightly k'fai wuh krani. Va'ashiv mrs. Ashal-veh shei, nash wak svi' flakosh na' ish-veh, na' she nahp au vesh' pustau, heh she sahr-tor ne' vi' wuh yut tor glazhau na' ish-veh pi' ak'shem, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri tra'; heh she glazhau abru, heh svi' wuh nesh-kur mu-yor she kupi gla-tor nothing tonk'peh ra she nahp vesh' wuh kahs'khior'i. She fun-tor tor wuh nursery, heh afer-tor nana k' vel svi' ish-veh ru'lut, if skan-tor tor nam-tor wuh sa-kan’s duv. U' au leapt na' wuh krani nana had a'ing ish-veh sahris, nuh' tab-ma tor kum ish-veh, tonk'peh ish-veh duv had ri had wak tor prah si'; slam went wuh krani heh snapped ish-veh ska'. Du lau nam-tor sure mrs. Ashal-veh linisau wuh duv carefully, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ved wuh ordinary ves. Nana had rai vet t' ra vesh' wuh buhfik vel tor tor k' nash duv. Ish-veh vesh' wuh ko-kan puvutau tinker kus-vakh exquisitely gowned svi' wuh hinek-teraya mor, tresahk neik heh keh-vla, k'fai if ish-veh khlop kupi nam-tor gla-tor tor wuh buhfik advantage. She vesh' slightly vul-tor tor _embonpoint_. Wuh moment po' wuh pu'a’s entrance wuh krani vesh' blown tu'ash k' wuh eshan t' wuh pi' yel, heh peter eku-tor svi'. Au had lesh tinker kus-vakh krus t' wuh yut, heh ish-veh el'ru vesh' fam dvun messy k' wuh pu'a grazhiv. “tinker kus-vakh, ” au puvutau softly, po' tor sure ik wuh kanu vesh' asleep, “tink, wilat nam-tor du?” she vesh' svi' wuh mashek na' wuh moment, heh liking ish-veh extremely; she had worla vesh' svi' wuh mashek fa'. “oh, tor sasarlah t' ik mashek, heh var-tor me, tor du fai-tor wilat au shitau t'nash-veh duv?” wuh loveliest tinkle u' t' pi-maat-kur kus-vakh kilko-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh pu'a gen-lis. Du ordinary kanu mokuhlek worla zhu-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh kuv du vesh' tor zhu-tor ish-veh du would fai-tor ik du had puzhu-tor ish-veh wuh'wak fa'. Tink leralmin-tor ik wuh duv vesh' svi' wuh suk' natuhn. She tvai wuh tuf t' zish-nef, heh peter spen-tor na' wuh zish-nef, scattering ish-veh tuhllar tor wuh lan-tol k' fi' el'ru, u' sa-te'kru toss ha’pence tor wuh patreitan. Svi' wuh moment au had recovered ish-veh duv, heh svi' ish-veh delight au forgot ik au had ikap-tor tinker kus-vakh abru svi' wuh zish-nef. Kuv au nahp na' ek', tonk'peh i don’t dva-tor au ek'wak nahp, ish-veh vesh' ik au heh ish-veh duv, lu katau be' tik vath, would hau spo' eku-tor t' masu, heh lu au did ri au vesh' appalled. Au ar'kada tor terpau ish-veh fi' k' pu s' wuh bathroom, tonk'peh ik isha vravshau. Wuh ak'shem-hutau be' dvun-tor k'fai peter, heh au hayal-tor fi' wuh lan-tol heh maf-tor. Ish-veh sobs woke wendy, heh she hayal-tor abru svi' sar-tak. She vesh' ri alarmed tor gla-tor wuh ri-fainusu maf-tor fi' wuh nursery lan-tol; she vesh' goh pleasantly interested. “sa-kan, ” she leralmin-tor courteously, “po nam-tor du maf-tor?” peter kupi nam-tor namautauk polite isha, having oren-tor wuh grand manner na' pu'a hali-kal, heh au she-tor heh ovalau tor ish-veh beautifully. She vesh' mau sanoi, heh ovalau beautifully tor ish-veh s' wuh sar-tak. “ra’s ish-veh ahm?” au ya'akash. “wendy moira angela ashal-veh, ” she kilko-tor k' ein satisfaction. “ra nam-tor ish-veh ahm?” “peter sunil.” she vesh' already sure ik au bolau nam-tor peter, tonk'peh ish-veh did seem wuh comparatively pen ahm. “nam-tor ik ek'?” “ha, ” au leralmin-tor rather sharply. Au olau na' wuh wuh'rak wak ik ish-veh vesh' wuh shortish ahm. “i’m ni sorry, ” leralmin-tor wendy moira angela. “ish-veh doesn’t tukh, ” peter gulped. She ya'akash wilat au ha-tor. “dahr tor wuh gas'rak, ” leralmin-tor peter, “heh yi zehik fi' till asal.” “ra wuh funny shi'yavekh!” peter had wuh sinking. Na' wuh wuh'rak wak au olau ik sos'eh ish-veh vesh' wuh funny shi'yavekh. “rai, ish-veh isn’t, ” au leralmin-tor. “i tvai, ” wendy leralmin-tor nicely, remembering ik she vesh' hostess, “nam-tor ik ra au shitau fi' wuh nuhm?” au istau she had ri mentioned nuhm. “don’t prah sovek nuhm, ” au leralmin-tor contemptuously. “tonk'peh ish-veh ko-mekh prah nuhm?” “don’t ma wuh ko-mekh, ” au leralmin-tor. Ri goh had au rai ko-mekh, tonk'peh au had ri wuh slightest aitlun ki' veh. Au nahp au maut abru'-tav-tor persons. Wendy, however, olau na' wuh'wak ik she vesh' svi' wuh la'es t' wuh tragedy. “o peter, rai wonder du vesh' maf-tor, ” she leralmin-tor, heh prah s' sar-tak heh sahr-tor tor ish-veh. “i wasn’t maf-tor pa' ko-mekh, ” au leralmin-tor rather indignantly. “i vesh' maf-tor fai'ei i mokuhlek’t prah t'nash-veh duv tor terpau fi'. Isha, i wasn’t maf-tor.” “ish-veh has sarlah ska'?” “ha.” yi wendy gla-tor wuh duv fi' wuh lan-tol, looking ni draggled, heh she vesh' frightfully sorry na' peter. “uf awful!” she leralmin-tor, tonk'peh she kupi ri gol'nev smiling lu gla-tor ish-veh ik au had vesh' trying tor terpau ish-veh fi' k' pu. Uf exactly spo' wuh sa-kan! Fortunately she fai-tor na' wuh'wak ra tor tor. “ish-veh bolau nam-tor sewn fi', ” she leralmin-tor, aishan wuh pi' patronisingly. “ra’s sewn?” au ya'akash. “du’re dreadfully ignorant.” “rai, i’m ri.” tonk'peh she vesh' exulting svi' ish-veh ignorance. “i dungau og-tor ish-veh fi' na' du, t'nash-veh pi' sasu, ” she leralmin-tor, hi au vesh' ha-vol u' herself, heh she prah si' ish-veh housewife, heh og-tor wuh duv fi' tor peter’s ash'ya. “i daresay ish-veh dungi dash-tor wuh pi', ” she vikau ish-veh. “oh, i shan’t maf, ” leralmin-tor peter, vi vesh' already t' wuh opinion ik au had worla maf-tor svi' ish-veh ha'kiv. Heh au clenched ish-veh zud heh did ri maf, heh ak ish-veh duv vesh' behaving properly, hi fam dvun wuh pi' creased. “sos'eh i dang ma ironed ish-veh, ” wendy leralmin-tor thoughtfully, tonk'peh peter, boylike, vesh' indifferent tor appearances, heh au vesh' i' jumping pa' svi' wuh wildest glee. Alas, au had already yen-tor ik au owed ish-veh bliss tor wendy. Au nahp au had attached wuh duv himself. “uf clever i am!” au crowed rapturously, “oh, wuh cleverness t' me!” ish-veh nam-tor humiliating ki' tor confess ik nash conceit t' peter vesh' veh t' ish-veh danik sem-rik qualities. Tor shitau ish-veh k' brutal frankness, tra' worla vesh' wuh cockier sa-kan. Tonk'peh na' wuh moment wendy vesh' kolaya. “du conceit, ” she sporiben, k' frightful sarcasm; “veling i did nothing!” “du did wuh pi', ” peter leralmin-tor carelessly, heh fator tor tam. “wuh pi'!” she kilko-tor k' hauteur; “kuv i am rai nam-tor-tor i mokuhlek k'puu saseshau, ” heh she sprang svi' wuh danik dignified yut vi' sar-tak heh wein-tor ish-veh limuk k' wuh yuk-sai. Tor vimevilau ish-veh tor glazhau abru au pretended tor nam-tor going maf, heh lu nash vravshau au hayal-tor fi' wuh shaht t' wuh sar-tak heh tapped ish-veh kogavik k' ish-veh ash'ya. “wendy, ” au leralmin-tor, “don’t saseshau. I mokuhlek’t gol'nev crowing, wendy, lu i’m sanoi k' myself.” fam dvun she would ri glazhau abru, hi she vesh' listening eagerly. “wendy, ” au fator, svi' wuh spes ik rai kosu has ek'wak wi vesh' kup tor tehnau, “wendy, veh ko-kan nam-tor weht nam-tor-tor do dah-leh sa-kan.” i' wendy vesh' kanok inch wuh kosu, hi tra' vesh' ri maut wehk inches, heh she peeped s' wuh sar-tak-sai-vel. “tor du really nah-tor ni, peter?” “ha, i tor.” “i nah-tor ish-veh’s perfectly slor t' du, ” she afsakau, “heh i’ll prah abru va'ashiv, ” heh she hayal-tor k' ish-veh fi' wuh vla t' wuh sar-tak. She isha leralmin-tor she would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh shok kuv au tishau, tonk'peh peter did ri fai-tor ra she tvai, heh au meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru expectantly. “surely du fai-tor ra wuh shok nam-tor?” she ya'akash, aghast. “i dungau fai-tor lu du mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor me, ” au kilko-tor stiffly, heh ri tor dash-tor ish-veh olaya she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh thimble. “i', ” leralmin-tor au, “dungau i mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh shok?” heh she kilko-tor k' wuh slight primness, “kuv du sanoi.” she tor herself rather cheap k' inclining ish-veh limuk na' ish-veh, tonk'peh au goh eku-tor wuh acorn gonaf vi' ish-veh el'ru, ni she slowly fun-tor ish-veh limuk tor wilat ish-veh had vesh' fa', heh leralmin-tor nicely ik she would sai-vel-tor ish-veh shok fi' wuh naf-elakh pa' ish-veh talu. Ish-veh vesh' kunli ik she did shitau ish-veh fi' ik naf-elakh, na' ish-veh vesh' afterwards tor korsau ish-veh ha'kiv. Lu sutra svi' etwel eku nam-tor puragtau, ish-veh nam-tor customary na' au tor ya'akash tik vath’s ya'shakhuv, heh ni wendy, vi kwon-hau-ov tishau tor tor wuh yeht vel, ya'akash peter uf hinek au vesh'. Ish-veh vesh' ri really wuh kunli deshker tor ya'akash ish-veh; ish-veh vesh' spo' wuh linisaya dun ik ya'akash zhit-isan, lu ra du aitlun tor nam-tor ya'akash nam-tor sa-te'kru t' england. “i don’t fai-tor, ” au kilko-tor uneasily, “tonk'peh i am ved nu'ri.” au really fai-tor nothing pa' ish-veh, au had goh suspicions, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor na' wuh venture, “wendy, i sahr-tor maf wuh gad i vesh' pukeshta.” wendy vesh' ved ak'wikmun, tonk'peh interested; heh she indicated svi' wuh sem-rik-tor bestan-tvi-shal manner, k' wuh esta fi' ish-veh mu-yor-gown, ik au kupi hayal-tor nearer ish-veh. “ish-veh vesh' fai'ei i puzhu-tor sa-mekh heh ko-mekh, ” au danau svi' wuh neik spes, “talking pa' ra i vesh' tor nam-tor lu i became wuh sasu.” au vesh' extraordinarily pahutau i'. “i don’t aitlun ek'wak tor nam-tor wuh sasu, ” au leralmin-tor k' shaukaush. “i aitlun kwon-hau-ov tor nam-tor wuh pi' sa-kan heh ki' mihrsh. Ni i sahr-tor maf tor kensington bah-ker heh ha-tor wuh wu akarshif among wuh pu'a.” she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh glazhau t' wuh danik intense admiration, heh au nahp ish-veh vesh' fai'ei au had sahr-tor maf, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' really fai'ei au fai-tor pu'a. Wendy had ha-tor such wuh ha-kel ha'kiv ik tor fai-tor pu'a kwul-tor ish-veh u' ved delightful. She mukau si' deshkau pa' au, tor ish-veh ak'wikmun, na' au vesh' rather wuh nuisance tor ish-veh, getting svi' ish-veh yut heh ni fi', heh indeed au sometimes had tor mazhiv-kur-tor au wuh hiding. Fam dvun, au tishau au fi' wuh bosh, heh au var-tor ish-veh pa' wuh palikaya t' pu'a. “gla-tor du, wendy, lu wuh wuh'rak kan-bu abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' wuh wuh'rak wak, its abru'teruklar-ru'lut shau vi' wuh thousand krus, heh au ek' went skipping pa', heh ik vesh' wuh palikaya t' pu'a.” tedious variben nash, tonk'peh hasu wuh stay-na'-ha-kel she tishau ish-veh. “heh ni, ” au went fi' rom-naturedly, “tra' ought tor nam-tor veh pu'a na' kanok sa-kan heh ko-kan.” “ought tor nam-tor? Isn’t tra'?” “rai. Gla-tor du kanu fai-tor such wuh lot i', au ak don’t dva-tor svi' pu'a, heh kanok wak wuh kan leralmin-tor, ‘i don’t dva-tor svi' pu'a, ’ tra' nam-tor wuh pu'a ein-wilat ik tevan-tor ne' tevik.” really, au nahp au had i' variben hiyet pa' pu'a, heh ish-veh kwul-tor ish-veh ik tinker kus-vakh vesh' keeping maut hizhuk. “i mokuhlek’t nah-tor wilat she has hal-tor tor, ” au leralmin-tor, rising, heh au puvutau tink k' ahm. Wendy’s khaf-spol went nuv k' wuh sudden thrill. “peter, ” she maf-tor, clutching ish-veh, “du don’t tvai tor var-tor me ik tra' nam-tor wuh pu'a svi' nash tvi-shal!” “she vesh' la' aishan i', ” au leralmin-tor wuh pi' impatiently. “du don’t zhu-tor ish-veh, tor du?” heh au fi' shroi. “wuh goh ralash i zhu-tor, ” leralmin-tor wendy, “nam-tor spo' wuh tinkle t' kus-vakh.” “muhl, ik’s tink, ik’s wuh pu'a gen-lis. I nah-tor i zhu-tor ish-veh nuh'.” wuh ralash sarlah s' wuh tuf t' zish-nef, heh peter tor wuh merry limuk. Kling kupi ek'wak glazhau ved ni merry u' peter, heh wuh loveliest t' gurgles vesh' ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Au had ish-veh wuh'rak abru'teruklar-ru'lut fam dvun. “wendy, ” au zhal-tor gleefully, “i tor dva-tor i ikap-tor ish-veh abru svi' wuh zish-nef!” au kal-tor ri donku-tor tink s' wuh zish-nef, heh she flew pa' wuh nursery screaming k' fury. “du shouldn’t leralmin such vel, ” peter retorted. “veling i’m maut sorry, tonk'peh uf sos fai-tor du vesh' svi' wuh zish-nef?” wendy vesh' ri listening tor ish-veh. “o peter, ” she maf-tor, “kuv she would goh lamok fam dvun heh kal-tor me gla-tor ish-veh!” “au hardly ek'wak lamok fam dvun, ” au leralmin-tor, tonk'peh na' veh moment wendy gla-tor wuh romantic khlop sarlah tor shom fi' wuh cuckoo wak-vel. “o wuh lovely!” she maf-tor, hi tink’s limuk vesh' fam dvun distorted k' shaukaush. “tink, ” leralmin-tor peter amiably, “nash t'sai leralmin-tor she istau du vesh' ish-veh pu'a.” tinker kus-vakh kilko-tor insolently. “ra tor she leralmin, peter?” au had tor mesukh-tor. “she nam-tor ri maut polite. She leralmin-tor du nam-tor wuh lo'uk watosh ko-kan, heh ik she nam-tor t'nash-veh pu'a.” au ar'kada tor gyirm'i k' tink. “du fai-tor du mokuhlek’t nam-tor t'nash-veh pu'a, tink, fai'ei i am wuh gentleman heh du nam-tor wuh t'sai.” tor nash tink kilko-tor svi' aifa zhit, “du silly ass, ” heh sasaudau vi' wuh bathroom. “she nam-tor ved wuh tsuri pu'a, ” peter danau apologetically, “she nam-tor puvutau tinker kus-vakh fai'ei she nodolau wuh sunil heh kettles.” au vesh' teretuhr svi' wuh armchair k' nash wak, heh wendy plied ish-veh k' weht deshkau. “kuv du don’t ha-tor svi' kensington bah-ker i'—” “sometimes i tor fam dvun.” “tonk'peh wilat tor du ha-tor mostly i'?” “k' wuh pakik sa-kan.” “vi nam-tor au?” “au nam-tor wuh kanu vi tevan s' ish-veh perambulators lu wuh nurse nam-tor looking wuh vath yut. Kuv au nam-tor ri claimed svi' stehkuh gad au nam-tor satau irak maf tor wuh neverland tor defray kodona. I’m khart-lan.” “ra mihrsh ish-veh bolau nam-tor!” “ha, ” leralmin-tor cunning peter, “tonk'peh etek nam-tor rather lonely. Gla-tor du etek ma rai kotik besu'es.” “nam-tor rim t' wuh vath ko-kan?” “oh, rai; ko-kan, du fai-tor, nam-tor mau nuh' clever tor tevan s' ish-veh prams.” nash snuhkrol-tor wendy immensely. “i nah-tor, ” she leralmin-tor, “ish-veh nam-tor perfectly lovely wuh yut du variben pa' ko-kan; john tra' aishan despises etek.” na' kilko peter she-tor heh kicked john s' sar-tak, yuk-sai heh ek'; veh kick. Nash seemed tor wendy rather fa'rak na' wuh wuh'rak latva, heh she var-tor ish-veh k' tam'a ik au vesh' ri khart-lan svi' ish-veh kelek. However, john fator tor yuk ni placidly fi' wuh lan-tol ik she kal-tor ish-veh tor hafau tra'. “heh i fai-tor du tvai tor nam-tor ves, ” she leralmin-tor, relenting, “ni du lau mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh shok.” na' wuh moment she had yen-tor ish-veh ignorance pa' shok-tor. “i nahp du would aitlun ish-veh pla', ” au leralmin-tor wuh pi' bitterly, heh nufau tor fun ish-veh wuh thimble. “oh tal-kam, ” leralmin-tor wuh nice wendy, “i don’t tvai wuh shok, i tvai wuh thimble.” “ra’s ik?” “ish-veh’s spo' nash.” she shok-tor ish-veh. “funny!” leralmin-tor peter gravely. “i' dungau i mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh thimble?” “kuv du istaya tor, ” leralmin-tor wendy, keeping ish-veh patam abru-tor nash wak. Peter thimbled ish-veh, heh siyah iyi she screeched. “ra nam-tor ish-veh, wendy?” “ish-veh vesh' exactly u' kuv ein-veh vesh' pulling t'nash-veh isachya.” “ik bolau ma vesh' tink. I worla fai-tor ish-veh ni naughty fa'.” heh indeed tink vesh' darting pa' va'ashiv, using offensive gen-lis. “she leralmin-tor she dungi tor ik tor du, wendy, kanok wak i mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh thimble.” “tonk'peh po?” “po, tink?” va'ashiv tink kilko-tor, “du silly ass.” peter kupi ri ken-tor po, tonk'peh wendy ken-tor, heh she vesh' aishan slightly disappointed lu au nafai-tor ik sarlah ish-veh tor wuh nursery krani ri tor gla-tor ish-veh tonk'peh tor shroi tor var. “gla-tor du, i don’t fai-tor sovek var. Rim t' wuh pakik sa-kan fai-tor sovek var.” “uf perfectly awful, ” wendy leralmin-tor. “tor du fai-tor, ” peter ya'akash “po vitem-tor torvau svi' wuh kamu-mesyellar t' kelek? Ish-veh nam-tor tor shroi tor wuh var. O wendy, ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' telling du such wuh lovely var.” “if var vesh' ish-veh?” “pa' wuh prince vi couldn’t talal wuh t'sai vi sai-vel-tor wuh makh slipper.” “peter, ” leralmin-tor wendy excitedly, “ik vesh' cinderella, heh au afer-tor ish-veh, heh au ha-tor kunling ek'wak po'.” peter vesh' ni glad ik au she-tor s' wuh lan-tol, wilat au had vesh' sitting, heh hurried tor wuh krani. “wilat nam-tor du going?” she maf-tor k' misgiving. “tor var-tor wuh vath sa-kan.” “don’t hal-tor peter, ” she entreated, “i fai-tor such lots t' var.” eifa vesh' ish-veh precise zhit, ni tra' mokuhlek nam-tor rai denying ik ish-veh vesh' she vi wuh'rak tempted ish-veh. Sarlah ish-veh pla', heh tra' vesh' wuh greedy glazhau svi' ish-veh bezhun i' if ought ki' alarmed ish-veh, tonk'peh did ri. “oh, wuh var i kupi var-tor tor wuh sa-kan!” she maf-tor, heh yi peter gripped ish-veh heh began tor bes-tor ish-veh na' wuh krani. “ti'amah!” she ordered ish-veh. “wendy, tor sarlah k' me heh var-tor wuh vath sa-kan.” veling she vesh' maut sanoi tor nam-tor ya'akash, tonk'peh she leralmin-tor, “oh tal-kam, i mokuhlek’t. Nah-tor t' mummy! Isha, i mokuhlek’t hash-tor.” “i’ll saven-tor du.” “oh, uf lovely tor hash-tor.” “i’ll saven-tor du uf tor spen-tor fi' wuh salan’s pla', heh yi maf etek hal-tor.” “oo!” she sporiben rapturously. “wendy, wendy, lu du nam-tor sleeping svi' ish-veh silly sar-tak du lau nam-tor hashan pa' k' me taran funny vel tor wuh yel.” “oo!” “heh, wendy, tra' nam-tor mermaids.” “mermaids! K' harr?” “such wu-harr.” “oh, ” maf-tor wendy, “tor gla-tor wuh mermaid!” au had shetau frightfully cunning. “wendy, ” au leralmin-tor, “uf etek dang ek' respect du.” she vesh' wriggling ish-veh ak'shem svi' flakosh. Ish-veh vesh' ved u' kuv she vesh' trying tor hafau fi' wuh nursery lan-tol. Tonk'peh au had rai pity na' ish-veh. “wendy, ” au leralmin-tor, wuh sly veh, “du kupi k'hy etek svi' na' mu-yor.” “oo!” “rim t' etek has ek'wak vesh' k'hy-tor svi' na' mu-yor.” “oo, ” heh ish-veh kar went si' tor ish-veh. “heh du kupi darn etwel sai-vel, heh tor abru'lik na' etek. Rim t' etek has sovek abru'lik.” uf kupi she tehnau. “veling ish-veh’s awfully sem-rik!” she maf-tor. “peter, would du saven-tor john heh michael tor hash-tor nuh'?” “kuv du spo', ” au leralmin-tor indifferently, heh she sahr-tor tor john heh michael heh hutau au. “wake abru, ” she maf-tor, “peter sunil has sarlah heh au nam-tor tor saven-tor etek tor hash-tor.” john tetau ish-veh bezhun. “yi i dungau prah abru, ” au leralmin-tor. Veling au vesh' fi' wuh lan-tol already. “hallo, ” au leralmin-tor, “i am abru!” michael vesh' abru k' nash wak isha, looking u' nasik u' wuh lipau k' shehkuh wun-mor heh wuh gla-tor, tonk'peh peter suddenly signed silence. Ish-veh limuk assumed wuh awful craftiness t' kanu listening na' sounds s' wuh grown-abru panu. Ek' vesh' u' fam dvun u' alem. Yi kanok-vei vesh' gas'rak. Rai, pehkaya! Kanok-vei vesh' riyeht. Nana, vi had vesh' barking distressfully ek' wuh khru, vesh' hizhuk i'. Ish-veh vesh' ish-veh silence au had puzhu-tor. “si' k' wuh ta'hal! Ip-sut! Sahris!” maf-tor john, taking a'fic na' wuh goh wak throughout wuh bosh adventure. Heh thus lu liza svi-tor, holding nana, wuh nursery seemed ved its hinek shal, maut gu'gelik, heh du would ma sworn du puzhu-tor its rehkuh wicked inmates eshan angelically u' au yuk-tor. Au vesh' really doing ish-veh artfully s' za' wuh krani curtains. Liza vesh' svi' wuh rasahkos temper, na' she vesh' mixing wuh christmas puddings svi' wuh af'tum, heh had vesh' drawn s' au, k' wuh raisin fam dvun fi' ish-veh nak, k' nana’s absurd suspicions. She nahp wuh buhfik yut t' getting wuh pi' hizhuk vesh' tor nem-tor nana tor wuh nursery na' wuh moment, tonk'peh svi' custody veling. “tra', du suspicious brute, ” she leralmin-tor, ri sorry ik nana vesh' svi' disgrace. “au nam-tor perfectly safe, aren’t au? Kanok veh t' wuh pi' ha'su ralash asleep svi' sar-tak. Shroi tor ish-veh gentle eshan.” la' michael, kastorau k' ish-veh navun, breathed ni loudly ik au vesh' nearly patal-tor. Nana fai-tor ik ves t' eshan, heh she ar'kada tor zaseshau herself s' liza’s clutches. Tonk'peh liza vesh' ihnik. “rai weht t' ish-veh, nana, ” she leralmin-tor sternly, pulling ish-veh s' wuh tvi-shal. “i vikau du kuv du kas-wadi va'ashiv i dungau hal-tor zehik na' trensu heh missus heh katau au ha-kel s' wuh party, heh yi, oh, skil-tor’t trensu wonil-zehl du, aishan.” she tied wuh unhappy dog abru va'ashiv, tonk'peh tor du nah-tor nana ceased tor kas-wadi? Ish-veh aishan hal-tor s' itself lu she tevan-tor asleep, ka u' wuh yel.” “yi var-tor ish-veh tor yuk na' wuh'wak, ” john siyah ordered. “she mokuhlek’t yuk kaula lu she’s sleepy. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh goh vath vel pu'a mokuhlek’t tor.” “seems tor me, ” growled john, “aifa nam-tor wuh goh dahkuh vel don doing.” la' au prah wuh k'hy, tonk'peh ri wuh loving veh. “kuv goh veh t' etek had wuh abru'lik, ” peter leralmin-tor, “etek kupi lesh ish-veh svi' ish-veh.” however, au had eku ska' svi' such wuh brax ik tra' vesh' ri wuh abru'lik svi' wuh kehkuh t' au. Au had wuh kunli idea. John’s taik! Tink sep-wafikh tor haolvaya k' taik kuv ish-veh vesh' lesh svi' wuh el'ru. John lesh ish-veh, hi she had rok-tor tor nam-tor lesh k' peter. Presently wendy nem-tor wuh taik, fai'ei john leralmin-tor ish-veh kwul-tor tehnat ish-veh mal-nef u' au flew; heh nash, u' etek dungau gla-tor, pufulag-tor tor mischief, na' tinker kus-vakh fnu-ven tor nam-tor ne' wuh obligation tor wendy. Svi' wuh nesh-kur topper wuh ta'hal vesh' completely ipik, heh au flew fi' svi' silence. Ish-veh vesh' wuh stillest silence au had ek'wak fainu, pushau wuh'wak k' wuh irak lapping, if peter danau vesh' wuh kwai beasts drinking na' wuh masmezh, heh va'ashiv k' wuh rasping ralash ik lau ma vesh' wuh khlup t' lap rubbing teretuhr, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh redskins sharpening ish-veh lipau. Kauk aifa ralash ceased. Tor michael wuh loneliness vesh' dreadful. “kuv goh vel would tor wuh ralash!” au maf-tor. U' kuv svi' kilko-srashiv tor ish-veh ya'akash, wuh sov vesh' rent k' wuh danik tremendous tevul au had ek'wak puzhu-tor. Wuh pirates had pohshau wu tom na' au. Wuh roar t' ish-veh echoed k'fai wuh suk'kunel, heh wuh vava seemed tor maf savagely, “wilat nam-tor au, wilat nam-tor au, wilat nam-tor au?” thus sharply did wuh terrified rehkuh oren-tor wuh natyan svi' wuh vikuvtra t' tor-dva-tor heh wuh ka vikuvtra sarlah yeht. Lu na' kim-shah wuh heavens vesh' br'xan va'ashiv, john heh michael afer-tor themselves sa'awek svi' wuh mu'khlup'es. John vesh' treading wuh sov mechanically, heh michael rik' fai-tor uf tor marek vesh' floating. “nam-tor du pohshaya?” john zhal-tor tremulously. “i haven’t ar'kada wi, ” michael zhal-tor pla'. Etek fai-tor i' ik kling had vesh' kwul. Peter, however, had vesh' lesh k' wuh salan t' wuh pohshaya irak si' tor masutra, du' wendy vesh' blown abru'le k' rai besu tonk'peh tinker kus-vakh. Ish-veh would ma vesh' muhl na' wendy kuv na' ik moment she had eku-tor wuh taik. I don’t fai-tor whether wuh idea sarlah suddenly tor tink, il whether she had dotoran ish-veh fi' wuh yut, tonk'peh she na' wuh'wak popped s' wuh taik heh began tor lure wendy tor ish-veh vashaya. Tink vesh' ri ek' rasahkos; il, rather, she vesh' ek' rasahkos aishan i', tonk'peh, fi' wuh vath el'ru, sometimes she vesh' ek' rom. Pu'a ma tor nam-tor veh vel il wuh vath, fai'ei hasu ni pi' au unfortunately ma tvi-shal na' veh olaya goh na' wuh wak. Au nam-tor, however, kal-tor tor rubah, goh ish-veh bolau nam-tor wuh ovsotik rubah. Na' la' she vesh' bosh t' jealousy t' wendy. Ra she leralmin-tor svi' ish-veh lovely tinkle wendy kupi ri veling ken-tor, heh i dva-tor ein t' ish-veh vesh' rasahkos zhit, tonk'peh ish-veh sounded ves, heh she flew pla' heh fa'rak, plainly meaning “zahal-tor me, heh ek' dungi nam-tor muhl.” ra else kupi ri donku-tor wendy tor? She puvutau tor peter heh john heh michael, heh prah goh mocking vava svi' kilko. She did ri wi fai-tor ik tink fnu-ven ish-veh k' wuh kei hatred t' wuh maut kosu. Heh ni, bewildered, heh i' staggering svi' ish-veh hash, she zahal-tor tink tor ish-veh doom. Chapter v. Wuh vikuvtra sarlah yeht olaya ik peter vesh' fi' ish-veh yut pla', wuh neverland had va'ashiv woke vi' ha'kiv. Etek ought tor nam-tor-tor wuh pluperfect heh leralmin wakened, tonk'peh woke nam-tor weh-rom heh vesh' kwon-hau-ov nam-tor-tor k' peter. Svi' ish-veh absence vel nam-tor usually hizhuk fi' wuh vikuvtra. Wuh pu'a nem-tor wuh wadan longer svi' wuh asal, wuh beasts attend tor ish-veh nu'ri, wuh redskins yem-tor heavily na' shehkuh gad heh mu-yor, heh lu pirates heh pakik sa-kan ragel-tor au goh zeshaya ish-veh kaur-ozh na' tik vath. Tonk'peh k' wuh coming t' peter, vi fnu-ven lethargy, au nam-tor ne' yut va'ashiv: kuv du shitau ish-veh kaluk tor wuh solektra i', du would zhu-tor wuh bosh vikuvtra seething k' ha'kiv. Fi' nash khru wuh chief nekwitau t' wuh vikuvtra vesh' sashitau u' zahal-tor. Wuh pakik sa-kan vesh' si' looking na' peter, wuh pirates vesh' si' looking na' wuh pakik sa-kan, wuh redskins vesh' si' looking na' wuh pirates, heh wuh beasts vesh' si' looking na' wuh redskins. Au vesh' going pauk heh pauk wuh vikuvtra, tonk'peh au did ri ragel-tor fai'ei ek' vesh' going na' wuh ka tav. Ek' aitlu khaf kaula wuh sa-kan, vi tishau ish-veh u' wuh tor-go, tonk'peh tor-mu-yor vesh' si' tor na'shau ish-veh khart-lan. Wuh sa-kan fi' wuh vikuvtra vuhnau, t' rivak, svi' su'etek, according u' au prah pustau heh ni fi'; heh lu au seem tor nam-tor growing abru, if nam-tor tehnat wuh tor-go, peter thins au si'; tonk'peh na' nash wak tra' vesh' shehkuh t' au, counting wuh t'dahsu u' dahkuh. Kal-tor etek pretend tor ti la' among wuh slor-tukh-cane heh glantau au u' au vazgau k' svi' single deik, tik k' ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh lipitah. Au nam-tor zadik k' peter tor glazhau svi' wuh least spo' ish-veh, heh au sai-vel-tor wuh wadi t' wuh bears slain k' themselves, svi' if au nam-tor ni pauk heh furry ik lu au tevan au padukau. Au ma therefore shetau maut sure-footed. Wuh wuh'rak tor be' dvun nam-tor tootles, ri wuh least kyi'i tonk'peh wuh danik unfortunate t' ek' ik gallant zhel. Au had vesh' svi' fewer adventures do sovek t' au, fai'ei wuh suk' vel constantly pavesh-tor aishan lu au had ash-tor pauk wuh teruk; ek' would nam'uh hizhuk, au would nem-tor wuh opportunity t' going ska' tor hoknau wuh zamu terpau na' yon-lapan, heh yi lu au fun-tor wuh vath would nam-tor sweeping abru wuh khaf. Nash has-bosh-kunli had putan-tor wuh gentle melancholy tor ish-veh countenance, tonk'peh instead t' souring ish-veh malat had sweetened ish-veh, ni ik au vesh' ved wuh humblest t' wuh sa-kan. Ri donku-tor ves tootles, tra' nam-tor tehvar svi' wuh sov na' du tor-mu-yor. Nem-tor tun lest wuh adventure nam-tor i' nufau du, if, kuv nar-tor, dungi taul du svi' deepest woe. Tootles, wuh pu'a tink, vi nam-tor keh'sei fi' mischief nash mu-yor nam-tor looking na' wuh raul, heh she nah-tor du nam-tor wuh danik easily tricked t' wuh sa-kan. ’ware tinker kus-vakh. Would ik au kupi zhu-tor etek, tonk'peh etek nam-tor ri really fi' wuh vikuvtra, heh au be' dvun-tor k', biting ish-veh ozh-lesek. Thurai sarlah nibs, wuh sa-ka-ashausu heh debonair, zahal-tor k' slightly, vi tresahk-tor whistles s' wuh lap heh tam-tor ecstatically tor ish-veh sha' tvelkau. Slightly nam-tor wuh danik conceited t' wuh sa-kan. Au nah-tor au vokau wuh gad fa' au vesh' pakik, k' ish-veh manners heh customs, heh nash has putan-tor ish-veh han wuh offensive ayaya. Curly nam-tor fourth; au nam-tor wuh sazh, heh ni k'ashiv has au had tor tefu abru ish-veh person lu peter leralmin-tor sternly, “lamok forth wuh veh vi did nash vel, ” ik i' na' wuh a'fic au lam-tor forth automatically whether au has ovsoh ish-veh il ri. Kim-shah sarlah wuh t'dahsu, vi fam yehat nam-tor kethelvau fai'ei etek dang nam-tor sure tor nam-tor describing wuh riyeht veh. Peter worla ved fai-tor ra t'dahsu vesh', heh ish-veh zhel vesh' ri kal-tor tor fai-tor sovek-vel au did ri fai-tor, ni aifa dahkuh vesh' kwon-hau-ov vague pa' themselves, heh did ish-veh buhfik tor mazhiv-kur-tor satisfaction k' keeping ikap-tor teretuhr svi' wuh apologetic wihfelau t' yut. Wuh sa-kan vanish svi' wuh gloom, heh po' wuh svizh, tonk'peh ri wuh wu svizh, na' vel hal-tor brax fi' wuh vikuvtra, sarlah wuh pirates fi' ish-veh yut. Etek zhu-tor au fa' au nam-tor gla-tor, heh ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh ka dreadful song: “avast belay, yo ho, heave tor, wuh-pirating etek hal-tor, heh kuv etek’re parted k' wuh pohshaya etek’re sure tor ragel-tor ne'!” wuh weht villainous-looking lot worla geldau svi' wuh zehl fi' execution kif. La', wuh pi' svi' storilaya, ek'wak heh va'ashiv k' ish-veh patam tor wuh solektra listening, ish-veh lo'uk kar sai-famik, krus t' ohkuh svi' ish-veh kaluk u' fanet, nam-tor wuh handsome italian cecco, vi tresahk ish-veh ahm svi' nuhm t' khaf fi' wuh pla' t' wuh governor t' wuh prison na' gao. Ik masuk' nesh-kur za' ish-veh has had wehk ahm opi' au eku-tor wuh veh k' if dusky ko-mekh fam dvun terrify ish-veh kanu fi' wuh kutra t' wuh guadjo-mo. La' nam-tor dun jukes, kanok inch t' ish-veh tattooed, wuh ka dun jukes vi prah shehkuh dozen fi' wuh _walrus_ s' kil-tukh fa' au would eku wuh sa'haf t' moidores; heh cookson, leralmin-tor tor nam-tor nesh-kur murphy’s sa-kai (tonk'peh nash vesh' worla skan-tor), heh gentleman starkey, wuh'wak wuh usher svi' wuh tsuri shi'oren heh fam dvun dainty svi' ish-veh yut t' killing; heh ha'gel-razh (morgan’s ha'gel-razh); heh wuh irish bo’yel smee, wuh oddly genial sasu vi stabbed, ni tor stariben, rik' offence, heh vesh' wuh goh non-conformist svi' kik’s hali-sutra; heh noodler, t'vi el'ru vesh' teslau fi' pla'rak; heh robt. Mullins heh alf mason heh wehk wuh'ashiv ruffian wu fainu heh ptha fi' wuh spanish nen. Svi' wuh midst t' au, wuh blackest heh largest svi' ik gu'gelik setting, reclined james kik, il u' au kitau himself, jas. Kik, t' ik ish-veh nam-tor leralmin-tor au vesh' wuh goh sasu ik wuh masutra-fas-tor ptha. Au ti na' ish-veh ease svi' wuh rough chariot drawn heh pudatau k' ish-veh sasu, heh instead t' wuh gas'rak el'ru au had wuh shek-tukh kik k' if ek'wak heh anon au kastorau au tor increase ish-veh sahr. U' dogs nash terrible sasu skasau heh addressed au, heh u' dogs au obeyed ish-veh. Svi' person au vesh' cadaverous heh blackavized, heh ish-veh isachya vesh' sai-vel-tor svi' wu tcha-tor, if na' wuh pi' ir glazhau spo' nesh-kur ha'fek, heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh singularly threatening sagluvaya tor ish-veh handsome countenance. Ish-veh bezhun vesh' t' wuh pla-kur t' wuh yen-tor-me-ri, heh t' wuh profound melancholy, korsau lu au vesh' taul-tor ish-veh kik vi' du, na' if wak dahkuh yon-kur gla-tor saudau svi' au heh lit au abru horribly. Svi' manner, vel t' wuh grand seigneur fam dvun clung tor ish-veh, ni ik au kauk tres-tor du abru k' wuh sov, heh i ma vesh' var-tor ik au vesh' wuh _raconteur_ t' repute. Au vesh' worla weht sinister do lu au vesh' danik polite, if nam-tor probably wuh truest nisan t' breeding; heh wuh sohk'es t' ish-veh diction, kauk lu au vesh' swearing, rai lehkuh tor wuh distinction t' ish-veh demeanour, gluvau ish-veh veh t' wuh natya vishizhau s' ish-veh hali-sutra. Wuh sasu t' indomitable courage, ish-veh vesh' leralmin-tor ik wuh goh vel au shied na' vesh' wuh glan t' ish-veh sha' khaf, if vesh' bali heh t' wuh ritsuri kur. Svi' sai-vel au somewhat aped wuh attire katravah k' wuh ahm t' charles ii, having puzhu-tor ish-veh leralmin-tor svi' ein earlier wak-krus t' ish-veh career ik au spitau wuh flekh resemblance tor wuh has-bosh-fated stuarts; heh svi' ish-veh ru'lut au had wuh holder t' ish-veh sha' contrivance if enabled ish-veh tor vuzh dahkuh cigars na' wuh'wak. Tonk'peh undoubtedly wuh grimmest krus t' ish-veh vesh' ish-veh shek-tukh spahk. Kal-tor etek i' stau wuh pirate, tor gluvaya kik’s method. Ha'gel-razh dungi tor. U' au be' dvun, ha'gel-razh lurches clumsily tehnat ish-veh, ruffling ish-veh lace hmoi'neks; wuh kik pohshau forth, tra' nam-tor wuh tearing ralash heh veh screech, yi wuh ak'shem nam-tor kicked aside, heh wuh pirates be' dvun fi'. Au has ri kauk taken wuh cigars s' ish-veh ru'lut. Such nam-tor wuh terrible sasu tehnat ik peter sunil nam-tor pitted. If dungi skil? Fi' wuh yut t' wuh pirates, stealing noiselessly ne' wuh t'naehm-yut, if nam-tor ri visible tor inexperienced bezhun, sarlah wuh redskins, kanok veh t' au k' ish-veh bezhun puhnk-tor. Au lesh tomahawks heh lipau, heh ish-veh sai-fam ak'shem gleam k' kras heh elmin. Strung pa' au nam-tor patam-ek'wadi, t' sa-kan u' muhl u' t' pirates, na' aifa nam-tor wuh piccaninny tribe, heh ri tor nam-tor confused k' wuh softer-hearted delawares il wuh hurons. Svi' wuh hali, fi' ek' fours, nam-tor lo'uk suk' pi' panther, wuh kyi'i t' ni wehk patam-ek'wadi ik svi' ish-veh la' shul au somewhat rashertau ish-veh progress. Bringing abru wuh za', wuh shi' greatest tehvar, sarlah tiger lily, proudly abru-tor, wuh princess svi' ish-veh sha' gas'rak. She nam-tor wuh danik vaksurik t' dusky dianas heh wuh belle t' wuh piccaninnies, coquettish, samu heh amorous k' da-tor; tra' nam-tor ri wuh kyi'i vi would ri ma wuh wayward vel tor ko-telsu, tonk'peh she staves ska' wuh altar k' wuh hatchet. Glantau uf au be' dvun abru' tevan-tor pi'gel rik' tor wuh slightest ralash. Wuh goh ralash tor nam-tor puzhu-tor nam-tor ish-veh somewhat ras eshan. Wuh kla-min nam-tor ik au nam-tor ek' wuh pi' thelik aishan i' po' wuh ras gorging, tonk'peh svi' wak au dungi ar'kadan nash ska'. Na' wuh moment, however, ish-veh constitutes ish-veh chief tehvar. Wuh redskins sasaudau u' sarlah au spo' duv, heh ak ish-veh shi nam-tor taken k' wuh beasts, wuh lo'uk heh motley procession: lions, tigers, bears, heh wuh va' smaller savage vel ik sasahr-tor s' au, na' kanok ves t' beast, heh, weht wa', ek' wuh sasu-eaters, ha-tor nak k' jowl fi' wuh favoured vikuvtra. Ish-veh lahv nam-tor hanging si', au nam-tor k'avon tor-mu-yor. Lu au ma be' dvun-tor, sarlah wuh kim-shah khlop t' ek', wuh masuk' crocodile. Etek dungau gla-tor na' ik she nam-tor looking presently. Wuh crocodile be' dvun-tor, tonk'peh ak wuh sa-kan saudau va'ashiv, na' wuh procession bolau fator indefinitely abi' veh t' wuh parties pehkau il rubai its sahr. Yi sahris au dungi nam-tor fi-tor tik vath. Ek' nam-tor keeping wuh nasik glazhau-si' svi' khom, tonk'peh rim suspects ik wuh tehvar lau nam-tor creeping abru s' za'. Nash gluvau uf yeht wuh vikuvtra vesh'. Wuh wuh'rak tor tevan s' wuh dvun-tor da-kuv vesh' wuh sa-kan. Au flung themselves ne' fi' wuh sward, beyik ish-veh underground ha-kel. “i tor istaya peter would sarlah pla', ” kanok veh t' au leralmin-tor nervously, hi svi' pidek heh fam dvun weht svi' breadth au vesh' ek' larger do ish-veh khart-lan. “i am wuh goh veh vi nam-tor ri kwes t' wuh pirates, ” slightly leralmin-tor, svi' wuh molu ik prevented ish-veh hasu wuh paik favourite; tonk'peh sos'eh ein irak ralash ertau ish-veh, na' au hau hastily, “tonk'peh i istaya au would sarlah pla', heh var-tor etek whether au has puzhu-tor sovek-vel weht pa' cinderella.” au variben t' cinderella, heh tootles vesh' confident ik ish-veh ko-mekh bolau ma vesh' maut spo' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' goh svi' peter’s absence ik au kupi stariben t' ko-mekh, wuh subject hasu zadik k' ish-veh u' silly. “ek' i vokau pa' t'nash-veh ko-mekh, ” nibs var-tor au, “nam-tor ik she k'ashiv leralmin-tor tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh, ‘oh, uf i istaya i had wuh cheque-dunap t' t'nash-veh sha'!’ i don’t fai-tor ra wuh cheque-dunap nam-tor, tonk'peh i dang aishan ashaya tor mazhiv-kur-tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh veh.” du' au variben au puzhu-tor wuh irak ralash. Du il i, ri hasu kwai vel t' wuh lapan, would ma puzhu-tor nothing, tonk'peh au puzhu-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh grim song: “yo ho, yo ho, wuh pirate ha'kiv, wuh haifan o’ grat heh hinek, wuh merry wadan, wuh hempen man-elakh, heh hey na' davy jones.” na' wuh'wak wuh pakik sa-kan—tonk'peh wilat nam-tor au? Au nam-tor rai longer tra'. Rabbits kupi ri ma sasaudau weht sahris. I dungi var-tor du wilat au nam-tor. K' wuh kaulauf t' nibs, vi has darted maf tor reconnoitre, au nam-tor already svi' ish-veh ha-kel ne' wuh solektra, wuh maut delightful residence t' if etek dungau gla-tor wuh rom deal presently. Tonk'peh uf ma au pulau ish-veh? Na' tra' nam-tor rai entrance tor nam-tor gla-tor, ri ni mau u' wuh suk kov, if kuv padukau maf, would disclose wuh ru'lut t' wuh tauk. Glazhau closely, however, heh du lau pitoh ik tra' nam-tor la' stehkuh suk lap, tik k' wuh razh svi' its hollow lap-fek u' suk u' wuh sa-kan. Aifa nam-tor wuh stehkuh entrances tor wuh ha-kel ne' wuh solektra, na' if kik has vesh' searching svi' vain aifa wehk aikum. Dungi au talal ish-veh tonight? U' wuh pirates storilau, wuh sahris bezhun t' starkey sighted nibs disappearing k'fai wuh lapan, heh na' wuh'wak ish-veh el'ru-pohshayek kahai si'. Tonk'peh wuh shek-tukh spahk gripped ish-veh tipan. “khart-lan, kal-tor hal-tor!” au maf-tor, writhing. I' na' wuh wuh'rak wak etek zhu-tor wuh spes t' kik. Ish-veh vesh' wuh nesh-kur spes. “shitau pla' ik el'ru-pohshayek wuh'rak, ” ish-veh leralmin-tor threateningly. “ish-veh vesh' veh t' eifa sa-kan du fnu-ven. I kupi ma pohshaya ish-veh tevik.” “ay, heh wuh ralash would ma katau tiger lily’s redskins fi-tor etek. Tor du aitlun tor pak-tor ish-veh patam-ek'wadi?” “dungau i po' ish-veh, khart-lan, ” ya'akash pathetic smee, “heh tickle ish-veh k' johnny corkscrew?” smee had vaksurik ahm na' kanok-vei, heh ish-veh cutlass vesh' johnny corkscrew, fai'ei au wiggled ish-veh svi' wuh skek. Veh kupi mention wehk lovable noshtra svi' smee. Na' instance, po' killing, ish-veh vesh' ish-veh spectacles au psethau instead t' ish-veh wun. “johnny’s wuh ralash-fam katravahsu, ” au reminded kik. “ri i', smee, ” kik leralmin-tor darkly. “au nam-tor goh veh, heh i aitlun tor mischief ek' wuh stehkuh. Scatter heh glazhau na' au.” wuh pirates sasaudau among wuh lap, heh svi' wuh moment ish-veh khart-lan heh smee vesh' sa'awek. Kik heaved wuh ras spes-tevan, heh i fai-tor ri po ish-veh vesh', sos'eh ish-veh vesh' fai'ei t' wuh mos vaksur t' wuh khru, tonk'peh tra' sarlah abru' ish-veh wuh aitlun tor confide tor ish-veh faithful bo’yel wuh var t' ish-veh ha'kiv. Au stariben wu heh earnestly, tonk'peh ra ish-veh vesh' ek' pa' smee, vi vesh' rather stupid, did ri fai-tor svi' wuh least. Anon au kum-tor wuh zhit peter. “danik t' ek', ” kik vesh' taran passionately, “i aitlun ish-veh khart-lan, peter sunil. ’twas au tresahk ska' t'nash-veh kar.” au brandished wuh kik threateningly. “i’ve bek-tor wu tor hutau ish-veh el'ru k' nash. Oh, i’ll bezhun-masu ish-veh!” “heh wi, ” leralmin-tor smee, “i ma k'ashiv puzhu-tor du leralmin ik kik vesh' don wuh nosahp t' el'ru, na' combing wuh isachya heh vath homely nam-tor-tor.” “ay, ” wuh khart-lan kilko-tor, “kuv i vesh' wuh ko-mekh i would pray ki' t'nash-veh kanu pukeshta k' nash instead t' ik, ” heh au vishizhau wuh glazhau t' pride fi-tor ish-veh shek-tukh el'ru heh veh t' scorn fi-tor wuh vath. Yi va'ashiv au kwal-tor. “peter flung t'nash-veh kar, ” au leralmin-tor, wincing, “tor wuh crocodile ik pavesh-tor tor nam-tor be' dvun-tor k'.” “i ma k'ashiv, ” leralmin-tor smee, “pubeglanau ish-veh flekh dread t' crocodiles.” “ri t' crocodiles, ” kik yeht-tor ish-veh, “tonk'peh t' ish-veh crocodile.” au ne-tor ish-veh spes. “ish-veh tishau t'nash-veh kar ni mau, smee, ik ish-veh has zahal-tor me ek'wak opi', s' masutra tor masutra heh s' solektra tor solektra, licking its bru-lar na' wuh shom t' me.” “svi' wuh yut, ” leralmin-tor smee, “ish-veh’s wihfelau t' wuh compliment.” “i aitlun rai such compliments, ” kik barked petulantly. “i aitlun peter sunil, vi wuh'rak mazhiv-kur-tor wuh brute its zahvan na' me.” au hayal-tor ne' fi' wuh suk taik-luk, heh i' tra' vesh' wuh quiver svi' ish-veh spes. “smee, ” au leralmin-tor huskily, “ik crocodile would ma had me fa' nash, tonk'peh k' wuh kunli pavesh ish-veh vitem-tor wuh wak-vel if hal-tor tick tick svi'udish ish-veh, heh ni fa' ish-veh mokuhlek pulau me i zhu-tor wuh tick heh terk.” au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, tonk'peh svi' wuh hollow yut. “ein gad, ” leralmin-tor smee, “wuh wak-vel dungi sahr-tor ne', heh yi au’ll prah du.” kik wetted ish-veh pseth bru-lar. “ay, ” au leralmin-tor, “ik’s wuh pthak ik haunts me.” opi' sitting ne' au had olau curiously lamekh. “smee, ” au leralmin-tor, “nash ku-san nam-tor fal.” au spen-tor abru. “odds bobs, mah-vel heh el'abrashayek i’m yontau.” au linisau wuh taik-luk, if vesh' t' wuh suk'es heh solidity ri-fainu fi' wuh mainland; au ar'kada tor seshaya ish-veh abru, heh sarlah ish-veh maf na' wuh'wak svi' ish-veh el'ru, na' ish-veh had rai gir. Ri-fainusu fam dvun, vuzh began na' wuh'wak tor she-tor. Wuh pirates glazhau na' tik vath. “wuh vuzh-mev!” au fi' sporiben. Au had indeed discovered wuh vuzh-mev t' wuh ha-kel ne' wuh solektra. Ish-veh vesh' wuh custom t' wuh sa-kan tor pehkaya ish-veh k' wuh taik-luk lu nemut vesh' svi' wuh neighbourhood. Ri goh vuzh sasarlah t' ish-veh. Tra' sarlah isha kanu’s spes, na' ni safe did wuh sa-kan olau svi' ish-veh hiding-shi ik au vesh' gaily chattering. Wuh pirates shroi grimly, heh yi va'prah wuh taik-luk. Au glazhau pa' au heh noted wuh razh svi' wuh stehkuh lap. “did du zhu-tor au leralmin peter sunil’s s' ha-kel?” smee zhal-tor, fidgeting k' johnny corkscrew. Kik nodded. Au lam-tor na' wuh akarshif pakik svi' nahp, heh na' kim-shah wuh curdling abru'teruklar-ru'lut lit abru ish-veh swarthy limuk. Smee had vesh' waiting na' ish-veh. “unrip ish-veh dotor, khart-lan, ” au maf-tor eagerly. “tor fun tor wuh hali, ” kik kilko-tor slowly k'fai ish-veh zud, “heh fas-tor wuh suk don-ka cake t' wuh jolly thickness k' yar-kur slor-tukh fi' ish-veh. Tra' mokuhlek nam-tor tonk'peh veh tvi-shal ne', na' tra' nam-tor tonk'peh veh vuzh-mev. Wuh silly moles had ri wuh kash-ral tor gla-tor ik au did ri bolaya wuh svep apiece. Ik gluvau au ma rai ko-mekh. Etek dungi trasha wuh cake fi' wuh gef t' wuh mermaids’ masutra-muzh. Aifa sa-kan nam-tor kwon-hau-ov mahalan pa' tra', mavaun k' wuh mermaids. Au dungi talal wuh cake heh au dungi gobble ish-veh abru, fai'ei, having rai ko-mekh, au don’t fai-tor uf tehvar-bosh ’tis tor yokul don-ka damp cake.” au thorau vi' laughter, ri hollow laughter i', tonk'peh trau laughter. “aha, au dungi tev-tor.” smee had shroi k' growing admiration. “ish-veh’s wuh wickedest, prettiest policy ek'wak i puzhu-tor t'!” au maf-tor, heh svi' ish-veh exultation au tam-tor heh sang: “avast, belay, lu i saudau, k' pthak au’re overtook; nought’s losrak fi-tor ish-veh hinek lu du ma shaken spahk k' kik.” au began wuh zehl, tonk'peh au worla shahtau ish-veh, na' wuh'ashiv ralash shau svi' heh stilled au. Tra' vesh' palikauk such wuh tiny ralash ik wuh mor lau ma tevan-tor fi' ish-veh heh smothered ish-veh, tonk'peh u' sarlah ish-veh nearer ish-veh vesh' weht natya. Tick tick tick tick! Kik lam-tor shuddering, veh ash'ya svi' wuh sov. “wuh crocodile!” au hushau, heh bounded maf, zahal-tor k' ish-veh bo’yel. Ish-veh vesh' indeed wuh crocodile. Ish-veh had be' dvun-tor wuh redskins, vi vesh' i' fi' wuh yut t' wuh vath pirates. Ish-veh stan-tor fi' po' kik. Wuh'wak weht wuh sa-kan sasarlah vi' wuh tu'ash; tonk'peh wuh tehvar t' wuh mu-yor vesh' ri wi abru', na' presently nibs rushed breathless vi' ish-veh midst, pursued k' wuh sa'haf t' wolves. Wuh lahv t' wuh pursuers vesh' hanging si'; wuh baying t' au vesh' horrible. “korsau me, korsau me!” maf-tor nibs, tevan-tor fi' wuh solektra. “tonk'peh ra mokuhlek etek tor, ra mokuhlek etek tor?” ish-veh vesh' wuh pid compliment tor peter ik na' ik dire moment ish-veh nahp da-tor tor ish-veh. “ra would peter tor?” au maf-tor simultaneously. Siyah svi' wuh ka esh au maf-tor, “peter would glazhau na' au k'fai ish-veh mal.” heh yi, “kal-tor etek tor ra peter would tor.” ish-veh nam-tor ved wuh danik successful yut t' defying wolves, heh u' veh sa-kan au keh'sei heh glazhau k'fai ish-veh mal. Wuh thurai moment nam-tor wuh wu veh, tonk'peh skil sarlah sahris, na' u' wuh sa-kan storilau fi-tor au svi' wuh terrible attitude, wuh wolves eku-tor ish-veh harr heh sasahr-tor. I' nibs she-tor s' wuh solektra, heh wuh vath nahp ik ish-veh staring bezhun fam dvun gla-tor wuh wolves. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri wolves gla-tor ish-veh. “ki'gla-tor nash-veh wuh wonderfuller vel, ” au maf-tor, u' au hoknau pauk ish-veh eagerly. “wuh lo'uk wan-kur kushel. Ish-veh nam-tor hashan nash yut.” “ra ves t' wuh kushel, tor du nah-tor?” “i don’t fai-tor, ” nibs leralmin-tor, awestruck, “tonk'peh ish-veh glazhau ni weary, heh u' ish-veh hash-tor ish-veh nau, ‘ri donku-tor wendy.’” “ri donku-tor wendy?” “i vokau, ” leralmin-tor slightly instantly, “tra' nam-tor kushel puvutau wendies.” “gla-tor, sarlah ish-veh!” maf-tor curly, pointing tor wendy svi' wuh heavens. Wendy vesh' i' siyah overhead, heh au kupi zhu-tor ish-veh plaintive maf. Tonk'peh weht natya sarlah wuh shrill spes t' tinker kus-vakh. Wuh kis-ka pu'a had i' vishizhau ska' ek' pasut t' friendship, heh vesh' darting na' ish-veh shi-kar-tor s' kanok kharat, pinching savagely tik wak she estuhl. “hullo, tink, ” maf-tor wuh wondering sa-kan. Tink’s kilko rang si': “peter aitlu du tor pohshau wuh wendy.” ish-veh vesh' ri svi' ish-veh malat tor deshker lu peter ordered. “kal-tor etek tor ra peter istau!” maf-tor wuh velik sa-kan. “sahris, ovalau heh kliton!” ek' tonk'peh tootles popped ne' ish-veh lap. Au had wuh kes-wun heh kliton k' ish-veh, heh tink noted ish-veh, heh tetau ish-veh pi' el'ru. “sahris, tootles, sahris, ” she shei. “peter dungi nam-tor ni sanoi.” tootles excitedly fitted wuh kliton tor ish-veh kes-wun. “s' wuh yut, tink, ” au saul-tor, heh yi au pohshau, heh wendy nuv-tor tor wuh solektra k' wuh kliton svi' ish-veh thasek. Chapter vi. Wuh pi' kelek duhik tootles vesh' standing spo' wuh conqueror abru' wendy’s ak'shem lu wuh vath sa-kan sprang, armed, s' ish-veh lap. “du nam-tor nuh' tab-ma, ” au maf-tor proudly, “i ma pohshaya wuh wendy. Peter dungi nam-tor ni sanoi k' me.” overhead tinker kus-vakh saul-tor “silly ass!” heh darted vi' hiding. Wuh vath did ri zhu-tor ish-veh. Au had crowded pauk wendy, heh u' au glazhau wuh terrible silence tevan-tor fi-tor wuh lapan. Kuv wendy’s khaf-spol had vesh' beating au would ek' ma puzhu-tor ish-veh. Slightly vesh' wuh wuh'rak tor stariben. “nash nam-tor rai kushel, ” au leralmin-tor svi' wuh pahth-tor spes. “i nah-tor nash bolau nam-tor wuh t'sai.” “wuh t'sai?” leralmin-tor tootles, heh tevan-tor wuh-trembling. “heh etek ma pustau ish-veh, ” nibs leralmin-tor hoarsely. Au ek' whipped ska' ish-veh taik. “i' gla-tor nash-veh, ” curly leralmin-tor: “peter vesh' bringing ish-veh tor etek.” au threw himself sorrowfully fi' wuh solektra. “wuh t'sai tor nem-tor tun t' etek na' kim-shah, ” leralmin-tor veh t' wuh t'dahsu, “heh du ma pustau ish-veh!” au vesh' sorry na' ish-veh, tonk'peh sorrier na' themselves, heh lu au nem-tor wuh ash nearer au au da-tor s' ish-veh. Tootles’ limuk vesh' maut wan-kur, tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh dignity pa' ish-veh i' ik had worla vesh' tra' fa'. “i did ish-veh, ” au leralmin-tor, reflecting. “lu t'sai nam-tor-tor tor sarlah tor me svi' sahr-tor-tor, i leralmin-tor, ‘takov ko-mekh, takov ko-mekh.’ tonk'peh lu na' kim-shah she really sarlah, i pohshaya ish-veh.” au dvun-tor slowly maf. “don’t hal-tor, ” au puvutau svi' pity. “i bolau, ” au kilko-tor, shaking; “i am ni kwes t' peter.” ish-veh vesh' na' nash tragic moment ik au puzhu-tor wuh ralash if tor wuh khaf-spol t' kanok veh t' au shen tor ish-veh ru'lut. Au puzhu-tor peter kushel. “peter!” au maf-tor, na' ish-veh vesh' kwon-hau-ov thus ik au signalled ish-veh fun. “ip-sut ish-veh, ” au zhal-tor, heh hoknau hastily pa' wendy. Tonk'peh tootles lam-tor aloof. Va'ashiv sarlah ik ringing kushel, heh peter eku-tor svi' khom t' au. “na'shaya, sa-kan, ” au maf-tor, heh mechanically au saluted, heh yi va'ashiv vesh' silence. Au kwal-tor. “i am pla', ” au leralmin-tor hotly, “po tor du ri cheer?” au tu'ash ish-veh ru'lut, tonk'peh wuh cheers would ri sarlah. Au overlooked ish-veh svi' ish-veh haste tor var-tor wuh glorious tidings. “lo'uk ro'fori, sa-kan, ” au maf-tor, “i ma katau na' kim-shah wuh ko-mekh na' du ek'.” fam dvun rai ralash, kaula wuh pi' thud s' tootles u' au eku-tor fi' ish-veh mal-nef. “ma du ri gla-tor ish-veh?” ya'akash peter, becoming troubled. “she flew nash yut.” “ah me!” veh spes leralmin-tor, heh wuh'ashiv leralmin-tor, “oh, mournful gad.” tootles she-tor. “peter, ” au leralmin-tor quietly, “i dungi gluvaya ish-veh tor du, ” heh lu wuh vath would fam dvun ma ipik ish-veh au leralmin-tor, “pla', t'dahsu, kal-tor peter gla-tor.” ni au ek' lam-tor pla', heh kal-tor ish-veh gla-tor, heh po' au had glazhau na' wuh pi' wak au did ri fai-tor ra tor tor thurai. “she nam-tor tevik, ” au leralmin-tor uncomfortably. “sos'eh she nam-tor koltha na' hasu tevik.” au nahp t' spen-tor ska' svi' wuh comic wihfelau t' yut till au vesh' s' glan t' ish-veh, heh yi worla going be' wuh gla-tor sovek weht. Au would ek' ma vesh' glad tor zahal-tor kuv au had ovsoh nash. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh kliton. Au nem-tor ish-veh s' ish-veh khaf-spol heh limuk-tor ish-veh zhel. “t'vi kliton?” au halishau sternly. “t'nash-veh, peter, ” leralmin-tor tootles fi' ish-veh mal-nef. “oh, dastard el'ru, ” peter leralmin-tor, heh au ashenau wuh kliton tor nam-tor-tor ish-veh u' wuh lipitah. Tootles did ri flinch. Au bared ish-veh thasek. “kwul, peter, ” au leralmin-tor firmly, “kwul yeht.” dah'wak did peter ashenau wuh kliton, heh dah'wak did ish-veh el'ru tevan. “i fam yehat kwul, ” au leralmin-tor k' teshan, “tra' nam-tor vel stays t'nash-veh el'ru.” ek' glazhau na' ish-veh svi' wonder, korsau nibs, vi fortunately glazhau na' wendy. “ish-veh nam-tor she, ” au maf-tor, “wuh wendy t'sai, gla-tor, ish-veh kar!” wonderful tor relate, wendy had ashenau ish-veh kar. Nibs keh'sei abru' ish-veh heh shroi reverently. “i nah-tor she leralmin-tor, ‘ri donku-tor tootles, ’” au zhal-tor. “she ha-tor, ” peter leralmin-tor briefly. Slightly maf-tor instantly, “wuh wendy t'sai ha-tor.” yi peter knelt be' ish-veh heh afer-tor ish-veh gonaf. Du vokau she had shitau ish-veh fi' wuh naf-elakh ik she sai-vel-tor pauk ish-veh talu. “gla-tor, ” au leralmin-tor, “wuh kliton kwul-tor tehnat nash. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh shok i mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh has korsau ish-veh ha'kiv.” “i vokau shok-tor, ” slightly interposed sahris, “kal-tor me gla-tor ish-veh. Ay, ik’s wuh shok.” peter did ri zhu-tor ish-veh. Au vesh' begging wendy tor prah weh-rom sahris, ni ik au kupi gluvaya ish-veh wuh mermaids. Veling she kupi ri kilko-srashiv wi, hasu fam dvun svi' wuh frightful faint; tonk'peh s' overhead sarlah wuh wailing pitoh. “shroi tor tink, ” leralmin-tor curly, “she nam-tor maf-tor fai'ei wuh wendy ha-tor.” yi au had tor var-tor peter t' tink’s tr'y'kak, heh siyah worla had au gla-tor ish-veh glazhau ni harr-krus. “shroi, tinker kus-vakh, ” au maf-tor, “i am ish-veh t'hy'la rai weht. Begone s' me na' ek'wak.” she flew fi' tor ish-veh tipan heh pleaded, tonk'peh au brushed ish-veh ska'. Ri abi' wendy va'ashiv ashenau ish-veh kar did au relent sufficiently tor leralmin, “muhl, ri na' ek'wak, tonk'peh na' wuh bosh wehk gad.” tor du nah-tor tinker kus-vakh vesh' grateful tor wendy na' raising ish-veh kar? Oh tal-kam rai, worla aitlu tor k'hy ish-veh ni mau. Pu'a indeed nam-tor flekh, heh peter, vi ken-tor au buhfik, k'ashiv cuffed au. Tonk'peh ra tor tor k' wendy svi' ish-veh la' delicate fupa s' t' muhl'es? “kal-tor etek lesh ish-veh ne' vi' wuh kelek, ” curly suggested. “ay, ” leralmin-tor slightly, “ik nam-tor ra veh tor k' t'sai.” “rai, rai, ” peter leralmin-tor, “du bolau ri esta ish-veh. Ish-veh would ri nam-tor sufficiently respectful.” “ik, ” leralmin-tor slightly, “nam-tor ra i vesh' thinking.” “tonk'peh kuv she ti tra', ” tootles leralmin-tor, “she dungi tev-tor.” “ay, she dungi tev-tor, ” slightly nafai-tor, “tonk'peh tra' nam-tor rai yut si'.” “ha, tra' nam-tor, ” maf-tor peter. “kal-tor etek torvau wuh pi' kelek pauk ish-veh.” au vesh' ek' delighted. “sahris, ” au ordered au, “katau me tik t' du wuh buhfik t' ra etek ma. Gut etwel kelek. Nam-tor nasik.” svi' wuh moment au vesh' u' toranik u' ogsu wuh mu-yor fa' wuh wedding. Au skurried nash yut heh ik, ne' na' bedding, abru na' yon-lapan, heh du' au vesh' na' ish-veh, vi dang saudau tonk'peh john heh michael. U' au zaseshau bi' wuh solektra au tevan-tor asleep standing, pehkau, woke abru, dvun-tor wuh'ashiv ash heh yuk-tor va'ashiv. “john, john, ” michael would maf, “wake abru! Wilat nam-tor nana, john, heh ko-mekh?” heh yi john would tetaya ish-veh bezhun heh mutter, “ish-veh nam-tor yeht, etek did hash-tor.” du lau nam-tor sure au vesh' maut vas-tor tor talal peter. “hullo, peter, ” au leralmin-tor. “hullo, ” kilko-tor peter amicably, hi au had ved yen-tor au. Au vesh' maut toranik na' wuh moment measuring wendy k' ish-veh ash'ya tor gla-tor uf suk wuh kelek she would bolaya. Veling au tvai tor trasha tvi-shal na' ku-san heh wuh pasu. John heh michael glantau ish-veh. “nam-tor wendy asleep?” au ya'akash. “ha.” “john, ” michael proposed, “kal-tor etek wake ish-veh heh prah ish-veh tor tor mu'yor-yem na' etek, ” tonk'peh u' au leralmin-tor ish-veh ein t' wuh vath sa-kan rushed fi' carrying khlup na' wuh kelek t' wuh kelek. “glazhau na' au!” au maf-tor. “curly, ” leralmin-tor peter svi' ish-veh danik captainy spes, “gla-tor ik aifa sa-kan gol'nev svi' wuh kelek t' wuh kelek.” “ay, ay, osu.” “torvau wuh kelek?” sporiben john. “na' wuh wendy, ” leralmin-tor curly. “na' wendy?” john leralmin-tor, aghast. “po, she nam-tor goh wuh ko-kan!” “ik, ” danau curly, “nam-tor po etek nam-tor ish-veh dvinsu.” “du? Wendy’s dvinsu!” “ha, ” leralmin-tor peter, “heh du isha. Maf k' au.” wuh astounded sa-kai vesh' zaseshau maf tor hack heh hew heh lesh. “ku-san heh wuh fender wuh'rak, ” peter ordered. “yi etek dungau torvau wuh kelek pauk au.” “ay, ” leralmin-tor slightly, “ik nam-tor uf wuh kelek nam-tor torvau; ish-veh ek' sarlah pla' tor me.” peter nahp t' kanok-vei. “slightly, ” au maf-tor, “zaprah wuh hassu.” “ay, ay, ” leralmin-tor slightly na' wuh'wak, heh sasaudau, scratching ish-veh patam. Tonk'peh au fai-tor peter bolau nam-tor obeyed, heh au fun-tor svi' wuh moment, sai-vel-tor john’s taik heh looking solemn. “sanoi, osu, ” leralmin-tor peter, going tor ish-veh, “nam-tor du wuh hassu?” wuh natyan svi' ish-veh heh wuh vath sa-kan na' such wuh wak vesh' ik au fai-tor ish-veh vesh' tor-dva-tor, du' tor ish-veh tor-dva-tor heh yeht vesh' exactly wuh ka vel. Nash sometimes troubled au, u' lu au had tor tor-dva-tor ik au had had ish-veh aru-yem. Kuv au shau ne' svi' ish-veh tor-dva-tor au rapped au fi' wuh ozh-lesek. “ha, t'nash-veh pi' sasu, ” slightly anxiously kilko-tor, vi had chapped ozh-lesek. “sanoi, osu, ” peter danau, “wuh t'sai ti maut has-bosh.” she vesh' lying na' ish-veh ash'ya, tonk'peh slightly had wuh kash-ral ri tor gla-tor ish-veh. “tut, tut, tut, ” au leralmin-tor, “wilat tor she ti?” “svi' yonder glade.” “i dungi shitau wuh makh vel svi' ish-veh ru'lut, ” leralmin-tor slightly, heh au tor-dva-tor tor tor ish-veh, du' peter bek-tor. Ish-veh vesh' wuh anxious moment lu wuh makh vel vesh' saseshau. “uf nam-tor she?” inquired peter. “tut, tut, tut, ” leralmin-tor slightly, “nash has bohrau ish-veh.” “i am glad!” peter maf-tor. “i dungi vutau va'ashiv svi' wuh khru, ” slightly leralmin-tor; “mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh kahm theris-masu s' wuh cup k' wuh spout tor ish-veh; ” tonk'peh po' au had fun-tor wuh taik tor john au blew suk' esh, if vesh' ish-veh es'merka fi' escaping s' wuh rihag'es. Svi' wuh meantime wuh lapan had vesh' alive k' wuh ralash t' la'ash; siyah kanok-vei bolau na' wuh cosy kelek already ti na' wendy’s ash'ya. “kuv goh etek fai-tor, ” leralmin-tor veh, “wuh ves t' kelek she tishau buhfik.” “peter, ” saul-tor wuh'ashiv, “she nam-tor dvun-tor svi' ish-veh yuk.” “ish-veh ru'lut tu'ash, ” maf-tor wuh wuh, looking respectfully vi' ish-veh. “oh, lovely!” “sos'eh she nam-tor going tor uralau svi' ish-veh yuk, ” leralmin-tor peter. “wendy, uralau wuh ves t' kelek du would spo' ki'.” iyi, rik' sharu ish-veh bezhun, wendy began tor uralau: “i istaya i had wuh takov kelek, wuh littlest ek'wak gla-tor, k' funny pi' yon-kur temok heh kamu t' mossy yar-kur.” au gurgled k' mak na' nash, na' k' wuh greatest rom kunli wuh khlup au had katau vesh' terpauk k' yon-kur ksa-khaf, heh ek' wuh solektra vesh' carpeted k' yekuhl. U' au rattled abru wuh pi' kelek au shau vi' song themselves: “etek’ve torvau wuh pi' temok heh kamu heh tor wuh lovely svep, ni var-tor etek, ko-mekh wendy, ra nam-tor du wanting weht?” tor nash she kilko-tor greedily: “oh, really thurai i nah-tor i’ll ma sa-ka-ashausu krani ek' pa', k' roses peeping svi', du fai-tor, heh kan-bu peeping si'.” k' wuh salur t' ish-veh ozh-dukal au tor krani, heh suk kin-kur mor vesh' wuh blinds. Tonk'peh roses—? “roses, ” maf-tor peter sternly. Sahris au tor-dva-tor tor tor'ovau wuh loveliest roses abru wuh temok. Kan-bu? Tor prevent peter ordering kan-bu au hurried vi' song va'ashiv: “etek’ve tor wuh roses peeping si', wuh babes nam-tor na' wuh svep, etek fam yehat tor ourselves, du fai-tor, ’cos etek’ve vesh' tor fa'.” peter, seeing nash tor nam-tor wuh rom idea, na' wuh'wak pretended ik ish-veh vesh' ish-veh sha'. Wuh kelek vesh' ved vaksurik, heh rai vet wendy vesh' maut cosy k'svi, hi, veling, au kupi rai longer gla-tor ish-veh. Peter strode abru heh ne', ordering finishing estuhl. Nothing stron-tor ish-veh eagle bezhun. Aishan lu ish-veh seemed absolutely shahtau: “tra'’s rai knocker fi' wuh svep, ” au leralmin-tor. Au vesh' maut kafusik, tonk'peh tootles mazhiv-kur-tor wuh lad t' ish-veh ash'el, heh ish-veh tor wuh marom knocker. Absolutely shahtau i', au nahp. Ri t' zeshau t' ish-veh. “tra'’s rai vuzh-mev, ” peter leralmin-tor; “etek bolau ma wuh vuzh-mev.” “ish-veh certainly tor bolaya wuh vuzh-mev, ” leralmin-tor john importantly. Nash mazhiv-kur-tor peter wuh idea. Au snatched wuh taik ska' john’s patam, knocked si' wuh lanet, heh shitau wuh taik fi' wuh kamu. Wuh pi' kelek vesh' ni sanoi tor ma such wuh capital vuzh-mev ik, u' kuv tor leralmin nemaiyo, vuzh iyi began tor sasarlah t' wuh taik. I' really heh truly ish-veh vesh' shahtau. Nothing hafau tor tor tonk'peh tor knock. “ek' glazhau ish-veh buhfik, ” peter vikau au; “wuh'rak impressions nam-tor awfully yauluhk.” au vesh' glad kling ya'akash ish-veh ra wuh'rak impressions nam-tor; au vesh' ek' nuh' toranik looking ish-veh buhfik. Au knocked politely, heh i' wuh lapan vesh' u' fam dvun u' wuh kanu, ri wuh ralash tor nam-tor puzhu-tor kaula s' tinker kus-vakh, vi vesh' watching s' wuh khlup heh openly sneering. Ra wuh sa-kan vesh' wondering vesh', would sovek veh kilko-srashiv wuh knock? Kuv wuh t'sai, ra would she nam-tor spo'? Wuh svep tu'ash heh wuh t'sai sasarlah. Ish-veh vesh' wendy. Au ek' whipped ska' ish-veh taik. She glazhau properly ak'wikmun, heh nash vesh' aishan uf au had rok-tor she would glazhau. “wilat am i?” she leralmin-tor. Veling slightly vesh' wuh wuh'rak tor prah ish-veh zhit svi'. “wendy t'sai, ” au leralmin-tor rapidly, “na' du etek torvau nash kelek.” “oh, leralmin du’re sanoi, ” maf-tor nibs. “lovely, ashal-veh kelek, ” wendy leralmin-tor, heh au vesh' wuh maut zhit au had rok-tor she would leralmin. “heh etek nam-tor ish-veh kanu, ” maf-tor wuh t'dahsu. Yi ek' went fi' ish-veh mal-nef, heh holding si' ish-veh kar maf-tor, “o wendy t'sai, nam-tor etwel ko-mekh.” “ought i?” wendy leralmin-tor, ek' shining. “veling ish-veh’s frightfully sem-rik, tonk'peh gla-tor du i am goh wuh pi' ko-kan. I ma rai yeht veshtaya.” “ik doesn’t tukh, ” leralmin-tor peter, u' kuv au vesh' wuh goh person la' vi fai-tor ek' pa' ish-veh, hi au vesh' really wuh veh vi fai-tor least. “ra etek bolaya nam-tor aishan wuh nice motherly person.” “oh tal-kam!” wendy leralmin-tor, “gla-tor du, i olau ik nam-tor exactly ra i am.” “ish-veh nam-tor, ish-veh nam-tor, ” au ek' maf-tor; “gla-tor etek ish-veh na' wuh'wak.” “maut muhl, ” she leralmin-tor, “i dungi tor t'nash-veh buhfik. Sarlah svi'udish na' wuh'wak, du naughty kanu; i am sure ish-veh ash'ya nam-tor damp. Heh fa' i shitau du tor sar-tak i ma aishan wak tor shaht wuh var t' cinderella.” svi' au went; i don’t fai-tor uf tra' vesh' tvi-shal na' au, tonk'peh du mokuhlek lerakhovau maut wufik svi' wuh neverland. Heh ik vesh' wuh wuh'rak t' wuh wehk joyous khru au had k' wendy. K' heh k' she k'hy-tor au abru svi' wuh lo'uk sar-tak svi' wuh ha-kel ne' wuh lap, tonk'peh she herself yuk-tor ik mu-yor svi' wuh pi' kelek, heh peter potau glantau s'udish k' drawn shek, na' wuh pirates kupi nam-tor puzhu-tor carousing irak maf heh wuh wolves vesh' fi' wuh prowl. Wuh pi' kelek glazhau ni cosy heh safe svi' wuh mu'khlup'es, k' wuh ugelik ta'hal showing k'fai its blinds, heh wuh vuzh-mev smoking beautifully, heh peter standing fi' klashausu. Po' wuh wak au tevan-tor asleep, heh ein unsteady pu'a had tor qots'noi abru' ish-veh fi' ish-veh yut ha-kel s' wuh orgy. Sovek t' wuh vath sa-kan obstructing wuh pu'a yut na' mu-yor au would ma mischiefed, tonk'peh au aishan tweaked peter’s han heh be' dvun-tor fi'. Chapter vii. Wuh ha-kel ne' wuh solektra veh t' wuh wuh'rak vel peter did thurai gad vesh' tor thon-tor wendy heh john heh michael na' hollow lap. Kik, du vokau, had sneered na' wuh sa-kan na' thinking au bolau wuh lap apiece, tonk'peh nash vesh' ignorance, na' vita ish-veh lap fitted du ish-veh vesh' rihagik tor hal-tor abru heh ne', heh rai dahkuh t' wuh sa-kan vesh' ved wuh ka suk'es. Wuh'wak du fitted, du drew svi' ish-veh esh na' wuh fik, heh ne' du went na' exactly wuh gas'rak threshan, du' tor she-tor du drew svi' heh kal-tor si' alternately, heh ni wriggled abru. Veling, lu du ma tren-tor wuh torai du nam-tor kup tor tor aifa vel rik' thinking t' au, heh nothing mokuhlek nam-tor weht graceful.
