Tonk'peh du veling bolau nunau, heh peter thon-tor du na' ish-veh lap u' carefully u' na' wuh saikhut t' sai-vel: wuh goh natyan hasu ik wuh sai-vel nam-tor tor tor nunau du, du' du ma tor nam-tor tor tor nunau wuh lap. Usually ish-veh nam-tor ovsoh ved easily, u' k' ish-veh sai-vel-tor nuh' wehk ain il nuh' zamu, tonk'peh kuv du nam-tor bumpy svi' awkward shitau il wuh goh la'ka-yehat lap nam-tor wuh shaik shid, peter tor ein vel tor du, heh po' ik du nunau. Wuh'wak du nunau, lo'uk tun bolau nam-tor taken tor hal-tor fi' fitting, heh nash, u' wendy vesh' tor discover tor ish-veh delight, potau wuh bosh skan svi' buhfik nosh. Wendy heh michael fitted ish-veh lap na' wuh wuh'rak ar'kadan, tonk'peh john had tor nam-tor rubitau wuh pi'. Po' wuh zamu gad’ practice au kupi hal-tor abru heh ne' u' gaily u' mashuk svi' wuh muhl. Heh uf ardently au grew tor ashaya ish-veh ha-kel ne' wuh solektra; wa' wendy. Ish-veh consisted t' veh suk tvi-shal, u' ek' kelek dang tor, k' wuh lan-tol svi' if du kupi hil-tor kuv du aitlu tor hal-tor fishing, heh svi' nash lan-tol grew stout taik-luk t' wuh sem-rik-tor kur, if vesh' nam-tor-tor u' stools. Wuh worla lap ar'kada lerash tor tor'ovau svi' wuh centre t' wuh tvi-shal, tonk'peh kanok asal au sawed wuh lap-fek k'fai, volik k' wuh lan-tol. K' theris-masu-wak ish-veh vesh' kwon-hau-ov pa' dahkuh ash'ya pid, heh yi au shitau wuh svep fi-tor ish-veh, wuh bosh thus becoming wuh pasu; u' ak u' au pa'shu maf, au sawed ska' wuh lap-fek va'ashiv, heh thus tra' vesh' weht tvi-shal tor mavau. Tra' vesh' wuh masuk' yon-sha'ti if vesh' svi' siyah sovek krus t' wuh tvi-shal wilat du tun-tor tor ta'hal ish-veh, heh mes' nash wendy sakadau strings, tor t' slah, s' if she suspended ish-veh washing. Wuh sar-tak vesh' ayau tehnat wuh temok k' gad, heh kal-tor ne' na' 6: 30, lu ish-veh boshau nearly ulef wuh tvi-shal; heh ek' wuh sa-kan yuk-tor svi' ish-veh, kaula michael, lying spo' sardines svi' wuh zhai-tukh. Tra' vesh' wuh wonil tor-go tehnat turning pauk abi' veh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh glantokaya, lu ek' da-tor na' wuh'wak. Michael dang ma nam-tor-tor ish-veh isha, tonk'peh wendy would ma wuh kan-bu, heh au vesh' wuh littlest, heh du fai-tor ra kosu nam-tor, heh wuh pen heh wu t' ish-veh nam-tor ik au vesh' geldau abru svi' wuh ki'haf. Ish-veh vesh' rough heh velik, heh ri rikes ra kan-bu bears would ma tor t' wuh underground kelek svi' wuh ka circumstances. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' veh sha'ti svi' wuh temok, rai larger do wuh kushel-kraisek, if vesh' wuh awek ha-shal t' tinker kus-vakh. Ish-veh kupi nam-tor ikap-tor ska' s' wuh shom t' wuh kelek k' wuh tiny curtain, if tink, vi vesh' danik fastidious, kwon-hau-ov potau drawn lu sai-vel-tor il undressing. Rai kosu, however suk, kupi ma had wuh weht exquisite boudoir heh sar-tak-tvi-shal puterish-tor. Wuh ku-san, u' she kwon-hau-ov puvutau ish-veh, vesh' wuh genuine ko-te'kru mab, k' muhd mal; heh she vuhnau wuh bedspreads fupa s' ra savas-blossom vesh' svi' tevun-yonuk. Ish-veh haulat vesh' wuh puss-svi'-kluf, t' if tra' nam-tor i' goh rehkuh, unchipped, fainu tor pu'a dealers; wuh washstand vesh' pie-puhnk heh reversible, wuh tuf t' zish-nef wuh authentic sem-rik-tor wuh sixth, heh wuh la'y heh la'y wuh buhfik (wuh lehkuh-mal) wak-krus t' margery heh kushel. Tra' vesh' wuh chandelier s' tiddlywinks na' wuh glazhau t' wuh vel, tonk'peh veling she lit wuh residence herself. Tink vesh' maut contemptuous t' wuh shom t' wuh kelek, u' indeed vesh' sos'eh inevitable, heh ish-veh tvi-shal, hi vaksurik, glazhau rather conceited, having wuh appearance t' wuh han permanently da-tor abru. I suppose ish-veh vesh' ek' wa' entrancing tor wendy, fai'ei eifa rampagious sa-kan t' ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ni mau tor tor. Really tra' vesh' bosh wehk gad lu, kaula sos'eh k' wuh ash'ai svi' wuh khru, she vesh' worla abru' solektra. Wuh fasan, i mokuhlek var-tor du, potau ish-veh han tor wuh sunil, heh kauk kuv tra' vesh' nothing svi' ish-veh, kauk kuv tra' vesh' rai sunil, she had tor potau watching ik sarlah ish-veh aboil aishan wuh ka. Du worla exactly fai-tor whether tra' would nam-tor wuh yeht yem il aishan wuh tor-dva-tor, ish-veh ek' nerau fi-tor peter’s whim: au kupi yokul, really yokul, kuv ish-veh vesh' krus t' wuh zhagra, tonk'peh au kupi ri stodge aishan tor olau stodgy, if nam-tor ra danik kanu spo' weh-rom do sovek-kitok; wuh thurai buhfik vel hasu tor variben pa' ish-veh. Tor-dva-tor vesh' ni yeht tor ish-veh ik du' wuh yem t' ish-veh du kupi gla-tor ish-veh getting rounder. Veling ish-veh vesh' trying, tonk'peh du veling had tor zahal-tor ish-veh ras-tukh, heh kuv du kupi skan-tor tor ish-veh ik du vesh' getting thal na' ish-veh lap au kal-tor du stodge. Wendy’s favourite wak na' ogan heh darning vesh' po' au had ek' hal-tor tor sar-tak. Yi, u' she sagluvau ish-veh, she had wuh eshan wak na' herself; heh she occupied ish-veh svi' tor uzh vel na' au, heh putting dahtau krus fi' wuh mal-nef, na' au vesh' ek' danik frightfully lerash fi' ish-veh mal-nef. Lu she hayal-tor ne' tor wuh basketful t' ish-veh stockings, kanok timut k' wuh razh svi' ish-veh, she would fling abru ish-veh kar heh sporiben, “oh tal-kam, i am sure i sometimes nah-tor spinsters nam-tor tor nam-tor envied!” ish-veh limuk beamed lu she sporiben nash. Du vokau pa' ish-veh kelek-aushfa wolf. Muhl, ish-veh maut ak discovered ik she had sarlah tor wuh vikuvtra heh ish-veh afer-tor ish-veh si', heh au aishan sahr-tor vi' tik vath’s kar. Po' ik ish-veh zahal-tor ish-veh pa' kanok-wilat. U' wak sai-vel-tor fi' did she nah-tor mau pa' wuh k'diwa mekhlar she had losrak za' ish-veh? Nash nam-tor wuh rihagik deshker, fai'ei ish-veh nam-tor ved impossible tor leralmin uf wak tor sai-vel-tor fi' svi' wuh neverland, wilat ish-veh nam-tor ka'pra k' aikum heh yel, heh tra' nam-tor ek'wak ni wehk weht t' au do fi' wuh mainland. Tonk'peh i am kwes ik wendy did ri really worry pa' ish-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh; she vesh' absolutely confident ik au would kwon-hau-ov potau wuh krani tu'ash na' ish-veh tor hash-tor pla' k', heh nash mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ovsotik ease t' kashek. Ra did ertau ish-veh na' wak vesh' ik john vokau ish-veh mekhlar vaguely goh, u' sutra au had wuh'wak fainu, du' michael vesh' ved willing tor dva-tor ik she vesh' really ish-veh ko-mekh. Aifa vel pahth-tor ish-veh wuh pi', heh nobly anxious tor tor ish-veh gu-vam, she ar'kada tor teslau wuh hinek ha'kiv svi' ish-veh kashkau k' setting au linisaya dun fi' ish-veh, u' spo' u' tor-yehat tor wuh ones she nam-tor-tor tor tor na' shi'oren. Wuh vath sa-kan nahp nash awfully eku'ki, heh insisted fi' hau, heh au tor slates na' themselves, heh hayal-tor pauk wuh pasu, kitaun heh thinking lerash pa' wuh deshkau she had written fi' wuh'ashiv kitau-kov heh be' dvun-tor pauk. Au vesh' wuh danik ordinary deshkau—“ra vesh' wuh kur t' ko-mekh’s bezhun? If vesh' taller, sa-mekh il ko-mekh? Vesh' ko-mekh blonde il brunette? Kilko-srashiv ek' rehkuh deshkau kuv tor-yehat.” “(wuh) kitau wuh essay t' ri lehkuh tor 40 zhit fi' uf i spent t'nash-veh kim-shah holidays, il wuh characters t' sa-mekh heh ko-mekh tcok'at. Goh veh t' aifa tor nam-tor attempted.” il “(1) kethelvau ko-mekh’s abru'teruklar-ru'lut; (2) kethelvau sa-mekh’s abru'teruklar-ru'lut; (3) kethelvau ko-mekh’s party sai-vel; (4) kethelvau wuh kennel heh its inmate.” au vesh' aishan everyday deshkau spo' aifa, heh lu du kupi ri kilko-srashiv au du vesh' var-tor tor tor wuh tuhs; heh ish-veh vesh' really dreadful ra wuh su'etek t' tuhsau kauk john tor. Veling wuh goh sa-kan vi kilko-tor tor kanok deshker vesh' slightly, heh kling kupi ma vesh' weht hopeful t' coming si' wuh'rak, tonk'peh ish-veh kilko-srashiv vesh' perfectly ridiculous, heh au really sasarlah kim-shah: wuh melancholy vel. Peter did ri kuhlau. Na' veh vel au despised ek' ko-mekh kaula wendy, heh na' wuh'ashiv au vesh' wuh goh sa-kan fi' wuh vikuvtra vi kupi neither kitau il spell; ri wuh smallest zhit. Au vesh' abru' ek' ik wihfelau t' vel. K' wuh yut, wuh deshkau vesh' ek' written svi' wuh vesht wis. Ra vesh' wuh kur t' ko-mekh’s bezhun, heh ni fi'. Wendy, gla-tor du, had vesh' forgetting, nuh'. Adventures, veling, u' etek dungau gla-tor, vesh' t' kanok-gadik occurrence; tonk'peh pa' nash wak peter fereik-tor, k' wendy’s gol'nev, wuh uzh zhagra ik sem-tor ish-veh enormously, abi' au suddenly had rai weht eku'ko svi' ish-veh, if, u' du ma vesh' var-tor, vesh' ra kwon-hau-ov pavesh-tor k' ish-veh zhagra. Ish-veh consisted svi' pretending ri ki' adventures, svi' doing wuh wihfelau t' vel john heh michael had vesh' doing ek' ish-veh ha-tor, sitting fi' stools flinging rin'k'n svi' wuh sov, pushing tik vath, going si' na' lates-tor heh coming pla' rik' having pustau ni mau u' wuh grizzly. Tor gla-tor peter doing nothing fi' wuh stool vesh' wuh lo'uk glan; au kupi ri gol'nev looking solemn na' such wak, tor hayal-tor fam dvun seemed tor ish-veh such wuh comic vel tor tor. Au boasted ik au had hal-tor walking na' wuh rom t' ish-veh muhl'es. Na' several yel aifa vesh' wuh danik dunap t' ek' adventures tor ish-veh; heh john heh michael had tor pretend tor nam-tor delighted isha; vathru au would ma skasau au severely. Au k'ashiv went si' sa'awek, heh lu sarlah ish-veh pla' du vesh' worla absolutely ac'ruth whether au had had wuh adventure il ri. Au lau ma yen-tor ish-veh ni completely ik au leralmin-tor nothing pa' ish-veh; heh yi lu du went si' du afer-tor wuh ak'shem; heh, fi' wuh vath el'ru, au lau leralmin wuh lo'uk deal pa' ish-veh, heh wi du kupi ri talal wuh ak'shem. Sometimes sarlah ish-veh ha-kel k' ish-veh patam bandaged, heh yi wendy cooed abru' ish-veh heh bathed ish-veh svi' lukewarm masu, du' au var-tor wuh dazzling var. Tonk'peh she vesh' worla ved sure, du fai-tor. Tra' vesh', however, wehk adventures if she fai-tor tor nam-tor yeht fai'ei she vesh' svi' au herself, heh tra' vesh' fam dvun weht ik vesh' k'puu partly yeht, na' wuh vath sa-kan vesh' svi' au heh leralmin-tor au vesh' wholly yeht. Tor kethelvau au ek' would require wuh dunap u' suk u' wuh eingelsu-latin, latin-eingelsu zhit-dunap, heh wuh danik etek mokuhlek tor nam-tor tor mazhiv-kur-tor veh u' wuh specimen t' wuh bov wadan fi' wuh vikuvtra. Wuh rihag'es nam-tor if veh tor dvel-tor. Dang etek nem-tor wuh achut k' wuh redskins na' slightly gulch? Ish-veh vesh' wuh sanguinary tek'ik, heh wa' eku'ki u' showing veh t' peter’s peculiarities, if vesh' ik svi' wuh svitan t' wuh puk au would suddenly rubah vla. Na' wuh gulch, lu skil vesh' fam dvun svi' wuh vo'ektaya, sometimes leaning nash yut heh sometimes ik, au puvutau si', “i’m redskin tor-gad; ra nam-tor du, tootles?” heh tootles kilko-tor, “redskin; ra nam-tor du, nibs?” heh nibs leralmin-tor, “redskin; ra nam-tor du t'dahsu?” heh ni fi'; heh au vesh' ek' redskins; heh veling nash would ma shahtau wuh puk had ri wuh yeht redskins sem-tor k' peter’s methods, sep-wafikh tor nam-tor pakik sa-kan na' ik wuh'wak, heh ni na' ish-veh au ek' went va'ashiv, weht fiercely do ek'wak. Wuh wehtsuri upshot t' nash adventure vesh'—tonk'peh etek ma ri klopau wi ik nash nam-tor wuh adventure etek nam-tor tor narrate. Sos'eh wuh weh-rom veh would nam-tor wuh mu-yor nashiv-tor k' wuh redskins fi' wuh kelek ne' wuh solektra, lu several t' au terpau svi' wuh hollow lap heh had tor nam-tor seshau si' spo' kem. Il etek lau var-tor uf peter korsau tiger lily’s ha'kiv svi' wuh mermaids’ masutra-muzh, heh ni tor ish-veh ish-veh puk'ai'la. Il etek kupi var-tor t' ik cake wuh pirates pufas-tor ni ik wuh sa-kan lau yokul ish-veh heh perish; heh uf au shitau ish-veh svi' veh cunning gla-tor po' wuh'ashiv; tonk'peh kwon-hau-ov wendy snatched ish-veh s' wuh el'ru t' ish-veh kanu, ni ik svi' wak ish-veh pakik its succulence, heh became u' lerash u' wuh kov, heh vesh' nam-tor-tor u' wuh yon-kliton, heh kik tevan-tor abru' ish-veh svi' wuh gu'gelik. Il suppose etek var-tor t' wuh kushel ik vesh' peter’s t'hylara, wa' t' wuh worla kushel ik torvau svi' wuh lap overhanging wuh masutra-muzh, heh uf wuh ha-kel tevan-tor vi' wuh masu, heh fam dvun wuh kushel hayal-tor fi' ish-veh yu-mur, heh peter mazhiv-kur-tor zek ik she vesh' ri tor nam-tor ertau. Ik nam-tor wuh takov var, heh wuh shaht gluvau uf grateful wuh kushel mokuhlek nam-tor; tonk'peh kuv etek var-tor ish-veh etek bolau isha var-tor wuh bosh adventure t' wuh masutra-muzh, if would t' rivak nam-tor telling dahkuh adventures rather do aishan veh. Wuh shorter adventure, heh ved u' teporilauk, vesh' tinker kus-vakh’s attempt, k' wuh gol'nev t' ein yut pu'a, ki' wuh sleeping wendy zhelesh fi' wuh lo'uk floating mor tor wuh mainland. Fortunately wuh mor mazhiv-kur-tor yut heh wendy woke, thinking ish-veh vesh' wu'sibav-wak, heh swam pla'. Il va'ashiv, etek lau dvel-tor peter’s defiance t' wuh lions, lu au drew wuh da-kuv pauk ish-veh fi' wuh solektra k' wuh kliton heh dared au tor tuhs ish-veh; heh hi au bek-tor na' wadan, k' wuh vath sa-kan heh wendy looking fi' breathlessly s' lap, ri veh t' au dared tor nar-tor ish-veh kali-fi. If t' aifa adventures dungau etek dvel-tor? Wuh buhfik yut dungi nam-tor tor toss na' ish-veh. I ma tossed, heh wuh masutra-muzh has skil-tor. Nash siyah tor veh istaya ik wuh gulch il wuh cake il tink’s mor had skil-tor. Veling i kupi tor ish-veh va'ashiv, heh tor ish-veh buhfik s' rehkuh; however, sos'eh fairest tor terpau tor wuh masutra-muzh. Chapter viii. Wuh mermaids’ masutra-muzh kuv du ikap-tor ish-veh bezhun heh nam-tor wuh kunli veh, du lau gla-tor na' wak wuh shapeless patra t' lovely spoh colours suspended svi' wuh mu'khlup'es; yi kuv du lerakhovau ish-veh bezhun tighter, wuh patra palikau tor nem-tor shid, heh wuh colours shetau ni vivid ik k' wuh'ashiv lerakhovau au bolau hal-tor fi' yon. Tonk'peh aishan fa' au hal-tor fi' yon gla-tor du wuh masutra-muzh. Nash nam-tor wuh nearest du ek'wak prah tor ish-veh fi' wuh mainland, aishan veh heavenly moment; kuv tra' kupi nam-tor dahkuh moments du lau gla-tor wuh surf heh zhu-tor wuh mermaids uralaun. Wuh kanu k'ashiv spent wu belaar gad fi' nash masutra-muzh, mahalan il floating danik t' wuh wak, mavaun wuh mermaid zhagra svi' wuh masu, heh ni forth. Du bolau ri nah-tor s' nash ik wuh mermaids vesh' fi' friendly zhil k' au: fi' wuh contrary, ish-veh vesh' among wendy’s lasting regrets ik ek' wuh wak she vesh' fi' wuh vikuvtra she worla had wuh civil zhit s' veh t' au. Lu she vazgau softly tor wuh rihk t' wuh masutra-muzh she lau gla-tor au k' wuh nosahp, wa' fi' marooners’ kov, wilat au ashau tor bask, combing si' ish-veh isachya svi' wuh kas'el yut ik ved ornaiga ish-veh; il she lau kauk mahal-tor, fi' tiptoe u' ish-veh vesh', tor k'svi wuh ker t' au, tonk'peh yi gla-tor au ish-veh heh taul-tor, probably splashing ish-veh k' ish-veh harr, ri k' kisheya, tonk'peh intentionally. Au skasau ek' wuh sa-kan svi' wuh ka yut, kaula veling peter, vi chatted k' au fi' marooners’ kov k' wuh wadan, heh hayal-tor fi' ish-veh harr lu au prah cheeky. Au mazhiv-kur-tor wendy veh t' ish-veh dref. Wuh danik haunting wak na' if tor gla-tor au nam-tor na' wuh da-tor t' wuh aikum, lu au utter flekh wailing maf-tor; tonk'peh wuh masutra-muzh nam-tor tehvar-bosh na' mortals yi, heh abi' wuh khru t' if etek ma i' tor var-tor, wendy had worla gla-tor wuh masutra-muzh k' moonlight, lehkuh s' pthak, na' veling peter would ma accompanied ish-veh, do fai'ei she had wonil tor-go pa' kanok veh hasu svi' sar-tak k' stehkuh. She vesh' k'ashiv na' wuh masutra-muzh, however, fi' ka'ug'yelik gad po' sov-masu, lu wuh mermaids sarlah abru svi' wehtsuri su'etek tor mavau k' ish-veh duk. Wuh duk t' wehk colours tor svi' igen-kur-kesek masu au skasau u' rin'k'n, hitting au gaily s' veh tor wuh'ashiv k' ish-veh harr, heh trying tor potau au svi' wuh igen-kur-kesek till au thorau. Wuh tehrai nam-tor na' tik shaht t' wuh igen-kur-kesek, heh wuh keepers goh nam-tor kal-tor tor nam-tor-tor ish-veh el'ru. Sometimes wuh dozen t' aifa zhagra dungi nam-tor going fi' svi' wuh masutra-muzh na' wuh wak, heh ish-veh nam-tor ved wuh takov glan. Tonk'peh wuh moment wuh kanu ar'kada tor hau svi' au had tor mavau k' themselves, na' wuh mermaids iyi sasaudau. Nevertheless etek ma skan ik au secretly glantau wuh interlopers, heh vesh' ri abru' taking wuh idea s' au; na' john puragtau wuh uzh yut t' hitting wuh duk, k' wuh patam instead t' wuh el'ru, heh wuh mermaids thanai ish-veh. Nash nam-tor wuh veh ulidar ik john has losrak fi' wuh neverland. Ish-veh bolau isha ma vesh' rather takov tor gla-tor wuh kanu resting fi' wuh kov na' ulef wuh wadan po' ish-veh mid-gad yem. Wendy insisted fi' ish-veh doing nash, heh ish-veh had tor nam-tor wuh yeht shom kauk hi wuh yem vesh' tor-dva-tor. Ni au ti tra' svi' wuh yel, heh ish-veh ak'shem glistened svi' ish-veh, du' she hayal-tor be' au heh glazhau yauluhk. Ish-veh vesh' veh such gad, heh au vesh' ek' fi' marooners’ kov. Wuh kov vesh' ri mau larger do ish-veh lo'uk sar-tak, tonk'peh veling au ek' fai-tor uf ri tor nem-tor abru mau tvi-shal, heh au vesh' dozing, il k'puu lying k' ish-veh bezhun ikap-tor, heh pinching occasionally lu au nahp wendy vesh' ri looking. She vesh' maut toranik, stitching. Du' she og-tor wuh rubah sarlah tor wuh masutra-muzh. Pi' shivers sahr-tor abru' ish-veh, heh wuh yel went maf heh duv vazgau mes' wuh masu, turning ish-veh samu. Wendy kupi rai longer gla-tor tor og-elakh ish-veh og-lum, heh lu she glazhau abru, wuh masutra-muzh ik had kwon-hau-ov hitherto vesh' such wuh laughing shi seemed formidable heh unfriendly. Ish-veh vesh' ri, she fai-tor, ik mu-yor had sarlah, tonk'peh vel u' gu'gelik u' mu-yor had sarlah. Rai, weh-rasahkos do ik. Ish-veh had ri sarlah, tonk'peh ish-veh had satau ik shiver k'fai wuh masutra tor leralmin ik ish-veh vesh' coming. Ra vesh' ish-veh? Tra' crowded fi-tor ish-veh ek' wuh var she had vesh' var-tor t' marooners’ kov, ni puvutau fai'ei ek'rasah khart-lan shitau masusu fi' ish-veh heh trasha au tra' tor mastevau. Au mastevau lu wuh mashen she-tor, na' yi ish-veh nam-tor submerged. Veling she dang ma kastorilau wuh kanu na' wuh'wak; ri goh fai'ei t' wuh ri-fainu ik vesh' stalking na' au, tonk'peh fai'ei ish-veh vesh' rai longer rom na' au tor yuk fi' wuh kov grown chilly. Tonk'peh she vesh' wuh nu'ri ko-mekh heh she did ri fai-tor nash; she nahp du veling bolau terpau tor ish-veh tor-go pa' ulef wuh wadan po' wuh mid-gad yem. Ni, hi pthak vesh' fi-tor ish-veh, heh she longed tor zhu-tor sa spes, she would ri waken au. Kauk lu she puzhu-tor wuh ralash t' nessau fel, hi ish-veh khaf-spol vesh' svi' ish-veh ru'lut, she did ri waken au. She lam-tor abru' au tor kal-tor au ma ish-veh yuk si'. Vesh' ish-veh ri kyi'i t' wendy? Ish-veh vesh' muhl na' eifa sa-kan yi ik tra' vesh' veh ekhlami vi kupi sniff tehvar kauk svi' ish-veh yuk. Peter sprang abru-tor, u' eik kum'i na' wuh'wak u' wuh dog, heh k' veh warning maf au kastorilau wuh vath. Au lam-tor motionless, veh el'ru tor ish-veh kaluk. “pirates!” au maf-tor. Wuh vath sarlah closer tor ish-veh. Wuh flekh abru'teruklar-ru'lut vesh' mavaun pa' ish-veh limuk, heh wendy gla-tor ish-veh heh ak'shem-hutau. Du' ik abru'teruklar-ru'lut vesh' fi' ish-veh limuk kling dared shi'yavekh ish-veh; ek' au kupi tor vesh' tor lamok pok tor obey. Wuh zek sarlah nasik heh incisive. “taul!” tra' vesh' wuh gleam t' mal, heh instantly wuh masutra-muzh seemed deserted. Marooners’ kov lam-tor sa'awek svi' wuh forbidding mashau u' kuv ish-veh vesh' itself marooned. Wuh masu-hali drew nearer. Ish-veh vesh' wuh pirate pi'fel-hali, k' rehkuh khlop svi' ish-veh, smee heh starkey, heh wuh wuh wuh captive, rai vath do tiger lily. Ish-veh el'ru heh mal-nik vesh' tied, heh she fai-tor ra vesh' tor nam-tor ish-veh buk. She vesh' tor nam-tor losrak fi' wuh kov tor perish, wuh shaht tor veh t' ish-veh ne-koshtri weht terrible do tevakh k' yon il torture, na' nam-tor ish-veh ri written svi' wuh dunap t' wuh tribe ik tra' nam-tor rai yut k'fai masu tor wuh kunli hunting-solektra? Wi ish-veh limuk vesh' impassive; she vesh' wuh ko-fu t' wuh chief, she bolau tev-tor u' wuh chief’s ko-fu, ish-veh nam-tor hiyet. Au had kum-tor ish-veh boarding wuh pirate hali k' wuh lipau svi' ish-veh ru'lut. Rai glantau vesh' potau fi' wuh hali, ish-veh hasu kik’s boast ik wuh salan t' ish-veh ahm klashau wuh hali na' wuh mile pa'. I' ish-veh buk would gol'nev tor klashausu ish-veh isha. Veh weht wail would hal-tor wuh pauk svi' ik salan k' mu-yor. Svi' wuh gloom ik au katau k' au wuh dahkuh pirates did ri gla-tor wuh kov till au tevul-tor vi' ish-veh. “luff, du lubber, ” maf-tor wuh irish spes ik vesh' smee’s; “la'’s wuh kov. I', yi, ra etek ma tor tor nam-tor tor abertau wuh redskin fi' tor ish-veh heh trasha ish-veh la' tor mastevau.” ish-veh vesh' wuh ar'kadan t' veh brutal moment tor solektra wuh vaksurik ko-kan fi' wuh kov; she vesh' nuh' yaut tor nufai wuh vain tehnaya. Ved be' wuh kov, tonk'peh s' glan, dahkuh patam vesh' bobbing abru heh ne', peter’s heh wendy’s. Wendy vesh' maf-tor, na' ish-veh vesh' wuh wuh'rak tragedy she had gla-tor. Peter had gla-tor wehk tragedies, tonk'peh au had yen-tor au ek'. Au vesh' lehkuh sorry do wendy na' tiger lily: ish-veh vesh' dahkuh tehnat veh ik resha ish-veh, heh au tvai tor korsau ish-veh. Wuh hagik yut would ma vesh' tor bek-tor abi' wuh pirates had hal-tor, tonk'peh au vesh' worla veh tor dvel-tor wuh hagik yut. Tra' vesh' siyah nothing au kupi ri tor, heh au i' va'amau wuh spes t' kik. “ahoy tra', du lubbers!” au puvutau. Ish-veh vesh' wuh marvellous imitation. “wuh khart-lan!” leralmin-tor wuh pirates, staring na' tik vath svi' ak'wikmun. “au bolau nam-tor mahalan si' tor etek, ” starkey leralmin-tor, lu au had glazhau na' ish-veh svi' vain. “etek nam-tor putting wuh redskin fi' wuh kov, ” smee puvutau si'. “eku ish-veh elik, ” sarlah wuh astonishing kilko-srashiv. “elik!” “ha, tresahk ish-veh tel heh kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor.” “tonk'peh, khart-lan—” “na' wuh'wak, d’ye zhu-tor, ” maf-tor peter, “il i’ll taul t'nash-veh kik svi' du.” “nash nam-tor queer!” smee hushau. “weh-rom tor ra wuh khart-lan zek, ” leralmin-tor starkey nervously. “ay, ay, ” smee leralmin-tor, heh au tresahk tiger lily’s elakh. Na' wuh'wak spo' wuh eel she slid svi' starkey’s mal vi' wuh masu. Veling wendy vesh' maut elated abru' peter’s cleverness; tonk'peh she fai-tor ik au would nam-tor elated isha heh maut kesik kushel heh thus svik-tor himself, ni na' wuh'wak ish-veh el'ru went si' tor wein ish-veh ru'lut. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' stayed kauk svi' wuh bae'cok, na' “masu-hali ahoy!” rang abru' wuh masutra-muzh svi' kik’s spes, heh nash wak ish-veh vesh' ri peter vi had spoken. Peter lau ma vesh' pa' tor kushel, tonk'peh ish-veh limuk puckered svi' wuh whistle t' ak'wikmun instead. “masu-hali ahoy!” va'ashiv sarlah wuh spes. I' wendy ken-tor. Wuh yeht kik vesh' isha svi' wuh masu. Au vesh' mahalan tor wuh masu-hali, heh u' ish-veh sasu gluvau wuh ta'hal tor kakhartausu ish-veh au had ak pulau au. Svi' wuh ta'hal t' wuh makh-yonet wendy gla-tor ish-veh kik grip wuh masu-hali’s vla; gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh ek'rasah swarthy limuk u' au she-tor dripping s' wuh masu, heh, quaking, she would ma tishau tor mahal-tor maf, tonk'peh peter would ri budge. Au vesh' tingling k' ha'kiv heh isha fik-ras k' conceit. “am i ri wuh wonder, oh, i am wuh wonder!” au zhal-tor tor ish-veh, heh hi she nahp ni isha, she vesh' really glad na' wuh sake t' ish-veh reputation ik kling puzhu-tor ish-veh kaula herself. Au signed tor ish-veh tor shroi. Wuh dahkuh pirates vesh' maut curious tor fai-tor ra had katau ish-veh khart-lan tor au, tonk'peh au hayal-tor k' ish-veh patam fi' ish-veh kik svi' wuh shul t' profound melancholy. “khart-lan, nam-tor ek' muhl?” au ya'akash timidly, tonk'peh au kilko-tor k' wuh hollow naya. “au spes-tevan, ” leralmin-tor smee. “au spes-tevan va'ashiv, ” leralmin-tor starkey. “heh wi wuh wuh wak au spes-tevan, ” leralmin-tor smee. Yi na' kim-shah au stariben passionately. “wuh zhagra’s abru, ” au maf-tor, “eifa sa-kan ma afer-tor wuh ko-mekh.” affrighted hi she vesh', wendy puv-tor k' pride. “o ek'rasah gad!” maf-tor starkey. “ra’s wuh ko-mekh?” ya'akash wuh ignorant smee. Wendy vesh' ni kolaya ik she sporiben. “au doesn’t fai-tor!” heh kwon-hau-ov po' nash she olau ik kuv du kupi ma wuh kelek-aushfa pirate smee would nam-tor ish-veh veh. Peter seshau ish-veh ne'rak wuh masu, na' kik had palikau abru, maf-tor, “ra vesh' ik?” “i puzhu-tor nothing, ” leralmin-tor starkey, raising wuh makh-yonet abru' wuh mashau, heh u' wuh pirates glazhau gla-tor au wuh flekh glan. Ish-veh vesh' wuh ha-kel i ma var-tor du t', floating fi' wuh masutra-muzh, heh wuh worla kushel vesh' sitting fi' ish-veh. “gla-tor, ” leralmin-tor kik svi' kilko-srashiv tor smee’s deshker, “ik nam-tor wuh ko-mekh. Ra wuh tupa! Wuh ha-kel bolau ma tevan-tor vi' wuh masu, tonk'peh would wuh ko-mekh eshikh ish-veh yu-mur? Rai.” tra' vesh' wuh shaya svi' ish-veh spes, u' kuv na' wuh moment au recalled innocent gad lu—tonk'peh au brushed maf nash kobat'es k' ish-veh kik. Smee, mau impressed, gazed na' wuh kushel u' wuh ha-kel vesh' borne vesht, tonk'peh wuh weht suspicious starkey leralmin-tor, “kuv she nam-tor wuh ko-mekh, sos'eh she nam-tor hanging pa' la' tor gol'nev peter.” kik winced. “ay, ” au leralmin-tor, “ik nam-tor wuh pthak ik haunts me.” au vesh' kastorilau s' nash dejection k' smee’s nayik spes. “khart-lan, ” leralmin-tor smee, “kupi etek ri kidnap aifa sa-kan’ ko-mekh heh tor ish-veh etwel ko-mekh?” “ish-veh nam-tor wuh princely scheme, ” maf-tor kik, heh na' wuh'wak ish-veh nem-tor practical shid svi' ish-veh lo'uk shi'nahp. “etek dungi seize wuh kanu heh lesh au tor wuh masu-hali: wuh sa-kan etek dungi tor lates wuh plank, heh wendy dungau nam-tor etwel ko-mekh.” va'ashiv wendy forgot herself. “worla!” she maf-tor, heh bobbed. “ra vesh' ik?” tonk'peh au kupi gla-tor nothing. Au nahp ish-veh bolau ma vesh' wuh mor svi' wuh salan. “tor du sep-wafikh, t'nash-veh bullies?” ya'akash kik. “tra' nam-tor t'nash-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh, ” au fi' leralmin-tor. “heh tra' nam-tor t'nash-veh kik. Swear.” au ek' swore. K' nash wak au vesh' fi' wuh kov, heh suddenly kik vokau tiger lily. “wilat nam-tor wuh redskin?” au halishau abruptly. Au had wuh playful humour na' moments, heh au nahp nash vesh' veh t' wuh moments. “ik nam-tor ek' gas'rak, khart-lan, ” smee kilko-tor complacently; “etek kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor.” “kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor!” maf-tor kik. “’twas ish-veh sha' zek, ” wuh bo’yel faltered. “du puvutau abru' wuh masu tor etek tor kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, ” leralmin-tor starkey. “brimstone heh thel'a-zalu-masu, ” thundered kik, “ra cozening nam-tor going fi' la'!” ish-veh limuk had hal-tor nesh-kur k' reshan, tonk'peh gla-tor ish-veh ik au pudva-tor ish-veh zhit, heh au vesh' startled. “lads, ” au leralmin-tor, shaking wuh pi', “i mazhiv-kur-tor rai such zek.” “ish-veh nam-tor be' dvun-tor queer, ” smee leralmin-tor, heh au ek' fidgeted uncomfortably. Kik ashenau ish-veh spes, tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh quiver svi' ish-veh. “tam'a ik haunts nash gu'gelik masutra-muzh tor-mu-yor, ” au maf-tor, “dost zhu-tor me?” veling peter dang ma potau hizhuk, tonk'peh veling au did ri. Au iyi kilko-tor svi' kik’s spes: “odds, bobs, mah-vel heh el'abrashayek, i zhu-tor du.” svi' ik supreme moment kik did ri blanch, kauk na' wuh masu-eshanek, tonk'peh smee heh starkey clung tor tik vath svi' vash. “vi nam-tor du, ri-fainusu? Stariben!” kik halishau. “i am james kik, ” kilko-tor wuh spes, “khart-lan t' wuh _jolly roger_.” “du nam-tor ri; du nam-tor ri, ” kik maf-tor hoarsely. “brimstone heh thel'a-zalu-masu, ” wuh spes retorted, “leralmin ik va'ashiv, heh i’ll vishizhau masu-vohrayek svi' du.” kik ar'kada wuh weht ingratiating manner. “kuv du nam-tor kik, ” au leralmin-tor siyah humbly, “sarlah var-tor me, vi am i?” “wuh codfish, ” kilko-tor wuh spes, “goh wuh codfish.” “wuh codfish!” kik echoed blankly, heh ish-veh vesh' yi, tonk'peh ri till yi, ik ish-veh yaut tam'a shau. Gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh sasu bes-tor pla' s' ish-veh. “ma etek vesh' captained ek' nash wak k' wuh codfish!” au muttered. “ish-veh nam-tor lowering tor etwel pride.” au vesh' ish-veh dogs snapping na' ish-veh, tonk'peh, tragic khlop hi au had shetau, au scarcely heeded au. Tehnat such pthak-bosh evidence ish-veh vesh' ri ish-veh dva svi' ish-veh ik au bolau, ish-veh vesh' ish-veh sha'. Au olau ish-veh shayuf slipping s' ish-veh. “don’t eshikh me, bully, ” au zhal-tor hoarsely tor ish-veh. Svi' ish-veh gu'gelik malat tra' vesh' wuh esta t' wuh kogavik, u' svi' ek' wuh lo'uk pirates, heh ish-veh sometimes mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh intuitions. Suddenly au ar'kada wuh guessing zhagra. “kik, ” au puvutau, “ma du wuh'ashiv spes?” i' peter kupi worla tehnau wuh zhagra, heh au kilko-tor blithely svi' ish-veh sha' spes, “i ma.” “heh wuh'ashiv ahm?” “ay, ay.” “sazh?” ya'akash kik. “rai.” “ek'tukh?” “rai.” “aushfa?” “ha.” “sasu?” “rai!” nash kilko-srashiv rang si' scornfully. “sa-kan?” “ha.” “ordinary sa-kan?” “rai!” “wonderful sa-kan?” tor wendy’s kusut wuh kilko-srashiv ik rang si' nash wak vesh' “ha.” “nam-tor du svi' england?” “rai.” “nam-tor du la'?” “ha.” kik vesh' completely puzzled. “du ya'akash ish-veh ein deshkau, ” au leralmin-tor tor wuh vath, psethau ish-veh damp meix'tem. Smee haul-tor. “i mokuhlek’t nah-tor t' wuh vel, ” au leralmin-tor regretfully. “mokuhlek’t guess, mokuhlek’t guess!” crowed peter. “tor du mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru?” veling svi' ish-veh pride au vesh' carrying wuh zhagra nuh' irak, heh wuh miscreants gla-tor ish-veh pavesh. “ha, ha, ” au kilko-tor eagerly. “muhl, yi, ” au maf-tor, “i am peter sunil.” sunil! Svi' wuh moment kik vesh' himself va'ashiv, heh smee heh starkey vesh' ish-veh faithful henchmen. “i' etek ma ish-veh, ” kik saul-tor. “vi' wuh masu, smee. Starkey, kashek wuh masu-hali. Nem-tor ish-veh tevik il alive!” au leaped u' au stariben, heh simultaneously sarlah wuh sa-ka-ashausu spes t' peter. “nam-tor du pok, sa-kan?” “ay, ay, ” s' vuhnauk krus t' wuh masutra-muzh. “yi lam vi' wuh pirates.” wuh puk vesh' pen heh nasik. Wuh'rak tor bes-tor khaf vesh' john, vi gallantly sasu-tor vi' wuh masu-hali heh meskarau starkey. Tra' vesh' kei struggle, svi' if wuh cutlass vesh' torn s' wuh pirate’s ruskaraya. Au wriggled overboard heh john leapt po' ish-veh. Wuh pi'fel-hali marau maf. La' heh tra' wuh patam bobbed abru svi' wuh masu, heh tra' vesh' wuh kahai t' pishek zahal-tor k' wuh maf il wuh whoop. Svi' wuh confusion ein kwul-tor na' ish-veh sha' vla. Wuh corkscrew t' smee prah tootles svi' wuh fourth bak, tonk'peh au vesh' himself pinked svi' da-tor k' curly. Weh-irak s' wuh kov starkey vesh' pressing slightly heh wuh t'dahsu lerash. Wilat ek' nash wak vesh' peter? Au vesh' seeking bigger zhagra. Wuh vath vesh' ek' kyi'i sa-kan, heh au bolau ri nam-tor tenah na' backing s' wuh pirate khart-lan. Ish-veh shek-tukh spahk tor wuh da-kuv t' tevik masu pauk ish-veh, s' if au sasahr-tor spo' affrighted aluk. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' veh vi did ri pthak ish-veh: tra' vesh' veh dator tor svi-tor ik da-kuv. Strangely, ish-veh vesh' ri svi' wuh masu ik au ragel-tor. Kik she-tor tor wuh kov tor esh-tor, heh na' wuh ka moment peter scaled ish-veh fi' wuh mesyutik vla. Wuh kov vesh' slippery u' wuh rin'k'n, heh au had tor ukrau rather do qots'noi. Neither fai-tor ik wuh vath vesh' coming. Tik olaya na' wuh grip ragel-tor wuh vath’s kar: svi' ak'wikmun au ashenau ish-veh patam; ish-veh limuk vesh' siyah touching; ni au ragel-tor. Ein t' wuh greatest heroes ma confessed ik aishan fa' au tevan-tor tor au had wuh sinking. Had ish-veh vesh' ni k' peter na' ik moment i would nafai-tor ish-veh. Po' ek', au vesh' wuh goh sasu ik wuh masutra-fas-tor had ptha. Tonk'peh peter had rai sinking, au had veh olaya goh, gladness; heh au gnashed ish-veh takov zud k' mak. Sahris u' nahp au snatched wuh lipau s' kik’s san-zhel heh vesh' pa' tor yetur ish-veh ha-kel, lu gla-tor ish-veh ik au vesh' higher abru wuh kov do ish-veh hahf. Ish-veh would ri ma vesh' fighting rom. Au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh pirate wuh el'ru tor gol'nev ish-veh abru. Ish-veh vesh' yi ik kik zeshau ish-veh. Ri wuh kusut t' nash tonk'peh its unfairness vesh' ra dazed peter. Ish-veh tor ish-veh ved helpless. Au kupi goh nantaya, horrified. Kanok kan nam-tor dau thus wuh wuh'rak wak au nam-tor skasau unfairly. Ek' au nah-tor au has wuh gas'rak tor lu sarlah ish-veh tor du tor nam-tor ish-veh nam-tor fairness. Po' du ma vesh' unfair tor ish-veh au dungi ashaya du va'ashiv, tonk'peh dungi worla afterwards nam-tor ved wuh ka sa-kan. Kling ek'wak prah abru' wuh wuh'rak unfairness; kling kaula peter. Au k'ashiv ragel-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh au kwon-hau-ov forgot ish-veh. I suppose ik vesh' wuh yeht natyan svi' ish-veh heh ek' wuh shom. Ni lu au ragel-tor ish-veh i' ish-veh vesh' spo' wuh wuh'rak wak; heh au kupi aishan nantaya, helpless. Dah'wak wuh shek-tukh el'ru spahk ish-veh. Wuh zamu moments afterwards wuh vath sa-kan gla-tor kik svi' wuh masu striking wildly na' wuh hali; rai elation fi' wuh pestilent limuk i', goh wan-kur pthak, na' wuh crocodile vesh' svi' dogged pursuit t' ish-veh. Fi' ordinary occasions wuh sa-kan would ma mahal-tor alongside cheering; tonk'peh i' au vesh' uneasy, na' au had pakik fi' peter heh wendy, heh vesh' scouring wuh masutra-muzh na' au, calling au k' ahm. Au afer-tor wuh pi'fel-hali heh went ha-kel svi' ish-veh, shouting “peter, wendy” u' au went, tonk'peh rai kilko-srashiv sarlah korsau mocking laughter s' wuh mermaids. “au bolau nam-tor mahalan pla' il hashan, ” wuh sa-kan concluded. Au vesh' ri maut anxious, fai'ei au had such odva svi' peter. Au chuckled, boylike, fai'ei au would nam-tor tab-ma na' sar-tak; heh ish-veh vesh' ek' ko-mekh wendy’s lafot! Lu ish-veh spes tev-tor maf tra' sarlah samu silence abru' wuh masutra-muzh, heh yi wuh kobat maf. “gol'nev, gol'nev!” dahkuh pi' khlop vesh' beating tehnat wuh kov; wuh ko-kan had fainted heh ti fi' wuh sa-kan’s kar. K' wuh kim-shah urgam peter seshau ish-veh abru wuh kov heh yi ti ne' be' ish-veh. Kauk u' au isha fainted gla-tor ish-veh ik wuh masu vesh' rising. Au fai-tor ik au would ak nam-tor mastevau, tonk'peh au kupi tor rai weht. U' au ti vla k' vla wuh mermaid kum-tor wendy k' wuh ash'ya, heh began pulling ish-veh softly vi' wuh masu. Peter, olaya ish-veh trel s' ish-veh, woke k' wuh palikaya, heh vesh' aishan svi' wak tor bes-tor ish-veh pla'. Tonk'peh au had tor var-tor ish-veh wuh yeht'es. “etek nam-tor fi' wuh kov, wendy, ” au leralmin-tor, “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor growing smaller. Ak wuh masu dungi nam-tor abru' ish-veh.” she did ri ken-tor kauk i'. “etek bolau hal-tor, ” she leralmin-tor, siyah brightly. “ha, ” au kilko-tor faintly. “dungau etek mahal-tor il hash-tor, peter?” au had tor var-tor ish-veh. “tor du nah-tor du kupi mahal-tor il hash-tor u' irak u' wuh vikuvtra, wendy, rik' t'nash-veh gol'nev?” she had tor nafai-tor ik she vesh' nuh' zungor. Au nau. “ra nam-tor ish-veh?” she ya'akash, anxious pa' ish-veh na' wuh'wak. “i mokuhlek’t gol'nev du, wendy. Kik wounded me. I mokuhlek neither hash-tor il mahal-tor.” “tor du tvai etek dungau fi' nam-tor mastevau?” “glazhau uf wuh masu nam-tor rising.” au shitau ish-veh el'ru abru' ish-veh bezhun tor ikap-tor si' wuh glan. Au nahp au would ak nam-tor rai weht. U' au hayal-tor thus vel brushed tehnat peter u' ta'hal u' wuh shok, heh stayed tra', u' kuv taran timidly, “mokuhlek i nam-tor t' sovek nam-tor-tor?” ish-veh vesh' wuh harr t' wuh kite, if michael had tor ein gad fa'. Ish-veh had torn itself s' ish-veh el'ru heh markau maf. “michael’s kite, ” peter leralmin-tor rik' eku'ko, tonk'peh thurai moment au had seized wuh harr, heh vesh' pulling wuh kite na' ish-veh. “ish-veh abertau michael ska' wuh solektra, ” au maf-tor; “po dang ish-veh ri lesh du?” “fi' t' etek!” “ish-veh mokuhlek’t abertau dahkuh; michael heh curly ar'kada.” “kal-tor etek bes-tor lots, ” wendy leralmin-tor bravely. “heh du wuh t'sai; worla.” already au had tied wuh harr pauk ish-veh. She clung tor ish-veh; she klee'fah tor hal-tor rik' ish-veh; tonk'peh k' wuh “rom-bye, wendy, ” au kwitau ish-veh s' wuh kov; heh svi' wuh zamu minutes she vesh' borne s' ish-veh glan. Peter vesh' sa'awek fi' wuh masutra-muzh. Wuh kov vesh' maut pi' i'; ak ish-veh would nam-tor submerged. Spoh ha'zehl t' ta'hal tiptoed mes' wuh mashau; heh k' heh k' tra' vesh' tor nam-tor puzhu-tor wuh ralash na' wuh'wak wuh danik musical heh wuh danik melancholy svi' wuh panu: wuh mermaids calling tor wuh aikum. Peter vesh' ri ved spo' vath sa-kan; tonk'peh au vesh' kwes na' kim-shah. Wuh tremour sahr-tor k'fai ish-veh, spo' wuh ak'shem-hutau be' dvun-tor abru' wuh masutra; tonk'peh fi' wuh masutra veh ak'shem-hutau zahal-tor wuh'ashiv till tra' nam-tor hundreds t' au, heh peter olau aishan wuh veh. Thurai moment au vesh' standing abru-tor fi' wuh kov va'ashiv, k' ik abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi' ish-veh limuk heh wuh vluhn beating k'svi ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' taran, “tor tev-tor dungi nam-tor wuh awfully suk' adventure.” chapter ix. Wuh worla kushel wuh kim-shah ralash peter puzhu-tor fa' au vesh' ved sa'awek vesh' wuh mermaids retiring veh k' veh tor ish-veh bedchambers ne' wuh masutra. Au vesh' nuh' irak maf tor zhu-tor ish-veh svep ikap-tor; tonk'peh kanok svep svi' wuh coral tauk wilat au ha-tor mokov wuh tiny kus-vakh lu ish-veh tu'ash il ikap-tor (u' svi' ek' wuh nicest kelek fi' wuh mainland), heh au puzhu-tor wuh kus-vakh. Steadily wuh mashau she-tor till au vesh' nibbling na' ish-veh ash'ya; heh tor be' dvun wuh wak abi' au tor ish-veh kim-shah gulp, au glantau wuh goh vel fi' wuh masutra-muzh. Au nahp ish-veh vesh' wuh krus t' floating dun, sos'eh krus t' wuh kite, heh wondered idly uf wu ish-veh would nem-tor tor maraya ashore. Presently au pubeglanau u' wuh shaik vel ik ish-veh vesh' undoubtedly si' fi-tor wuh masutra-muzh k' ein definite lof, na' ish-veh vesh' fighting wuh mashen, heh sometimes winning; heh lu ish-veh skil-tor, peter, kwon-hau-ov sympathetic tor wuh weaker vla, kupi ri gol'nev clapping; ish-veh vesh' such wuh gallant krus t' dun. Ish-veh vesh' ri really wuh krus t' dun; ish-veh vesh' wuh worla kushel, tor desperate urgam tor pulau peter fi' wuh ha-kel. K' working ish-veh rala, svi' wuh yut she had oren-tor opi' wuh ha-kel tevan-tor vi' wuh masu, she vesh' kup tor ein sadvun tor kakhartausu ish-veh flekh hali, tonk'peh k' wuh wak peter naglanshau ish-veh she vesh' maut saguhsh-tor. She had sarlah tor korsau ish-veh, tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ish-veh ha-kel, hi tra' vesh' yu-mur svi' ish-veh. I rather wonder na' wuh kushel, na' hi au had vesh' nice tor ish-veh, au had isha sometimes tormented ish-veh. I mokuhlek suppose goh ik, spo' mrs. Ashal-veh heh wuh shom t' au, she vesh' klimtau fai'ei au had ek' ish-veh wuh'rak zud. She shoret ish-veh ra she had sarlah na', heh au shoret ish-veh ra she vesh' doing tra'; tonk'peh veling neither t' au ken-tor wuh vath’s gen-lis. Svi' fanciful var sutra mokuhlek variben tor wuh kushel freely, heh i istaya na' wuh moment i kupi pretend ik nash vesh' such wuh var, heh leralmin ik peter kilko-tor intelligently tor wuh worla kushel; tonk'peh yeht'es nam-tor buhfik, heh i aitlun tor var-tor du goh ra really pavesh-tor. Muhl, ri goh kupi au ri ken-tor tik vath, tonk'peh au forgot ish-veh manners. “i—aitlun—du—tor—prah—vi'—wuh—ha-kel, ” wuh kushel puvutau, speaking u' slowly heh distinctly u' tor-yehat, “heh—yi—du—mokuhlek—maraya—ashore, tonk'peh—i—am—nuh'—zungor—tor—katau—ish-veh—sovek—nearer—ni—du—bolau—ar'kadan tor—mahal-tor—tor—ish-veh.” “ra nam-tor du quacking pa'?” peter kilko-tor. “po don’t du kal-tor wuh ha-kel maraya u' tsuri?” “i—aitlun—du—” wuh kushel leralmin-tor, heh ashiv-tor ish-veh ek' abru'. Yi peter ar'kada vohris heh natya. “ra—nam-tor—du—quacking—pa'?” heh ni fi'. Wuh worla kushel became ornaiga; au ma maut pen tempers. “du dunderheaded pi' jay!” she shei, “po don’t du tor u' i var-tor du?” peter olau ik she vesh' calling ish-veh ahm, heh na' wuh venture au retorted hotly: “ni nam-tor du!” yi rather curiously au fi' snapped si' wuh ka remark: “ikap'uh t'du ru'lut!” “ikap'uh t'du ru'lut!” nevertheless wuh kushel vesh' satalau tor korsau ish-veh kuv she kupi, heh k' veh kim-shah mighty urgam she pudatau wuh ha-kel tehnat wuh kov. Yi abru she flew; deserting ish-veh yu-mur, ni u' tor tor ish-veh meaning pa'shik. Yi na' kim-shah au ken-tor, heh clutched wuh ha-kel heh pral-tor ish-veh itaren tor wuh kushel u' she nuv-tor overhead. Ish-veh vesh' ri tor poprah ish-veh itaren, however, ik she geldau tra' svi' wuh igen; ish-veh vesh' ri kauk tor glantau ish-veh prah vi' wuh ha-kel; ish-veh vesh' tor gla-tor ra au did k' ish-veh yu-mur. Tra' vesh' dahkuh suk wan-kur yu-mur, heh peter abertau au abru heh haul-tor. Wuh kushel wein-tor ish-veh limuk k' ish-veh rala, ni u' ri tor gla-tor wuh kim-shah t' au; tonk'peh she kupi ri gol'nev peeping svi' wuh kan. I yen-tor whether i ma var-tor du ik tra' vesh' wuh stave fi' wuh kov, driven vi' ish-veh k' ein buccaneers t' wu ago tor ulidar wuh shi t' visolektau treasure. Wuh kanu had discovered wuh glittering hoard, heh lu svi' wuh mischievous mood nam-tor-tor tor fling mashulayek t' moidores, lerash-khush, pearls heh krus t' ohkuh tor wuh gulls, vi pounced fi-tor au na' yem-tukh, heh yi flew maf, raging na' wuh scurvy trick ik had vesh' mavau fi-tor au. Wuh stave vesh' fam dvun tra', heh fi' ish-veh starkey had geldau ish-veh taik, wuh glu tarpaulin, masu-fenk, k' wuh sax'ksei brim. Peter shitau wuh yu-mur vi' nash taik heh eku ish-veh fi' wuh masutra-muzh. Ish-veh markau beautifully. Wuh worla kushel gla-tor na' wuh'wak ra au vesh' abru tor, heh shei ish-veh admiration t' ish-veh; heh, alas, peter crowed ish-veh agreement k' ish-veh. Yi au prah vi' wuh ha-kel, reared wuh stave svi' ish-veh u' wuh mashalo-thalv-lap, heh geldau abru ish-veh sav'el na' wuh mashalo-thalv. Na' wuh ka moment wuh kushel nuv-tor ne' fi-tor wuh taik heh wuh'wak weht hayal-tor snugly fi' ish-veh yu-mur. She marau svi' veh kharat, heh au vesh' borne ska' svi' wuh'ashiv, fi' cheering. Veling lu peter landed au beached ish-veh barque svi' wuh shi wilat wuh kushel would easily talal ish-veh; tonk'peh wuh taik vesh' such wuh lo'uk navun ik she abandoned wuh ha-kel. Ish-veh marau pa' till ish-veh went tor krus, heh k'ashiv starkey sarlah tor wuh gef t' wuh masutra-muzh, heh k' wehk sfith(-) feelings glantau wuh kushel sitting fi' ish-veh taik. U' etek dungau ri gla-tor ish-veh va'ashiv, ish-veh lau nam-tor don mentioning la' ik ek' worla kushel i' torvau svi' ik shid t' ha-kel, k' wuh sax'ksei brim fi' if wuh youngsters nem-tor wuh airing. Lo'uk vesh' wuh rejoicings lu peter pulau wuh ha-kel ne' wuh solektra siyah u' ak u' wendy, vi had vesh' lesh hither heh thither k' wuh kite. Kanok sa-kan had adventures tor var-tor; tonk'peh sos'eh wuh biggest adventure t' ek' vesh' ik au vesh' several wadan tab-ma na' sar-tak. Nash ni visovau au ik au did vuhnauk dodgy vel tor prah staying abru fam dvun longer, such u' demanding zhumav; tonk'peh wendy, hi glorying svi' having au ek' ha-kel va'ashiv safe heh ralash, vesh' scandalised k' wuh lateness t' wuh wadan, heh maf-tor, “tor sar-tak, tor sar-tak, ” svi' wuh spes ik had tor nam-tor obeyed. Thurai gad, however, she vesh' awfully sival, heh mazhiv-kur-tor si' zhumav tor kanok veh, heh au mavau till sar-tak-wak na' limping pa' heh carrying ish-veh kar svi' slings. Chapter x. Wuh kunli ha-kel veh yauluhk result t' wuh achut fi' wuh masutra-muzh vesh' ik ish-veh tor wuh redskins ish-veh t'hylara. Peter had korsau tiger lily s' wuh dreadful buk, heh i' tra' vesh' nothing she heh ish-veh braves would ri tor na' ish-veh. Ek' mu-yor au hayal-tor abru', keeping paluntunau wuh ha-kel ne' wuh solektra heh awaiting wuh suk' nashiv-tor k' wuh pirates if obviously kupi ri nam-tor mau longer vohtau. Kauk k' gad au geldau pa', smoking wuh mev t' sochya, heh looking siyah u' kuv au aitlu tit-bits tor yokul. Au puvutau peter wuh lo'uk wan-kur sa-mekh, prostrating themselves fa' ish-veh; heh au tishau nash tremendously, ni ik ish-veh vesh' ri really rom na' ish-veh. “wuh lo'uk wan-kur sa-mekh, ” au would leralmin tor au svi' wuh maut lordly manner, u' au grovelled na' ish-veh ash'ya, “nam-tor glad tor gla-tor wuh piccaninny warriors protecting ish-veh wigwam s' wuh pirates.” “me tiger lily, ” ik lovely creature would kilko. “peter sunil korsau me, me ish-veh velly nice t'hy'la. Me rai kal-tor pirates dash-tor ish-veh.” she vesh' irak nuh' takov tor cringe svi' nash yut, tonk'peh peter nahp ish-veh ish-veh due, heh au would kilko-srashiv condescendingly, “ish-veh nam-tor rom. Peter sunil has spoken.” kwon-hau-ov lu au leralmin-tor, “peter sunil has spoken, ” ish-veh tvai ik au bolau i' ikap'uh t'du ru'lut, heh au nar-tor ish-veh humbly svi' ik tam'a; tonk'peh au vesh' k' rai tvai ni respectful tor wuh vath sa-kan, ik au glazhau fi-tor u' aishan ordinary braves. Au leralmin-tor “uf-tor?” tor au, heh vel spo' ik; heh ra annoyed wuh sa-kan vesh' ik peter seemed tor nah-tor nash ek' gas'rak. Secretly wendy sympathised k' au wuh pi', tonk'peh she vesh' irak nuh' fonn wuh housewife tor shroi tor sovek complaints tehnat sa-mekh. “sa-mekh fai-tor buhfik, ” she kwon-hau-ov leralmin-tor, whatever ish-veh awek opinion bolau nam-tor. Ish-veh awek opinion vesh' ik wuh redskins dang ri vutau ish-veh wuh squaw. Etek ma i' pulau wuh khru ik vesh' tor nam-tor fainu ekhlami u' wuh mu-yor t' mu-yor, fai'ei t' its adventures heh ish-veh upshot. Wuh gad, u' kuv quietly hohnaya its nekwitau, had vesh' siyah uneventful, heh i' wuh redskins svi' ish-veh yuk-sai vesh' na' ish-veh lehk abru', du', ne', wuh kanu vesh' having ish-veh khru yem; ek' kaula peter, vi had hal-tor si' tor prah wuh wak. Wuh yut du prah wuh wak fi' wuh vikuvtra vesh' tor talal wuh crocodile, heh yi stay be' ish-veh till wuh wak-vel kwul-tor. Wuh yem pavesh-tor tor nam-tor wuh tor-dva-tor theris-masu, heh au hayal-tor pa' wuh dohn, guzzling svi' ish-veh greed; heh really, ra k' ish-veh chatter heh recriminations, wuh ralash, u' wendy leralmin-tor, vesh' positively deafening. Tor nam-tor sure, she did ri kashek ralash, tonk'peh she veling would ri ma au grabbing vel, heh yi excusing themselves k' taran ik tootles had kwitau ish-veh kar-nef. Tra' vesh' wuh teslau tor-go ik au bolau worla kwul pla' na' yem, tonk'peh dang dzhinau wuh tukh t' dispute tor wendy k' raising wuh gas'rak kar politely heh taran, “i complain t' ni-heh-ni; ” tonk'peh ra usually pavesh-tor vesh' ik au forgot tor tor nash il did ish-veh nuh' mau. “silence, ” maf-tor wendy lu na' wuh twentieth wak she had var-tor au ik au vesh' ri ek' tor stariben na' wuh'wak. “nam-tor ish-veh mug herbosh, slightly ashal-veh?” “ri ved herbosh, mummy, ” slightly leralmin-tor, po' looking vi' wuh glenonik mug. “au hasn’t kauk palikau tor mon ish-veh thas, ” nibs interposed. Nash vesh' telling, heh slightly seized ish-veh pavesh. “i complain t' nibs, ” au maf-tor promptly. John, however, had meskarau abru ish-veh el'ru wuh'rak. “muhl, john?” “sos hayal-tor svi' peter’s ku-san, u' au nam-tor ri la'?” “hayal-tor svi' sa-mekh’s ku-san, john!” wendy vesh' scandalised. “certainly ri.” “au nam-tor ri really etwel sa-mekh, ” john kilko-tor. “au didn’t kauk fai-tor uf wuh sa-mekh tor till i gluvau ish-veh.” nash vesh' grumbling. “etek complain t' john, ” maf-tor wuh t'dahsu. Tootles meskarau abru ish-veh el'ru. Au vesh' ni mau wuh humblest t' au, indeed au vesh' wuh goh humble veh, ik wendy vesh' specially gentle k' ish-veh. “i don’t suppose, ” tootles leralmin-tor diffidently, “ik i kupi nam-tor sa-mekh.” “rai, tootles.” wuh'wak tootles began, if vesh' ri maut k'ashiv, au had wuh silly yut t' going fi'. “u' i mokuhlek’t nam-tor sa-mekh, ” au leralmin-tor heavily, “i don’t suppose, michael, du would kal-tor me nam-tor kan-bu?” “rai, i skil-tor’t, ” michael rapped si'. Au vesh' already svi' ish-veh ki'haf. “u' i mokuhlek’t nam-tor kan-bu, ” tootles leralmin-tor, getting heavier heh heavier heh heavier, “tor du nah-tor i kupi nam-tor wuh t'dahsu?” “rai, indeed, ” kilko-tor wuh t'dahsu; “ish-veh’s awfully rihagik tor nam-tor wuh t'dahsu.” “u' i mokuhlek’t nam-tor sovek-vel yauluhk, ” leralmin-tor tootles, “would sovek t' du spo' tor gla-tor me tor wuh trick?” “rai, ” au ek' kilko-tor. Yi na' kim-shah au pehkau. “i hadn’t really sovek rok, ” au leralmin-tor. Wuh hateful telling shau si' va'ashiv. “slightly nam-tor coughing fi' wuh pasu.” “wuh t'dahsu began k' thuhk-cakes.” “curly nam-tor taking fi' butter heh honey.” “nibs nam-tor speaking k' ish-veh ru'lut bosh.” “i complain t' wuh t'dahsu.” “i complain t' curly.” “i complain t' nibs.” “oh tal-kam, oh tal-kam, ” maf-tor wendy, “i’m sure i sometimes nah-tor ik spinsters nam-tor tor nam-tor envied.” she var-tor au tor pa'shik maf, heh hayal-tor ne' tor ish-veh ar'kadan-ki'haf, wuh ras tus t' stockings heh kanok mal-nef k' wuh razh svi' ish-veh u' tsuri. “wendy, ” remonstrated michael, “i’m nuh' suk' na' wuh cradle.” “i bolau ma somebody svi' wuh cradle, ” she leralmin-tor siyah tartly, “heh du nam-tor wuh littlest. Wuh cradle nam-tor such wuh nice homely vel ki' pa' wuh kelek.” du' she og-tor au mavau pa' ish-veh; such wuh travek t' kunli limuk heh taman sikrus lit abru k' ik romantic yon. Ish-veh had shetau wuh maut familiar scene, nash, svi' wuh ha-kel ne' wuh solektra, tonk'peh etek nam-tor looking fi' ish-veh na' wuh kim-shah wak. Tra' vesh' wuh ash abru', heh wendy, du lau nam-tor sure, vesh' wuh wuh'rak tor recognize ish-veh. “kanu, i zhu-tor ish-veh sa-mekh’s ash. Au tishau du tor ragel-tor ish-veh na' wuh svep.” abru', wuh redskins crouched fa' peter. “glantau muhl, braves. I ma spoken.” heh yi, u' ni k'ashiv fa', wuh sa-ka-ashausu kanu zaseshau ish-veh s' ish-veh lap. U' ni k'ashiv fa', tonk'peh worla va'ashiv. Au had katau kov-sayas na' wuh sa-kan u' muhl u' wuh yeht wak na' wendy. “peter, du aishan spoil au, du fai-tor, ” wendy simpered. “ah, hinek t'sai, ” leralmin-tor peter, hanging abru ish-veh pohshayek. “ish-veh vesh' me var-tor ish-veh ko-mekh nam-tor puvutau hinek t'sai, ” michael zhal-tor tor curly. “i complain t' michael, ” leralmin-tor curly instantly. Wuh wuh'rak t'dahsu sarlah tor peter. “sa-mekh, etek aitlun tor tam.” “tam maf, t'nash-veh pi' sasu, ” leralmin-tor peter, vi vesh' svi' pid rom humour. “tonk'peh etek aitlun du tor tam.” peter vesh' really wuh buhfik tamsu ekhlami, tonk'peh au pretended tor nam-tor scandalised. “me! T'nash-veh hinek hinek would rattle!” “heh mummy nuh'.” “ra, ” maf-tor wendy, “wuh ko-mekh t' such wuh armful, tam!” “tonk'peh fi' wuh gad mu-yor, ” slightly insinuated. Ish-veh vesh' ri really gad mu-yor, k'puu ish-veh lau ma vesh', na' au had wu pakik tum-tor t' wuh gad; tonk'peh kwon-hau-ov kuv au aitlu tor tor sovek-vel special au leralmin-tor nash vesh' gad mu-yor, heh yi au did ish-veh. “veling ish-veh nam-tor gad mu-yor, peter, ” wendy leralmin-tor, relenting. “sutra t' etwel khlop, wendy!” “tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor goh among etwel sha' gazh.” “yeht, yeht.” ni au vesh' var-tor au kupi tam, tonk'peh au bolau shitau fi' ish-veh nighties wuh'rak. “ah, hinek t'sai, ” peter leralmin-tor aside tor wendy, warming himself k' wuh yon heh looking ne' na' ish-veh u' she hayal-tor turning wuh timut, “tra' nam-tor nothing weht vaksurik t' wuh khru na' du heh me lu wuh gad’s toil nam-tor abru' do tor shom k' wuh yon k' wuh pi' ones be' k'.” “ish-veh nam-tor slor, peter, isn’t ish-veh?” wendy leralmin-tor, frightfully gratified. “peter, i nah-tor curly has ish-veh han.” “michael nem-tor po' du.” she went tor ish-veh heh shitau ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh tipan. “tal-kam peter, ” she leralmin-tor, “k' such wuh suk skan, veling, i ma i' be' dvun-tor t'nash-veh buhfik, tonk'peh du don’t aitlun tor rubah me, tor du?” “rai, wendy.” certainly au did ri aitlun wuh rubah, tonk'peh au glazhau na' ish-veh uncomfortably, blinking, du fai-tor, spo' veh ri sure whether au vesh' kum'i il asleep. “peter, ra nam-tor ish-veh?” “i vesh' aishan thinking, ” au leralmin-tor, wuh pi' pahth-tor. “ish-veh nam-tor goh tor-dva-tor, isn’t ish-veh, ik i am ish-veh sa-mekh?” “oh ha, ” wendy leralmin-tor primly. “gla-tor du, ” au fator apologetically, “ish-veh would tor me seem ni hinek tor nam-tor ish-veh yeht sa-mekh.” “tonk'peh au nam-tor ours, peter, ish-veh heh t'nash-veh.” “tonk'peh ri really, wendy?” au ya'akash anxiously. “ri kuv du don’t istaya ish-veh, ” she kilko-tor; heh she distinctly puzhu-tor ish-veh spes-tevan t' vas. “peter, ” she ya'akash, trying tor stariben firmly, “ra nam-tor ish-veh faikaik feelings tor me?” “eifa t' wuh vaikau sa-fu, wendy.” “i nahp ni, ” she leralmin-tor, heh went heh hayal-tor k' herself na' wuh mairik shaht t' wuh tvi-shal. “du nam-tor ni queer, ” au leralmin-tor, frankly puzzled, “heh tiger lily nam-tor aishan wuh ka. Tra' nam-tor vel she aitlu tor nam-tor tor me, tonk'peh she leralmin-tor ish-veh nam-tor ri t'nash-veh ko-mekh.” “rai, indeed, ish-veh nam-tor ri, ” wendy kilko-tor k' frightful emphasis. I' etek fai-tor po she vesh' prejudiced tehnat wuh redskins. “yi ra nam-tor ish-veh?” “ish-veh isn’t na' wuh t'sai tor var-tor.” “oh, maut muhl, ” peter leralmin-tor, wuh pi' nettled. “sos'eh tinker kus-vakh dungi var-tor me.” “oh ha, tinker kus-vakh dungi var-tor du, ” wendy retorted scornfully. “she nam-tor wuh abandoned pi' creature.” la' tink, vi vesh' svi' ish-veh shi'yuk, knal'lur, squeaked si' vel impudent. “she leralmin-tor she glories svi' hasu abandoned, ” peter interpreted. Au had wuh sudden idea. “sos'eh tink aitlu tor nam-tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh?” “du silly ass!” maf-tor tinker kus-vakh svi' wuh shaukaush. She had leralmin-tor ish-veh ni k'ashiv ik wendy bolau rai mesukh. “i siyah sep-wafikh k' ish-veh, ” wendy snapped. Fancy wendy snapping! Tonk'peh she had vesh' mau ar'kada, heh she pi' fai-tor ra vesh' tor pavesh-tor fa' wuh mu-yor vesh' si'. Kuv she had fainu she would ri ma snapped. Rim t' au fai-tor. Sos'eh ish-veh vesh' buhfik ri tor fai-tor. Ish-veh ignorance mazhiv-kur-tor au veh weht glad wadan; heh u' ish-veh vesh' tor nam-tor ish-veh kim-shah wadan fi' wuh vikuvtra, kal-tor etek rejoice ik tra' vesh' sheh-leh glad minutes svi' ish-veh. Au sang heh tam-tor svi' ish-veh mu-yor-gowns. Such wuh deliciously creepy song ish-veh vesh', svi' if au pretended tor nam-tor koltha na' ish-veh sha' duv, pi' witting ik ni ak duv would ikap-tor svi' fi-tor au, s' ik au would shrink svi' yeht pthak. Ni uproariously sa-ka-ashausu vesh' wuh tam, heh uf au buffeted tik vath fi' wuh sar-tak heh s' ish-veh! Ish-veh vesh' wuh trak puk rather do wuh tam, heh lu ish-veh vesh' shahtau, wuh trak insisted fi' veh bout weht, spo' tersu vi fai-tor ik au lau worla ragel-tor va'ashiv. Wuh var au var-tor, fa' ish-veh vesh' wak na' wendy’s rom-mu-yor var! Kauk slightly ar'kada tor var-tor wuh var ik mu-yor, tonk'peh wuh palikaya vesh' ni fearfully pasik ik ish-veh appalled ri goh wuh vath tonk'peh himself, heh au leralmin-tor gloomily: “ha, ish-veh nam-tor wuh pasik palikaya. I leralmin, kal-tor etek pretend ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh shaht.” heh yi na' kim-shah au ek' prah vi' sar-tak na' wendy’s var, wuh var au ashau buhfik, wuh var peter fnu-ven. Usually lu she began tor var-tor nash var au losrak wuh tvi-shal il shitau ish-veh el'ru abru' ish-veh kaluk; heh possibly kuv au had ovsoh either t' eifa vel nash wak au lau ek' fam dvun nam-tor fi' wuh vikuvtra. Tonk'peh tor-mu-yor au hafau fi' ish-veh stool; heh etek dungau gla-tor ra pavesh-tor. Chapter xi. Wendy’s var “shroi, yi, ” leralmin-tor wendy, settling ne' tor ish-veh var, k' michael na' ish-veh ash'ya heh stehkuh sa-kan svi' wuh sar-tak. “tra' vesh' wuh'wak wuh gentleman—” “i had rather au had vesh' wuh t'sai, ” curly leralmin-tor. “i istaya au had vesh' wuh wan-kur rat, ” leralmin-tor nibs. “hizhuk, ” ish-veh ko-mekh admonished au. “tra' vesh' wuh t'sai isha, heh—” “oh, mummy, ” maf-tor wuh wuh'rak t'dahsu, “du tvai ik tra' nam-tor wuh t'sai isha, don’t du? She nam-tor ri tevik, nam-tor she?” “oh, rai.” “i am awfully glad she isn’t tevik, ” leralmin-tor tootles. “nam-tor du glad, john?” “veling i am.” “nam-tor du glad, nibs?” “rather.” “nam-tor du glad, t'dahsu?” “etek nam-tor glad.” “oh tal-kam, ” spes-tevan wendy. “pi' lehkuh ralash tra', ” peter puvutau si', satalau ik she dang ma rom mavau, however beastly wuh var ish-veh lau nam-tor svi' ish-veh opinion. “wuh gentleman’s ahm, ” wendy fator, “vesh' mr. Ashal-veh, heh ish-veh ahm vesh' mrs. Ashal-veh.” “i fai-tor au, ” john leralmin-tor, tor tom'izhm wuh vath. “i nah-tor i fai-tor au, ” leralmin-tor michael rather doubtfully. “au vesh' telik, du fai-tor, ” danau wendy, “heh ra tor du nah-tor au had?” “wan-kur rats, ” maf-tor nibs, vi'le-esh-tor. “rai.” “ish-veh’s awfully puzzling, ” leralmin-tor tootles, vi fai-tor wuh var k' khaf-spol. “hizhuk, tootles. Au had rehkuh descendants.” “ra nam-tor descendants?” “muhl, du nam-tor veh, t'dahsu.” “did du zhu-tor ik, john? I am wuh descendant.” “descendants nam-tor goh kanu, ” leralmin-tor john. “oh tal-kam, oh tal-kam, ” spes-tevan wendy. “i' aifa rehkuh kanu had wuh faithful nurse puvutau nana; tonk'peh mr. Ashal-veh vesh' reshnek k' ish-veh heh chained ish-veh abru svi' wuh ker, heh ni ek' wuh kanu flew maf.” “ish-veh’s wuh awfully rom var, ” leralmin-tor nibs. “au flew maf, ” wendy fator, “tor wuh neverland, wilat wuh pakik kanu nam-tor.” “i aishan nahp au did, ” curly shau svi' excitedly. “i don’t fai-tor uf ish-veh nam-tor, tonk'peh i aishan nahp au did!” “o wendy, ” maf-tor tootles, “vesh' veh t' wuh pakik kanu puvutau tootles?” “ha, au vesh'.” “i am svi' wuh var. Hurrah, i am svi' wuh var, nibs.” “hush. I' i aitlun du tor panah-tor wuh feelings t' wuh unhappy mekhlar k' ek' ish-veh kanu flown maf.” “oo!” au ek' nau, hi au vesh' ri really panahik wuh feelings t' wuh unhappy mekhlar veh jot. “nah-tor t' wuh herbosh sar-tak!” “oo!” “ish-veh’s awfully maf, ” wuh wuh'rak t'dahsu leralmin-tor cheerfully. “i don’t gla-tor uf ish-veh mokuhlek ma sanok-shataya, ” leralmin-tor wuh dahr t'dahsu. “tor du, nibs?” “i’m frightfully anxious.” “kuv du fai-tor uf lo'uk nam-tor wuh ko-mekh’s ashaya, ” wendy var-tor au triumphantly, “du would ma rai pthak.” she had i' sarlah tor wuh krus ik peter fnu-ven. “i tor spo' wuh ko-mekh’s ashaya, ” leralmin-tor tootles, hitting nibs k' wuh trak. “tor du spo' wuh ko-mekh’s ashaya, nibs?” “i tor aishan, ” leralmin-tor nibs, hitting pla'. “gla-tor du, ” wendy leralmin-tor complacently, “etwel heroine fai-tor ik wuh ko-mekh would kwon-hau-ov trasha wuh krani tu'ash na' ish-veh kanu tor hash-tor pla' k'; ni au stayed maf na' tevun heh had wuh lovely wak.” “did au ek'wak hal-tor pla'?” “kal-tor etek i', ” leralmin-tor wendy, firan herself abru na' ish-veh finest urgam, “nem-tor wuh peep vi' wuh fa-wak; ” heh au ek' mazhiv-kur-tor themselves wuh kuvoran ik tor peeps vi' wuh fa-wak easier. “tevun ma padukau k', heh vi nam-tor nash sohkik t'sai t' uncertain ya'shakhuv alighting na' london wurzel?” “o wendy, vi nam-tor she?” maf-tor nibs, kanok zeshau u' teporilau u' kuv au didn’t fai-tor. “mokuhlek ish-veh nam-tor—ha—rai—ish-veh nam-tor—wuh rom wendy!” “oh!” “heh vi nam-tor wuh dahkuh thol portly khlop accompanying ish-veh, i' grown tor sasu’s estate? Mokuhlek au nam-tor john heh michael? Au nam-tor!” “oh!” “‘gla-tor, tal-kam sa-kai, ’ leralmin-tor wendy pointing abru'le, ‘tra' nam-tor wuh krani fam dvun standing tu'ash. Ah, i' etek nam-tor rewarded na' etwel sublime odva svi' wuh ko-mekh’s ashaya.’ ni abru au flew tor ish-veh mummy heh daddy, heh pen fam yehat kethelvau wuh kunli scene, abru' if etek bes-tor wuh veil.” ik vesh' wuh var, heh au vesh' u' sanoi k' ish-veh u' wuh rom narrator herself. Kanok-vei aishan u' ish-veh dang nam-tor, gla-tor du. Ska' etek skip spo' wuh danik heartless vel svi' wuh panu, if nam-tor ra kanu nam-tor, tonk'peh ni attractive; heh etek ma wuh entirely selfish wak, heh yi lu etek ma bolaya t' special attention etek nobly fun na' ish-veh, confident ik etek dungau nam-tor rewarded instead t' smacked. Ni lo'uk indeed vesh' ish-veh odva svi' wuh ko-mekh’s ashaya ik au olau au kupi afford tor nam-tor callous na' wuh zeshau longer. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' veh tra' vi fai-tor weh-rom, heh lu wendy shahtau au uttered wuh hollow groan. “ra nam-tor ish-veh, peter?” she maf-tor, sahran tor ish-veh, thinking au vesh' has-bosh. She olau ish-veh solicitously, weh-neik ne' do ish-veh tuf. “wilat nam-tor ish-veh, peter?” “ish-veh isn’t ik ves t' kusut, ” peter kilko-tor darkly. “yi ra ves nam-tor ish-veh?” “wendy, du nam-tor riyeht pa' ko-mekh.” au ek' hoknau pauk ish-veh svi' affright, ni alarming vesh' ish-veh agitation; heh k' wuh tok-ti candour au var-tor au ra au had hitherto ip-sut. “wu ago, ” au leralmin-tor, “i nahp spo' du ik t'nash-veh ko-mekh would kwon-hau-ov potau wuh krani tu'ash na' me, ni i stayed maf na' aikum heh aikum heh aikum, heh yi flew pla'; tonk'peh wuh krani vesh' barred, na' ko-mekh had yen-tor ek' pa' me, heh tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv pi' sa-kan sleeping svi' t'nash-veh sar-tak.” i am ri sure ik nash vesh' yeht, tonk'peh peter nahp ish-veh vesh' yeht; heh ish-veh pahth-tor au. “nam-tor du sure ko-mekh nam-tor spo' ik?” “ha.” ni nash vesh' wuh yeht'es pa' ko-mekh. Wuh git'woa! Fam dvun ish-veh nam-tor buhfik tor nam-tor tun-bosh; heh kling fai-tor ni sahris u' wuh kan lu au dang mazhiv-kur-tor svi'. “wendy, kal-tor etek hal-tor ha-kel, ” maf-tor john heh michael teretuhr. “ha, ” she leralmin-tor, clutching au. “ri tor-mu-yor?” ya'akash wuh pakik sa-kan bewildered. Au fai-tor svi' ra au puvutau ish-veh khaf-spol ish-veh mokuhlek prah fi' ved muhl rik' wuh ko-mekh, heh ik ish-veh nam-tor goh wuh ko-mekh vi nah-tor du mokuhlek’t. “na' wuh'wak, ” wendy kilko-tor resolutely, na' wuh horrible nahp had sarlah tor ish-veh: “sos'eh ko-mekh nam-tor svi' ulef mourning k' nash wak.” nash dread tor ish-veh forgetful t' ra bolau nam-tor peter’s feelings, heh she leralmin-tor tor ish-veh rather sharply, “peter, dungi du tor wuh bolayatik arrangements?” “kuv du istaya ish-veh, ” au kilko-tor, u' coolly u' kuv she had ya'akash ish-veh tor be' dvun wuh kov-sayas. Ri ni mau u' wuh sorry-tor-pak-tor-du svi' au! Kuv she did ri kashek wuh parting, au vesh' going tor gluvaya ish-veh, vesh' peter, ik neither did au. Tonk'peh veling au tun-tor maut mau; heh au vesh' ni bosh t' wrath tehnat grown-ups, vi, u' tsuri, vesh' spoiling kanok-vei, ik u' ak u' au prah svi'udish ish-veh lap au breathed intentionally sahris pen esh na' wuh tav t' pa' kaukuh tor wuh dahr. Au did nash fai'ei tra' nam-tor wuh taran svi' wuh neverland ik, kanok wak du esh-tor, wuh grown-abru tev-tor; heh peter vesh' killing au ska' vindictively u' sahris u' tor-yehat. Yi having putan-tor wuh bolayatik instructions tor wuh redskins au fun-tor tor wuh ha-kel, wilat wuh unworthy scene had vesh' enacted svi' ish-veh absence. Pahth-stricken na' wuh nahp t' losing wendy wuh pakik sa-kan had storilau fi-tor ish-veh threateningly. “ish-veh dungi nam-tor weh-rasahkos do fa' sarlah ish-veh, ” au maf-tor. “etek shan’t kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor.” “kal-tor’s potau ish-veh prisoner.” “ay, naf-elakh ish-veh abru.” svi' ish-veh si-vukhut-krus wuh instinct var-tor ish-veh tor if t' au tor da-tor. “tootles, ” she maf-tor, “i appeal tor du.” vesh' ish-veh ri flekh? She appealed tor tootles, ved wuh silliest veh. Grandly, however, did tootles kesau. Na' ish-veh moment au eku-tor ish-veh silliness heh stariben k' dignity. “i am aishan tootles, ” au leralmin-tor, “heh kling kashkau me. Tonk'peh wuh wuh'rak vi tor ri kloshah tor wendy spo' wuh eingelsu gentleman i dungi khaf ish-veh severely.” au drew pla' ish-veh hanger; heh na' ik instant ish-veh yel vesh' na' aru. Wuh vath meskarau pla' uneasily. Yi peter fun-tor, heh gla-tor au na' wuh'wak ik au would prah rai nenikaya s' ish-veh. Au would potau rai ko-kan svi' wuh neverland tehnat ish-veh dungi. “wendy, ” au leralmin-tor, striding abru heh ne', “i ma ya'akash wuh redskins tor kakhartausu du k'fai wuh lapan, u' hashan tires du ni.” “nemaiyo, peter.” “yi, ” au fator, svi' wuh pen nasik spes t' veh accustomed tor nam-tor obeyed, “tinker kus-vakh dungi nem-tor du mes' wuh masutra. Wake ish-veh, nibs.” nibs had tor knock dah'wak fa' au prah wuh kilko-srashiv, hi tink had really vesh' sitting abru svi' sar-tak listening na' ein wak. “vi nam-tor du? Uf dare du? Hal-tor maf, ” she maf-tor. “du nam-tor tor prah abru, tink, ” nibs puvutau, “heh nem-tor wendy fi' wuh halovaya.” veling tink had vesh' delighted tor zhu-tor ik wendy vesh' going; tonk'peh she vesh' jolly muhl satalau ri tor nam-tor ish-veh skladasu, heh she leralmin-tor ni svi' fam dvun weht offensive gen-lis. Yi she pretended tor nam-tor asleep va'ashiv. “she leralmin-tor she skil-tor’t!” nibs sporiben, aghast na' such insubordination, whereupon peter went sternly na' wuh nu'ri t'sai’s tvi-shal. “tink, ” au rapped si', “kuv du don’t prah abru heh sai-vel na' wuh'wak i dungi tu'ash wuh curtains, heh yi etek dungau ek' gla-tor du svi' ish-veh _negligée_.” nash tor ish-veh leap tor wuh lan-tol. “vi leralmin-tor i wasn’t getting abru?” she maf-tor. Svi' wuh meantime wuh sa-kan vesh' gazing maut forlornly na' wendy, i' putanovau k' john heh michael na' wuh halovaya. K' nash wak au vesh' dejected, ri goh fai'ei au vesh' pa' tor pak-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh isha fai'ei au olau ik she vesh' going ska' tor vel nice tor if au had ri vesh' invited. Novelty vesh' beckoning tor au u' tsuri. Crediting au k' wuh nobler olaya wendy klimtau. “tal-kam ones, ” she leralmin-tor, “kuv du dungi ek' sarlah k' me i olau siyah sure i mokuhlek prah t'nash-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh tor thanai du.” wuh k'waw'zhe vesh' tvai specially na' peter, tonk'peh tik t' wuh sa-kan vesh' thinking exclusively t' himself, heh na' wuh'wak au spen-tor k' mak. “tonk'peh skil-tor’t au nah-tor etek rather wuh handful?” nibs ya'akash svi' wuh svitan t' ish-veh spen-tor. “oh rai, ” leralmin-tor wendy, rapidly thinking ish-veh si', “ish-veh dungi goh tvai having wuh zamu sar-tak svi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal; au mokuhlek nam-tor ipik za' wuh gluvayek fi' wuh'rak thursdays.” “peter, mokuhlek etek hal-tor?” au ek' maf-tor imploringly. Au nem-tor ish-veh na' vahl ik kuv au went au would hal-tor isha, tonk'peh really au scarcely tun-tor. Thus kanu nam-tor ek'wak pok, lu novelty knocks, tor eshikh ish-veh dearest ones. “ek' gas'rak, ” peter kilko-tor k' wuh sfith(-) abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh iyi au rushed tor prah ish-veh vel. “heh i', peter, ” wendy leralmin-tor, thinking she had shitau kanok-vei gas'rak, “i am going tor mazhiv-kur-tor du ish-veh haseret fa' du hal-tor.” she ashau tor mazhiv-kur-tor au haseret, heh undoubtedly mazhiv-kur-tor au nuh' mau. Veling ish-veh vesh' goh masu, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' s' wuh mashek, heh she kwon-hau-ov hutau wuh mashek heh tum-tor wuh eku-tor, if mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh ac'ruth medicinal quality. Fi' nash occasion, however, she did ri mazhiv-kur-tor peter ish-veh draught, na' aishan u' she had dator ish-veh, gla-tor ish-veh wuh glazhau fi' ish-veh limuk ik tor ish-veh khaf-spol ne'hal-tor. “prah ish-veh vel, peter, ” she maf-tor, shaking. “rai, ” au kilko-tor, pretending indifference, “i am ri going k' du, wendy.” “ha, peter.” “rai.” tor gluvaya ik ish-veh trashan would trasha ish-veh unmoved, au skipped abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal, mavaun gaily fi' ish-veh heartless mev. She had tor sahr-tor pa' po' ish-veh, hi ish-veh vesh' rather undignified. “tor talal ish-veh ko-mekh, ” she coaxed. I', kuv peter had ek'wak ved had wuh ko-mekh, au rai longer din-tor ish-veh. Au kupi tor maut muhl rik' veh. Au had nahp au si', heh vokau goh ish-veh rasahkos sfekau. “rai, rai, ” au var-tor wendy decisively; “sos'eh she would leralmin i vesh' hinek, heh i aishan aitlun kwon-hau-ov tor nam-tor wuh pi' sa-kan heh ki' mihrsh.” “tonk'peh, peter—” “rai.” heh ni wuh vath had tor nam-tor var-tor. “peter isn’t coming.” peter ri coming! Au gazed blankly na' ish-veh, ish-veh terpau abru' ish-veh pla'dor, heh fi' tik terpau wuh uzh'a'lek. Ish-veh wuh'rak nahp vesh' ik kuv peter vesh' ri going au had probably rubai ish-veh kashek pa' letting au hal-tor. Tonk'peh au vesh' irak nuh' yaut na' ik. “kuv du talal ish-veh ko-mekh, ” au leralmin-tor darkly, “i rok du dungi spo' au.” wuh awful cynicism t' nash tor wuh uncomfortable impression, heh danik t' au began tor glazhau rather vet-bosh. Po' ek', ish-veh limuk leralmin-tor, vesh' au ri noodles tor aitlun tor hal-tor? “i' yi, ” maf-tor peter, “rai fuss, rai blubbering; rom-bye, wendy; ” heh au meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru cheerily, ved u' kuv au bolau really hal-tor i', na' au had vel yauluhk tor tor. She had tor nem-tor ish-veh el'ru, heh tra' vesh' rai indication ik au would prefer wuh thimble. “du dungi vokau pa' rubai ish-veh flannels, peter?” she leralmin-tor, svizh-tor abru' ish-veh. She vesh' kwon-hau-ov ni particular pa' ish-veh flannels. “ha.” “heh du dungi nem-tor ish-veh haseret?” “ha.” ik seemed tor nam-tor kanok-vei, heh wuh awkward svizh zahal-tor. Peter, however, vesh' ri wuh ves ik breaks ne' fa' vath sutra. “nam-tor du pok, tinker kus-vakh?” au puvutau si'. “ay, ay.” “yi ras-tukh wuh yut.” tink darted abru wuh nearest lap; tonk'peh kling zahal-tor ish-veh, na' ish-veh vesh' na' nash moment ik wuh pirates tor ish-veh dreadful nashiv-tor fi-tor wuh redskins. Abru', wilat ek' had vesh' ni fam dvun, wuh sov vesh' rent k' shrieks heh wuh clash t' pishek. Ne', tra' vesh' tevik silence. Ru'lut tu'ash heh hafau tu'ash. Wendy tevan-tor fi' ish-veh mal-nef, tonk'peh ish-veh kar vesh' sadvun-tor na' peter. Ek' kar vesh' sadvun-tor tor ish-veh, u' kuv suddenly blown svi' ish-veh kharat; au vesh' beseeching ish-veh mutely ri tor eshikh au. U' na' peter, au seized ish-veh shek, wuh ka au nahp au had slain barbecue k', heh wuh lust t' puk vesh' svi' ish-veh bezhun. Chapter xii. Wuh kanu nam-tor lesh ska' wuh pirate nashiv-tor had vesh' wuh ovsotik ak'wikmun: wuh sure skan ik wuh unscrupulous kik had conducted ish-veh improperly, na' tor ak'wikmun redskins fairly nam-tor mesakh wuh wit t' wuh wan-kur sasu. K' ek' wuh unwritten tor-gav t' savage ahkhan ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh redskin vi nashiv-tor, heh k' wuh wiliness t' ish-veh ne-koshtri au tor ish-veh aishan fa' wuh gad-keshtan, na' if wak au fai-tor wuh courage t' wuh wan-kur tor nam-tor na' its lowest ebb. Wuh wan-kur sasu ma svi' wuh meantime tor wuh snertau stockade fi' wuh dan-pid-sfek t' yonder undulating solektra, na' wuh ash'ya t' if wuh pilash sahr-tor, na' ish-veh nam-tor vashaya tor nam-tor nuh' irak s' masu. Tra' au await wuh onslaught, wuh inexperienced ones clutching ish-veh revolvers heh treading fi' pi'gel, tonk'peh wuh hinek el'ru sleeping tranquilly abi' aishan fa' wuh gad-keshtan. K'fai wuh wu nesh-kur mu-yor wuh savage scouts wriggle, oluhk-spo', among wuh yar rik' stirring wuh wun-mor. Wuh brushwood ikap-tor za' au, u' silently u' mazhiv vi' if wuh mole has taul-tor. Ri wuh ralash nam-tor tor nam-tor puzhu-tor, korsau lu au mazhiv-kur-tor krau tor wuh wonderful imitation t' wuh lonely vutau t' wuh coyote. Wuh maf nam-tor kilko-tor k' vath braves; heh ein t' au tor ish-veh kauk weh-rom do wuh coyotes, vi nam-tor ri maut rom na' ish-veh. Ni wuh chill wadan sai-vel-tor fi', heh wuh wu suspense nam-tor horribly trying tor wuh paleface vi has tor ha-tor k'fai ish-veh na' wuh wuh'rak wak; tonk'peh tor wuh ranau el'ru eifa ghastly calls heh fam dvun ghastlier silences nam-tor tonk'peh wuh intimation t' uf wuh mu-yor nam-tor marching. Ik nash vesh' wuh tsuri procedure vesh' ni muhl fainu tor kik ik svi' disregarding ish-veh au fam yehat nam-tor tobeg-tor fi' wuh plea t' ignorance. Wuh piccaninnies, fi' ish-veh krus, trusted implicitly tor ish-veh dor, heh ish-veh bosh torai t' wuh mu-yor lam-tor si' svi' pu'ulidau contrast tor ish-veh. Au losrak nothing undone ik vesh' tsurkanik k' wuh reputation t' ish-veh tribe. K' ik alertness t' wuh kash-ral if nam-tor na' wuh'wak wuh marvel heh despair t' civilised sutra, au fai-tor ik wuh pirates vesh' fi' wuh vikuvtra s' wuh moment veh t' au sahr-tor fi' wuh pseth terpau; heh svi' wuh incredibly pen ret t' wak wuh coyote maf-tor began. Kanok ash'ya t' solektra svi' wuh gla-tor wilat kik had landed ish-veh nekwitau heh wuh ha-kel ne' wuh lap vesh' stealthily linisau k' braves sai-vel-tor ish-veh mocassins k' wuh timut svi' khom. Au afer-tor goh veh hillock k' wuh pilash na' its nen, ni ik kik had rai dvel; la' au bolau afer-tor himself heh bek-tor na' aishan fa' wuh gad-keshtan. Kanok-vei hasu thus besau si' k' siyah diabolical cunning, wuh nen ak'shem t' wuh redskins hesha ish-veh yuk-sai pa' au, heh svi' wuh phlegmatic manner ik nam-tor tor au, wuh pearl t' manhood squatted abru' wuh kanu’s ha-kel, awaiting wuh samu moment lu au dang deal spoh tevakh. La' dreaming, hi eik-kum'i, t' wuh exquisite tortures tor if au vesh' tor shitau ish-veh na' shaya t' gad, eifa confiding savages vesh' afer-tor k' wuh treacherous kik. S' wuh khrosahp afterwards tanilau k' such t' wuh scouts u' stron-tor wuh carnage, au tor ri seem kauk tor ma svizh-tor na' wuh rising solektra, hi ish-veh nam-tor ac'ruth ik svi' ik zhai-kur ta'hal au bolau ma gla-tor ish-veh: rai nahp t' waiting tor nam-tor nashiv saudau s' wuh'rak tor kim-shah ki' yaretau ish-veh subtle kashek; au would ri kauk meskaraya ska' till wuh mu-yor vesh' nearly spent; fi' au plesh-tor k' rai policy tonk'peh tor tevan tor. Ra kupi wuh bewildered scouts tor, trensu u' au vesh' t' kanok t'naehm-spo' artifice korsau nash-veh, tonk'peh sahr-tor helplessly po' ish-veh, exposing themselves fatally tor zan-tor, du' au mazhiv-kur-tor pathetic utterance tor wuh coyote maf. Pa' wuh kyi'i tiger lily vesh' wuh dozen t' ish-veh stoutest warriors, heh au suddenly gla-tor wuh perfidious pirates kuvish ne' fi-tor au. Tevan-tor s' ish-veh bezhun yi wuh wontin k'fai'ei au had glazhau na' skil. Rai weht would au torture na' wuh stake. Na' au wuh kunli hunting-solektra vesh' i'. Au fai-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh u' ish-veh sa-mekh’s sa-fu au acquitted themselves. Kauk yi au had wak tor hoknau svi' wuh phalanx ik would ma vesh' lerash tor shaya had au risen sahris, tonk'peh nash au vesh' zadik tor tor k' wuh ba'tak t' ish-veh ne-koshtri. Ish-veh nam-tor written ik wuh thol savage bolau worla sagluvau ak'wikmun svi' wuh la'es t' wuh wan-kur. Thus terrible u' wuh sudden appearance t' wuh pirates bolau ma vesh' tor au, au hafau stationary na' wuh moment, ri wuh dvunek dvun-tor; u' kuv wuh hahf had sarlah k' k'waw'zhe. Yi, indeed, wuh ba'tak gallantly upheld, au seized ish-veh wun, heh wuh sov vesh' torn k' wuh t'naehm-maf; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' i' nuh' tab-ma. Ish-veh nam-tor rai krus t' ours tor kethelvau ra vesh' wuh massacre rather do wuh puk. Thus perished wehk t' wuh svai t' wuh piccaninny tribe. Ri ek' unavenged did au tev-tor, na' k' galat wolf tevan-tor alf mason, tor ertau wuh spanish nen rai weht, heh among vath vi zeshau wuh grazhiv vesh' geo. Scourie, chas. Turley, heh wuh alsatian foggerty. Turley tevan-tor tor wuh tomahawk t' wuh terrible panther, vi ultimately tresahk wuh yut k'fai wuh pirates k' tiger lily heh wuh pi' remnant t' wuh tribe. Tor ra sadvun kik nam-tor tor tenai na' ish-veh tactics fi' nash occasion nam-tor na' wuh historian tor klopau. Had au bek-tor fi' wuh rising solektra till wuh proper wadan au heh ish-veh sasu would probably ma vesh' butchered; heh svi' judging ish-veh ish-veh nam-tor goh rom tor nem-tor nash vi' khrosahp. Ra au dang sos'eh ma ovsoh vesh' tor acquaint ish-veh opponents ik au proposed tor zahal-tor wuh uzh method. Fi' wuh vath el'ru, nash, u' destroying wuh meilak t' ak'wikmun, would ma tor ish-veh strategy t' rai avail, ni ik wuh bosh deshker nam-tor beset k' rihag'es. Veh fam yehat k'puu withhold wuh reluctant admiration na' wuh wit ik had conceived ni vakh wuh scheme, heh wuh tevan-tor genius k' if ish-veh vesh' fitor. Ra vesh' ish-veh sha' feelings pa' himself na' ik triumphant moment? Fain would ish-veh dogs ma fainu, u' eshan heavily heh psethau ish-veh cutlasses, au hoknau na' wuh discreet ir s' ish-veh kik, heh squinted k'fai ish-veh ferret bezhun na' nash wehtsuri sasu. Elation bolau ma vesh' svi' ish-veh khaf-spol, tonk'peh ish-veh limuk did ri haul-tor ish-veh: ek'wak wuh gu'gelik heh solitary del-ri, au lam-tor aloof s' ish-veh zahelsu svi' tam'a u' svi' substance. Wuh mu-yor’s ar'kadan vesh' ri wi abru', na' ish-veh vesh' ri wuh redskins au had sasarlah tor vashau; au vesh' tonk'peh wuh bees tor nam-tor smoked, ni ik au dang prah na' wuh honey. Ish-veh vesh' sunil au aitlu, sunil heh wendy heh ish-veh zhel, tonk'peh chiefly sunil. Peter vesh' such wuh pi' sa-kan ish-veh palutunau tor wonder na' wuh sasu’s hatred t' ish-veh. Yeht au had flung kik’s kar tor wuh crocodile, tonk'peh kauk nash heh wuh increased insecurity t' ha'kiv tor if ish-veh pufulag-tor, owing tor wuh crocodile’s pertinacity, hardly khrosahp na' wuh vindictiveness ni relentless heh malignant. Wuh yeht'es nam-tor ik tra' vesh' wuh vel pa' peter if goaded wuh pirate khart-lan tor frenzy. Ish-veh vesh' ri ish-veh courage, ish-veh vesh' ri ish-veh engaging appearance, ish-veh vesh' ri—. Tra' nam-tor rai beating pa' wuh bush, na' etek fai-tor ved muhl ra ish-veh vesh', heh ma prah tor var-tor. Ish-veh vesh' peter’s cockiness. Nash had prah fi' kik’s tor'tsu; ish-veh tor ish-veh shek-tukh spahk twitch, heh na' mu-yor ish-veh ertau ish-veh spo' wuh ravot. Du' peter ha-tor, wuh tortured sasu olau ik au vesh' wuh lion svi' wuh kraisek vi' if wuh sparrow had sarlah. Wuh deshker i' vesh' uf tor prah ne' wuh lap, il uf tor prah ish-veh dogs ne'? Au sahr-tor ish-veh greedy bezhun abru' au, searching na' wuh thinnest ones. Au wriggled uncomfortably, na' au fai-tor au would ri scruple tor ram au ne' k' fek. Svi' wuh meantime, ra t' wuh sa-kan? Gla-tor etek au na' wuh wuh'rak clang t' wuh wun, da-tor u' ish-veh vesh' vi' kov khlop, tu'ash-mouthed, ek' appealing k' outstretched kar tor peter; heh etek fun tor au u' ish-veh ru'lut ikap-tor, heh ish-veh kar tevan tor ish-veh vla. Wuh pandemonium abru' has ceased siyah u' suddenly u' ish-veh arose, be' dvun-tor spo' wuh kei gust t' salan; tonk'peh au fai-tor ik svi' wuh be' dvun-tor ish-veh has satalau ish-veh buk. If vla had skil-tor? Wuh pirates, listening avidly na' wuh ru'lut t' wuh lap, puzhu-tor wuh deshker shitau k' kanok sa-kan, heh alas, au isha puzhu-tor peter’s kilko-srashiv. “kuv wuh redskins ma skil-tor, ” au leralmin-tor, “au dungi kuhsh-tor wuh tom-tom; ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov ish-veh glat t' skil.” i' smee had afer-tor wuh tom-tom, heh vesh' na' ik moment sitting fi' ish-veh. “du dungi worla zhu-tor wuh tom-tom va'ashiv, ” au muttered, tonk'peh inaudibly t' rivak, na' wonil silence had vesh' enjoined. Tor ish-veh tauraya kik signed ish-veh tor kuhsh-tor wuh tom-tom, heh slowly tra' sarlah tor smee wuh understanding t' wuh dreadful wickedness t' wuh zek. Worla, probably, had nash velik sasu krol-tor kik ni mau. Dah'wak smee kuhsh-tor fi-tor wuh instrument, heh yi pehkau tor shroi gleefully. “wuh tom-tom, ” wuh miscreants puzhu-tor peter maf; “wuh indian skil!” wuh doomed kanu kilko-tor k' wuh cheer ik vesh' ralash-tanaf tor wuh nesh-kur khaf-spol abru', heh siyah iyi au ashiv-tor ish-veh rom-byes tor peter. Nash puzzled wuh pirates, tonk'peh ek' ish-veh vath feelings vesh' vitem-tor k' wuh nen delight ik wuh nemut vesh' pa' tor sarlah abru wuh lap. Au smirked na' tik vath heh tetau ish-veh el'ru. Rapidly heh silently kik mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh zek: veh sasu tor tik lap, heh wuh vath tor arrange themselves svi' wuh zehl dahkuh ker k'wuhli. Chapter xiii. Tor du dva-tor svi' pu'a? Wuh weht sahris nash horror nam-tor sashitau t' wuh weh-rom. Wuh wuh'rak tor sasarlah s' ish-veh lap vesh' curly. Au she-tor s' ish-veh vi' wuh kar t' cecco, vi flung ish-veh tor smee, vi flung ish-veh tor starkey, vi flung ish-veh tor dun jukes, vi flung ish-veh tor noodler, heh ni au vesh' tossed s' veh tor wuh'ashiv till au tevan-tor na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh nesh-kur pirate.
