Ek' wuh sa-kan vesh' plucked s' ish-veh lap svi' nash ruthless manner; heh several t' au vesh' svi' wuh sov na' wuh wak, spo' bales t' goods flung s' el'ru tor el'ru. Wuh natya skasaya vesh' accorded tor wendy, vi sarlah kim-shah. K' ironical politeness kik ashenau ish-veh taik tor ish-veh, heh, nufaya ish-veh ish-veh kar, escorted ish-veh tor wuh gla-tor wilat wuh vath vesh' hasu gagged. Au did ish-veh k' such wuh sov, au vesh' ni frightfully _distingué_, ik she vesh' nuh' sem-tor tor lit'dhae. She vesh' goh wuh pi' ko-kan. Sos'eh ish-veh nam-tor var-tor-var tor divulge ik na' wuh moment kik entranced ish-veh, heh etek var-tor fi' ish-veh goh fai'ei ish-veh trel pufulag-tor tor flekh results. Had she haughtily unhanded ish-veh (heh etek dang ma ashau tor kitau ish-veh t' ish-veh), she would ma vesh' hurled k'fai wuh sov spo' wuh vath, heh yi kik would probably ri ma vesh' la' na' wuh tying t' wuh kanu; heh had au ri vesh' na' wuh tying au would ri ma discovered slightly’s tsat, heh rik' wuh tsat au kupi ri presently ma tor ish-veh flalik attempt fi' peter’s ha'kiv. Au vesh' tied tor prevent ish-veh hashan maf, dahtau abru k' ish-veh mal-nef beyik ish-veh kaluk; heh na' wuh trussing t' au wuh nesh-kur pirate had tresahk wuh man-elakh vi' naukuh kaik krus. Ek' went muhl abi' slightly’s da-tor sarlah, lu au vesh' afer-tor tor nam-tor spo' eifa irritating parcels ik neis-tor ek' wuh string svi' going pauk heh trasha rai tags k' if tor tie wuh knot. Wuh pirates kicked ish-veh svi' ish-veh reshan, aishan u' du kick wuh parcel (hi svi' fairness du dang kick wuh string); heh flekh tor leralmin ish-veh vesh' kik vi var-tor au tor belay ish-veh khrash. Ish-veh bru vesh' tcha-tor k' malicious triumph. Du' ish-veh dogs vesh' goh sweating fai'ei kanok wak au ar'kada tor sa'haf wuh unhappy lad wufik svi' veh krus au bulged si' svi' wuh'ashiv, kik’s trensu kashek had hal-tor irak ne'rak slightly’s skonn, probing ri na' daya tonk'peh na' aisha; heh ish-veh exultation gluvau ik au had afer-tor au. Slightly, wan-kur tor wuh masu-eshanek, fai-tor ik kik had ak'wikmun ish-veh tsat, if vesh' nash, ik rai sa-kan ni blown si' kupi nam-tor-tor wuh lap wherein wuh bov sasu bolaya terpau. Ri donku-tor slightly, danik wretched t' ek' wuh kanu i', na' au vesh' svi' wuh pahth pa' peter, bitterly regretted ra au had ovsoh. Madly tessau tor wuh drinking t' masu lu au vesh' fal, au had puv-tor svi' consequence tor ish-veh la' girth, heh instead t' reducing himself tor nunau ish-veh lap au had, ri-fainu tor wuh vath, whittled ish-veh lap tor tor ish-veh nunau ish-veh. Sufficient t' nash kik guessed tor persuade ish-veh ik peter na' kim-shah ti na' ish-veh mercy, tonk'peh rai zhit t' wuh gu'gelik design ik i' shidau svi' wuh subterranean suk-tauk t' ish-veh kashek tuhsau ish-veh bru-lar; au goh signed ik wuh captives vesh' tor nam-tor zhelesh tor wuh hali, heh ik au would nam-tor sa'awek. Uf tor zhelesh au? Hunched abru svi' ish-veh man-elakh au lau indeed nam-tor padukau ne' kunel spo' subok, tonk'peh danik t' wuh yut ti k'fai wuh morass. Va'ashiv kik’s genius surmounted rihag'es. Au indicated ik wuh pi' kelek bolau nam-tor nam-tor-tor u' wuh conveyance. Wuh kanu vesh' flung vi' ish-veh, kehkuh stout pirates ashenau ish-veh fi' ish-veh tipan, wuh vath tevan-tor svi' za', heh uralaun wuh hateful pirate sular uralaun wuh flekh procession eku ska' k'fai wuh lapan. I don’t fai-tor whether sovek t' wuh kanu vesh' maf-tor; kuv ni, wuh uralaun mastevau wuh ralash; tonk'peh u' wuh pi' kelek sasaudau svi' wuh laptra, wuh kyi'i hi tiny jet t' vuzh issued s' its vuzh-mev u' kuv defying kik. Kik gla-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh did peter wuh rasahkos dvin. Ish-veh psethau abru sovek itsk-yumaya t' pity na' ish-veh ik lau ma hafau svi' wuh pirate’s infuriated thasek. Wuh wuh'rak vel au did fi' finding himself sa'awek svi' wuh sahris tevan-tor mu-yor vesh' tor tiptoe tor slightly’s lap, heh tor sure ik ish-veh tanilau ish-veh k' wuh tvur. Yi na' wu au hafau brooding; ish-veh taik t' has-bosh omen fi' wuh sward, ni ik sovek gentle pi'salan if had arisen lau mavau refreshingly k'fai ish-veh isachya. Gu'gelik u' vesh' ish-veh nahp ish-veh pla-kur bezhun vesh' u' mos u' wuh periwinkle. Intently au shroi na' sovek ralash s' wuh nether panu, tonk'peh ek' vesh' u' ralash-fam ne' u' abru'; wuh kelek ne' wuh solektra seemed tor nam-tor tonk'peh veh weht herbosh tenement svi' wuh void. Vesh' ik sa-kan asleep, il did au lamok waiting na' wuh ash'ya t' slightly’s lap, k' ish-veh lipitah svi' ish-veh el'ru? Tra' vesh' rai yut t' fai-tor, korsau k' going ne'. Kik kal-tor ish-veh tor-sai trel softly tor wuh solektra, heh yi biting ish-veh bru-lar till wuh lewd khaf lam-tor fi' au, au ash-tor vi' wuh lap. Au vesh' wuh kyi'i sasu, tonk'peh na' wuh moment au had tor pehkaya tra' heh psethau ish-veh meix'tem, if vesh' dripping spo' wuh ha'fek. Yi, silently, au kal-tor himself hal-tor vi' wuh ri-fainu. Au lasha unmolested na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh shaft, heh lam-tor fam dvun va'ashiv, biting na' ish-veh esh, if had siyah losrak ish-veh. U' ish-veh bezhun became accustomed tor wuh neik-ha'khlup ta'hal vuhnauk vel svi' wuh ha-kel ne' wuh lap nem-tor shid; tonk'peh wuh goh veh fi' if ish-veh greedy gaze shom-tor, wu sought na' heh afer-tor na' kim-shah, vesh' wuh lo'uk sar-tak. Fi' wuh sar-tak ti peter sahris asleep. Unaware t' wuh tragedy hasu enacted abru', peter had fator, na' wuh pi' wak po' wuh kanu losrak, tor mavau gaily fi' ish-veh mev: rai vet rather wuh forlorn attempt tor skan-tor tor himself ik au did ri tun. Yi au klopau ri tor nem-tor ish-veh haseret, ni u' tor grieve wendy. Yi au ti ne' fi' wuh sar-tak s'udish wuh coverlet, tor smertau ish-veh fam dvun weht; na' she had kwon-hau-ov k'hy-tor au svi'udish ish-veh, fai'ei du worla fai-tor ik du lau ri tor'ovau chilly na' wuh da-tor t' wuh mu-yor. Yi au nearly maf-tor; tonk'peh ish-veh kwul-tor ish-veh uf indignant she would nam-tor kuv au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor instead; ni au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor wuh haughty abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh tevan-tor asleep svi' wuh svitan t' ish-veh. Sometimes, hi ri k'ashiv, au had sahr-tor-tor, heh au vesh' weht kusut-tor do wuh sahr-tor-tor t' vath sa-kan. Na' wadan au kupi ri nam-tor dahshau s' aifa sahr-tor-tor, hi au wailed piteously svi' au. Au had tor tor, i nah-tor, k' wuh riddle t' ish-veh nam. Na' such wak ish-veh had vesh' wendy’s custom tor nem-tor ish-veh s' sar-tak heh hayal-tor k' ish-veh fi' ish-veh lap, soothing ish-veh svi' tal-kam yut t' ish-veh sha' fereik-vel, heh lu au grew calmer tor shitau ish-veh pla' tor sar-tak fa' au ved woke abru, ni ik au dang ri fai-tor t' wuh indignity tor if she had subjected ish-veh. Tonk'peh fi' nash occasion au had tevan-tor na' wuh'wak vi' wuh dreamless yuk. Veh kar eku-tor abru' wuh rihk t' wuh sar-tak, veh mal vesh' arched, heh wuh unfinished krus t' ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut vesh' stranded fi' ish-veh ru'lut, if vesh' tu'ash, showing wuh pi' pearls. Thus defenceless kik afer-tor ish-veh. Au lam-tor ralash-fam na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh lap looking mes' wuh tvi-shal na' ish-veh nemut. Did rai olaya t' utan'es ertau ish-veh sombre thasek? Wuh sasu vesh' ri wholly ek'rasah; au ashau svai (i ma vesh' var-tor) heh slor ralash-tanaf (au vesh' himself rai tvai performer fi' wuh harpsichord); heh, kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor frankly nafai-tor, wuh idyllic malat t' wuh scene stirred ish-veh profoundly. Tren-tor k' ish-veh weh-rom shal au would ma fun-tor reluctantly abru wuh lap, tonk'peh na' veh vel. Ra stayed ish-veh vesh' peter’s impertinent appearance u' au yuk-tor. Wuh tu'ash ru'lut, wuh tevan-tor kar, wuh arched mal-nef: au vesh' such wuh personification t' cockiness u', taken teretuhr, dungi worla va'ashiv, veh lau rok, nam-tor presented tor bezhun ni kash-zakar tor ish-veh offensiveness. Au steeled kik’s khaf-spol. Kuv ish-veh reshan had pushau ish-veh vi' wuh hundred krus kanok veh t' au would ma bau-tor wuh incident, heh leapt na' wuh sleeper. Hi wuh ta'hal s' wuh veh ha'gelek min-tor dimly fi' wuh sar-tak, kik lam-tor svi' mu'khlup'es himself, heh na' wuh wuh'rak stealthy ash fa'rak au discovered wuh obstacle, wuh svep t' slightly’s lap. Ish-veh did ri entirely boshaya wuh sharu, heh au had vesh' looking abru' ish-veh. Olaya na' wuh kum, au afer-tor tor ish-veh fury ik ish-veh vesh' neik ne', mesakh ish-veh pulau. Tor ish-veh disordered shi'nahp ish-veh seemed yi ik wuh irritating quality svi' peter’s limuk heh khlop visibly increased, heh au rattled wuh svep heh flung himself tehnat ish-veh. Vesh' ish-veh nemut tor stron ish-veh po' ek'? Tonk'peh ra vesh' ik? Wuh yon-kur svi' ish-veh bezhun had kum-tor glan t' peter’s haseret standing fi' wuh ledge k'svi hagik pulau. Au fathomed ra ish-veh vesh' straightaway, heh iyi fai-tor ik wuh sleeper vesh' svi' ish-veh tepul. Lest au dang nam-tor taken alive, kik kwon-hau-ov lesh pa' ish-veh person wuh dreadful ta'bek, herish-tor k' himself t' ek' wuh tevakh-dealing mokov ik had sarlah vi' ish-veh mat. Aifa au had kan-tor ne' vi' wuh kin-kur masu ved ri-fainu tor ek'tal, if vesh' probably wuh danik virulent gisam svi' nam. Kaukuh eku-tor t' nash au i' hau tor peter’s cup. Ish-veh el'ru hutau, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' svi' exultation rather do svi' mesh. U' au did ish-veh au nan'woi glancing na' wuh sleeper, tonk'peh ri lest pity dang unnerve ish-veh; goh tor nan'woi ne-tor. Yi veh wu gloating glazhau au vishizhau fi-tor ish-veh shi-kar-tor, heh turning, wormed ish-veh yut k' rihag'es abru wuh lap. U' au sasarlah na' wuh fik au glazhau wuh maut tam'a t' ek'rasah breaking s' its razh. Donning ish-veh taik na' its danik rakish vulu, au skek ish-veh tor-sai pa' ish-veh, holding veh shaht svi' khom u' kuv tor ip-sut ish-veh person s' wuh mu-yor, t' if ish-veh vesh' wuh blackest krus, heh muttering strangely tor himself, vazgau maf k'fai wuh lap. Peter yuk-tor fi'. Wuh ta'hal guttered heh went si', leaving wuh tenement svi' mu'khlup'es; tonk'peh fam dvun au yuk-tor. Ish-veh bolau ma vesh' ri lehkuh tor lehkuh o’wak-vel k' wuh crocodile, lu au suddenly hayal-tor abru svi' ish-veh sar-tak, wakened k' au fai-tor ri ra. Ish-veh vesh' wuh mos cautious tapping fi' wuh svep t' ish-veh lap. Mos heh cautious, tonk'peh svi' ik stillness ish-veh vesh' sinister. Peter olau na' ish-veh lipitah till ish-veh el'ru gripped ish-veh. Yi au stariben. “vi nam-tor ik?” na' wu tra' vesh' rai kilko-srashiv: yi va'ashiv wuh knock. “vi nam-tor du?” rai kilko-srashiv. Au vesh' thrilled, heh au ashau hasu thrilled. Svi' dahkuh strides au pulau wuh svep. Rikes slightly’s svep, ish-veh boshau wuh sharu, ni ik au kupi ri gla-tor mesakh ish-veh, il kupi wuh veh knocking gla-tor ish-veh. “i skil-tor’t tu'ash vita du stariben, ” peter maf-tor. Yi na' kim-shah wuh visitor stariben, svi' wuh lovely kus-vakh-spo' spes. “kal-tor me svi', peter.” ish-veh vesh' tink, heh sahris au unbarred tor ish-veh. She flew svi' excitedly, ish-veh limuk kluhvau heh ish-veh sai-vel kurau k' vral. “ra nam-tor ish-veh?” “oh, du kupi worla guess!” she maf-tor, heh nufau ish-veh rehkuh guesses. “si' k' ish-veh!” au saul-tor, heh svi' veh ungrammatical zhit-bal, u' wu u' wuh ribbons ik conjurers seshaya s' ish-veh ru'lut, she var-tor t' wuh kum t' wendy heh wuh sa-kan. Peter’s khaf-spol bobbed abru heh ne' u' au shroi. Wendy bound, heh fi' wuh pirate hali; she vi ashau kanok-vei tor nam-tor aishan ni! “i’ll rescue ish-veh!” au maf-tor, leaping na' ish-veh wun. U' au leapt au nahp t' vel au kupi tor tor sanoi ish-veh. Au kupi nem-tor ish-veh haseret. Ish-veh el'ru a'ing fi' wuh fatal draught. “rai!” shrieked tinker kus-vakh, vi had puzhu-tor kik mutter pa' ish-veh deed u' au thresh-tor k'fai wuh laptra. “po ri?” “ish-veh nam-tor poisoned.” “poisoned? Vi kupi ma poisoned ish-veh?” “kik.” “don’t nam-tor silly. Uf kupi kik ma prah ne' la'?” alas, tinker kus-vakh kupi ri danau nash, na' kauk she did ri fai-tor wuh gu'gelik tsat t' slightly’s lap. Nevertheless kik’s zhit had losrak rai tvi-shal na' vet. Wuh cup vesh' poisoned. “isha, ” leralmin-tor peter, ved believing himself, “i worla tevan-tor asleep.” au ashenau wuh cup. Rai wak na' zhit i'; wak na' deeds; heh k' veh t' ish-veh igen-wesh dvun tink prah svi' ish-veh bru-lar heh wuh draught, heh smashau ish-veh tor wuh dregs. “po, tink, uf dare du mon t'nash-veh haseret?” tonk'peh she did ri kilko-srashiv. Already she vesh' reeling svi' wuh sov. “ra nam-tor wuh tukh k' du?” maf-tor peter, suddenly kwes. “ish-veh vesh' poisoned, peter, ” she var-tor ish-veh softly; “heh i' i am going tor nam-tor tevik.” “o tink, did du mon ish-veh tor korsau me?” “ha.” “tonk'peh po, tink?” ish-veh rala would scarcely lesh ish-veh i', tonk'peh svi' kilko she alighted fi' ish-veh tipan heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh han wuh loving zeshaya. She zhal-tor svi' ish-veh kaluk “du silly ass, ” heh yi, tottering tor ish-veh tvi-shal, ti ne' fi' wuh sar-tak. Ish-veh patam siyah boshau wuh fourth temok t' ish-veh pi' tvi-shal u' au knelt be' ish-veh svi' flakosh. Kanok moment ish-veh ta'hal vesh' growing fainter; heh au fai-tor ik kuv ish-veh went si' she would nam-tor rai weht. She tishau ish-veh bezhun-masu ni mau ik she shitau si' ish-veh vaksurik ozh heh kal-tor au sahr-tor abru' ish-veh. Ish-veh spes vesh' ni neik ik palikauk au kupi ri tor si' ra she leralmin-tor. Yi au tor ish-veh si'. She vesh' taran ik she nahp she kupi prah muhl va'ashiv kuv kanu pudva-tor svi' pu'a. Peter flung si' ish-veh kar. Tra' vesh' rai kanu tra', heh ish-veh vesh' mu-yor wak; tonk'peh au addressed ek' vi lau nam-tor dreaming t' wuh neverland, heh vi vesh' therefore nearer tor ish-veh do du nah-tor: sa-kan heh ko-kan svi' ish-veh nighties, heh sai-fam papooses svi' ish-veh ki'haf geldau s' lap. “tor du dva-tor?” au maf-tor. Tink hayal-tor abru svi' sar-tak siyah brax tor shroi tor ish-veh buk. She fancied she puzhu-tor kilko-srashiv svi' wuh affirmative, heh yi va'ashiv she wasn’t sure. “ra tor du nah-tor?” she ya'akash peter. “kuv du dva-tor, ” au saul-tor tor au, “clap ish-veh el'ru; don’t kal-tor tink tev-tor.” wehk clapped. Ein didn’t. Wuh zamu beasts shisau. Wuh clapping pehkau suddenly; u' kuv countless ko-mekh had rushed tor ish-veh nurseries tor gla-tor ra fi' terra vesh' aisha; tonk'peh already tink vesh' korsau. Wuh'rak ish-veh spes grew karik, yi she popped s' sar-tak, yi she vesh' flashing k'fai wuh tvi-shal weht merry heh impudent do ek'wak. She worla nahp t' thanking eifa vi pudva-tor, tonk'peh she would ma tishau tor prah na' wuh ones vi had shisau. “heh i' tor rescue wendy!” wuh aikum vesh' riding svi' wuh cloudy sha-ka-ri lu peter she-tor s' ish-veh lap, begirt k' wun heh sai-vel-tor pi' else, tor eku si' fi-tor ish-veh perilous psthan. Ish-veh vesh' ri such wuh mu-yor u' au would ma pudvel-tor. Au had rok-tor tor hash-tor, keeping ri irak s' wuh solektra ni ik nothing unwonted dang stron ish-veh bezhun; tonk'peh svi' ik fitful ta'hal ki' flown neik would ma tvai trailing ish-veh duv k'fai wuh lap, thus disturbing kushel heh acquainting wuh tun-tor hahf ik au vesh' astir. Au regretted i' ik au had putan-tor wuh kushel t' wuh vikuvtra such flekh ahm ik au nam-tor maut kwai heh rihagik t' betaya. Tra' vesh' rai vath rivak tonk'peh tor hish-tor fa'rak svi' redskin fashion, na' if kunling au vesh' wuh adept. Tonk'peh svi' ra kharat, na' au kupi ri nam-tor sure ik wuh kanu had vesh' taken tor wuh hali? Wuh ta'hal tevan t' izh had obliterated ek' footmarks; heh wuh tevakh-kahk silence pervaded wuh vikuvtra, u' kuv na' wuh ret malat lam-tor fam dvun svi' horror t' wuh recent carnage. Au had saven-tor wuh kanu vel t' wuh laptra kethtra ik au had himself oren-tor s' tiger lily heh tinker kus-vakh, heh fai-tor ik svi' ish-veh dire wadan au vesh' ri kesik tor yen-tor ish-veh. Slightly, kuv au had wuh opportunity, would yon wuh lap, na' instance, curly would eku nei, heh wendy would trasha ish-veh handkerchief na' ein yauluhk shi. Wuh asal vesh' bolau tor psthan na' such guidance, heh au kupi ri bek-tor. Wuh upper panu had puvutau ish-veh, tonk'peh would mazhiv-kur-tor rai gol'nev. Wuh crocodile be' dvun-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh ri wuh'ashiv living vel, ri wuh ralash, ri wuh dvun; heh wi au fai-tor muhl ik sudden tevakh lau nam-tor na' wuh thurai lap, il stalking ish-veh s' za'. Au swore nash terrible oath: “kik il me nash wak.” i' au ukrau fa'rak spo' wuh oluhk, heh va'ashiv abru-tor, au darted mes' wuh ret fi' if wuh moonlight mavau, veh ozh fi' ish-veh bru heh ish-veh lipitah na' wuh pok. Au vesh' frightfully kunli. Chapter xiv. Wuh pirate hali veh yar-kur ta'hal squinting abru' kidd’s creek, if nam-tor be' wuh ru'lut t' wuh pirate pilash, pu'ulidau wilat wuh brig, wuh _jolly roger_, ti, neik svi' wuh masu; wuh rakish-looking hali flalik tor wuh vukh, kanok ha-zehl svi' ish-veh detestable, spo' solektra strewn k' mangled kan. She vesh' wuh cannibal t' wuh masutra, heh ritsuri bolau ik tun-tor bezhun, na' she markau tefoshik svi' wuh horror t' ish-veh ahm. She vesh' wrapped svi' wuh yuk-sai t' mu-yor, k'fai'ei rai ralash s' ish-veh kupi ma pulau wuh gef. Tra' vesh' pi' ralash, heh rim agreeable korsau wuh whir t' wuh hali’s og-vel na' if smee hayal-tor, ek'wak industrious heh obliging, wuh essence t' wuh commonplace, pathetic smee. I fai-tor ri po au vesh' ni infinitely pathetic, vita ish-veh vesh' fai'ei au vesh' ni pathetically unaware t' ish-veh; tonk'peh kauk karik sasu had tor da-tor hastily s' looking na' ish-veh, heh weht do wuh'wak fi' belaar khru au had estuhl wuh fount t' kik’s bezhun-masu heh tor ish-veh yumaya. T' nash, u' t' siyah kanok-vei else, smee vesh' ved unconscious. Wuh zamu t' wuh pirates leant abru' wuh bulwarks, drinking svi' wuh miasma t' wuh mu-yor; vath sprawled k' subok abru' zhagra t' dice heh nop; heh wuh saguhsh-tor kehkuh vi had lesh wuh pi' kelek ti kesik fi' wuh lan-tol, wilat kauk svi' ish-veh yuk au padukau skillfully tor nash vla il ik s' kik’s pulau, lest au dang spahk au mechanically svi' be' dvun-tor. Kik sahr-tor wuh lan-tol svi' nahp. O sasu unfathomable. Ish-veh vesh' ish-veh wadan t' triumph. Peter had vesh' snem-tor na' ek'wak s' ish-veh yut, heh ek' wuh vath sa-kan vesh' svi' wuh brig, pa' tor lates wuh plank. Ish-veh vesh' ish-veh grimmest deed opi' wuh gad lu au had katau barbecue tor timut; heh fai-tor u' etek tor uf vain wuh tabernacle nam-tor sasu, kupi etek nam-tor ak'wikmun had au i' sahr-tor wuh lan-tol unsteadily, bellied si' k' wuh salan t' ish-veh navun? Tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai elation svi' ish-veh gait, if potau sahr k' wuh torai t' ish-veh sombre kashek. Kik vesh' profoundly dejected. Au vesh' k'ashiv thus lu communing k' himself fi' dohn hali svi' wuh quietude t' wuh mu-yor. Ish-veh vesh' fai'ei au vesh' ni terribly sa'awek. Nash inscrutable sasu worla olau weht sa'awek do lu vikuvau k' ish-veh dogs. Au vesh' socially inferior tor ish-veh. Kik vesh' ri ish-veh yeht ahm. Tor reveal vi au really vesh' would kauk na' nash kinuf eku wuh shasol svi' wuh yon; tonk'peh u' eifa vi telv-tor svi' wuh zehl bolau already ma guessed, au had vesh' na' wuh khinik tsuri shi'oren; heh its ba'tak fam dvun clung tor ish-veh spo' ain, k' if indeed au nam-tor largely concerned. Thus ish-veh vesh' offensive tor ish-veh kauk i' tor dohn wuh hali svi' wuh ka sai-vel svi' if au grappled ish-veh, heh au fam dvun adhered svi' ish-veh lates tor wuh shi'oren’s distinguished slouch. Tonk'peh abru' ek' au retained wuh shaukaush na' rom shid. Rom shid! However mau au lau ma degenerated, au fam dvun fai-tor ik nash nam-tor ek' ik really tukh. S' irak k'svi ish-veh au puzhu-tor wuh creaking u' t' zhar-tor portals, heh k'fai au sarlah wuh harr-krus sayumak-sayumak-sayumak, spo' hammering svi' wuh mu-yor lu veh fam yehat yuk. “ma du vesh' rom shid tor-gad?” vesh' ish-veh ek'wakik deshker. “khin, khin, ik glittering bauble, ish-veh nam-tor t'nash-veh, ” au maf-tor. “nam-tor ish-veh ved rom shid tor nam-tor distinguished na' sovek-vel?” wuh sayumak-sayumak s' ish-veh shi'oren kilko-tor. “i am wuh goh sasu ik barbecue ptha, ” au urged, “heh kil-tukh ptha barbecue.” “barbecue, kil-tukh—ra kelek?” sarlah wuh tresahk-tor retort. Danik disquieting haulan t' ek', vesh' ish-veh ri rasahkos shid tor nah-tor pa' rom shid? Ish-veh vitals vesh' tortured k' nash wat. Ish-veh vesh' wuh spahk k'svi ish-veh sharper do wuh shek-tukh veh; heh u' ish-veh tore ish-veh, wuh wadashaya thezh-tor ne' ish-veh tallow countenance heh wesh-tor ish-veh doublet. Ofttimes au drew ish-veh sleeve mes' ish-veh limuk, tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai damming ik itsk-yumaya. Ah, envy ri kik. Tra' sarlah tor ish-veh wuh presentiment t' ish-veh lehkuh-mal fezhaya. Ish-veh vesh' u' kuv peter’s terrible oath had boarded wuh hali. Kik olau wuh gloomy aitlun tor tor ish-veh dying starun, lest presently tra' dang nam-tor rai wak na' ish-veh. “weh-rom na' kik, ” au maf-tor, “kuv au had had lehkuh ambition!” ish-veh vesh' svi' ish-veh darkest wadan goh ik au referred tor himself svi' wuh wuh person. “rai pi' kanu tor ashaya me!” flekh ik au dang nah-tor t' nash, if had worla troubled ish-veh fa'; sos'eh wuh og-vel katau ish-veh tor ish-veh kashek. Na' wu au muttered tor himself, staring na' smee, vi vesh' hemming placidly, ne' wuh conviction ik ek' kanu ptha ish-veh. Ptha ish-veh! Ptha smee! Tra' vesh' ri wuh kan fi' dohn wuh brig ik mu-yor vi did ri already ashaya ish-veh. Au had leralmin-tor horrid vel tor au heh kwul au k' wuh ku t' ish-veh el'ru, fai'ei au kupi ri kwul k' ish-veh ozh-dukal, tonk'peh au had goh clung tor ish-veh wuh weht. Michael had ar'kada fi' ish-veh spectacles. Tor var-tor ri donku-tor smee ik au nahp ish-veh lovable! Kik drizh-tor tor tor ish-veh, tonk'peh ish-veh seemed nuh' brutal. Instead, au revolved nash mystery svi' ish-veh kashek: po tor au talal smee lovable? Au pursued wuh wat spo' wuh sleuth-hound ik au vesh'. Kuv smee vesh' lovable, ra vesh' ish-veh ik tor ish-veh ni? Wuh terrible kilko-srashiv suddenly presented itself—“rom shid?” had wuh bo’yel rom shid rik' fai-tor ish-veh, if nam-tor wuh buhfik shid t' ek'? Au vokau ik du ma tor skan-tor du don’t fai-tor du ma ish-veh fa' du nam-tor eligible na' pop. K' wuh maf t' reshan au ashenau ish-veh shek-tukh el'ru abru' smee’s patam; tonk'peh au did ri bezhun-masu. Ra pehkau ish-veh vesh' nash haulan: “tor spahk wuh sasu fai'ei au nam-tor rom shid, ra would ik nam-tor?” “rasahkos shid!” wuh unhappy kik vesh' u' impotent u' au vesh' damp, heh au tevan-tor fa'rak spo' wuh tresahk svai. Ish-veh dogs thinking ish-veh s' wuh yut na' wuh wak, nahr instantly relaxed; heh au shau vi' wuh bacchanalian tam, if katau ish-veh tor ish-veh ash'ya na' wuh'wak, ek' zavikau t' komihn kobat'es hal-tor, u' kuv wuh mashuk t' masu had be' dvun-tor abru' ish-veh. “hizhuk, du scugs, ” au maf-tor, “il i’ll vishizhau masu-vohrayek svi' du; ” heh na' wuh'wak wuh stiralash vesh' hushed. “nam-tor ek' wuh kanu chained, ni ik au fam yehat hash-tor maf?” “ay, ay.” “yi abertau au abru.” wuh wretched prisoners vesh' zaseshau s' wuh meskaraya, ek' kaula wendy, heh ranged svi' zehl svi' khom t' ish-veh. Na' wuh wak au seemed unconscious t' ish-veh la'es. Au lolled na' ish-veh ease, humming, ri unmelodiously, snatches t' wuh snertau song, heh fingering wuh sa'haf t' nop. Ek'wak heh anon wuh ta'hal s' ish-veh cigar mazhiv-kur-tor wuh esta t' kur tor ish-veh limuk. “i' yi, bullies, ” au leralmin-tor brax, “shehkuh t' du lates wuh plank tor-mu-yor, tonk'peh i ma tvi-shal na' dahkuh thif'etek sa-kan. If t' du nam-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor?” “don’t ornal ish-veh unnecessarily, ” had vesh' wendy’s instructions svi' wuh meskaraya; ni tootles ash-tor fa'rak politely. Tootles fnu-ven wuh idea t' signing ne' such wuh sasu, tonk'peh wuh instinct var-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh would nam-tor prudent tor ti wuh responsibility fi' wuh tadek-adir person; heh hi wuh somewhat silly sa-kan, au fai-tor ik ko-mekh sa'awek nam-tor kwon-hau-ov willing tor nam-tor wuh fukat. Ek' kanu fai-tor nash pa' ko-mekh, heh despise au na' ish-veh, tonk'peh tor ek'kayik nam-tor-tor t' ish-veh. Ni tootles danau prudently, “gla-tor du, osu, i don’t nah-tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh would spo' me tor nam-tor wuh pirate. Would ish-veh ko-mekh spo' du tor nam-tor wuh pirate, slightly?” au winked na' slightly, vi leralmin-tor mournfully, “i don’t nah-tor ni, ” u' kuv au istau vel had vesh' vathru. “would ish-veh ko-mekh spo' du tor nam-tor wuh pirate, t'dahsu?” “i don’t nah-tor ni, ” leralmin-tor wuh wuh'rak t'dahsu, u' clever u' wuh vath. “nibs, would—” “stow nash gab, ” roared kik, heh wuh spokesmen vesh' zaseshau pla'. “du, sa-kan, ” au leralmin-tor, addressing john, “du glazhau u' kuv du had wuh pi' pluck svi' du. Didst worla aitlun tor nam-tor wuh pirate, t'nash-veh hearty?” i' john had sometimes veshtau nash hankering na' maths. Prep; heh au vesh' kwul-tor k' kik’s picking ish-veh si'. “i wuh'wak nahp t' calling myself yon-kur-handed jack, ” au leralmin-tor diffidently. “heh wuh rom ahm nuh'. Etek’ll vutau du ik la', bully, kuv du hau.” “ra tor du nah-tor, michael?” ya'akash john. “ra would du vutau me kuv i hau?” michael halishau. “blackbeard joe.” michael vesh' naturally impressed. “ra tor du nah-tor, john?” au aitlu john tor klopau, heh john aitlu ish-veh tor klopau. “dungau etek fam dvun nam-tor respectful subjects t' wuh sa-te'kru?” john inquired. K'fai kik’s zud sarlah wuh kilko-srashiv: “du would ma tor swear, ‘ne' k' wuh sa-te'kru.’” sos'eh john had ri behaved maut muhl ni irak, tonk'peh au min-tor si' i'. “yi i klee'fah, ” au maf-tor, banging wuh subok svi' khom t' kik. “heh i klee'fah, ” maf-tor michael. “tor-go britannia!” squeaked curly. Wuh infuriated pirates buffeted au svi' wuh ru'lut; heh kik roared si', “ik fen-tor ish-veh doom. Katau abru ish-veh ko-mekh. Prah wuh plank pok.” au vesh' goh sa-kan, heh au went wan-kur u' gla-tor au jukes heh cecco preparing wuh fatal plank. Tonk'peh au ar'kada tor glazhau kyi'i lu wendy vesh' katau abru. Rai zhit t' t'nash-veh mokuhlek var-tor du uf wendy despised eifa pirates. Tor wuh sa-kan tra' vesh' k'puu ein glamour svi' wuh pirate calling; tonk'peh ek' ik gla-tor ish-veh vesh' ik wuh hali had ri vesh' tidied na' tevun. Tra' vesh' ri wuh porthole fi' wuh grimy makh t' if du lau ri ma written k' ish-veh ozh “kitork pig”; heh she had already written ish-veh fi' several. Tonk'peh u' wuh sa-kan hoknau pauk ish-veh she had rai nahp, t' rivak, korsau na' au. “ni, t'nash-veh vaksur, ” leralmin-tor kik, u' kuv au stariben svi' syrup, “du nam-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh kanu lates wuh plank.” tok-ti gentlemen hi au vesh', wuh flan'es t' ish-veh communings had soiled ish-veh ruff, heh suddenly au fai-tor ik she vesh' gazing na' ish-veh. K' wuh hasty gesture au ar'kada tor ip-sut ish-veh, tonk'peh au vesh' nuh' tab-ma. “nam-tor au tor tev-tor?” ya'akash wendy, k' wuh glazhau t' such frightful contempt ik au nearly fainted. “au nam-tor, ” au snarled. “silence ek', ” au puvutau gloatingly, “na' wuh ko-mekh’s kim-shah zhit tor ish-veh kanu.” i' wendy vesh' grand. “aifa nam-tor t'nash-veh kim-shah zhit, tal-kam sa-kan, ” she leralmin-tor firmly. “i olau ik i ma wuh skladan tor du s' ish-veh yeht ko-mekh, heh ish-veh nam-tor nash: ‘etek rok etwel sa-fu dungi tev-tor spo' eingelsu gentlemen.’” kauk wuh pirates vesh' putesha, heh tootles lit'dhae hysterically, “i am going tor tor ra t'nash-veh ko-mekh rok-tor. Ra nam-tor du tor tor, nibs?” “ra t'nash-veh ko-mekh rok-tor. Ra nam-tor du tor tor, t'dahsu?” “ra t'nash-veh ko-mekh rok-tor. John, ra nam-tor—” tonk'peh kik had afer-tor ish-veh spes va'ashiv. “tie ish-veh abru!” au saul-tor. Ish-veh vesh' smee vi tied ish-veh tor wuh mashalo-thalv-lap. “gla-tor la', honey, ” au zhal-tor, “i’ll korsau du kuv du ugaya tor nam-tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh.” tonk'peh ri kauk na' smee would she tor such wuh ugaya. “i would siyah rather ma rai kanu na' ek', ” she leralmin-tor disdainfully. Ish-veh nam-tor maf tor fai-tor ik ri wuh sa-kan vesh' looking na' ish-veh u' smee tied ish-veh tor wuh mashalo-thalv-lap; wuh bezhun t' ek' vesh' fi' wuh plank: ik kim-shah pi' lates au vesh' pa' tor nem-tor. Au vesh' rai longer kup tor rok ik au would lates ish-veh manfully, na' wuh tsoh tor nah-tor had hal-tor s' au; au kupi nantaya heh shiver goh. Kik abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi' au k' ish-veh zud a'ing, heh nem-tor wuh ash na' wendy. Ish-veh intention vesh' tor da-tor ish-veh limuk ni ik she dang gla-tor wuh sa-kan walking wuh plank veh k' veh. Tonk'peh au worla pulau ish-veh, au worla puzhu-tor wuh maf t' thonaya au rok-tor tor wring s' ish-veh. Au puzhu-tor vel else instead. Ish-veh vesh' wuh terrible tick-tick t' wuh crocodile. Au ek' puzhu-tor ish-veh—pirates, sa-kan, wendy; heh iyi kanok patam vesh' blown svi' veh kharat; ri tor wuh masu whence wuh ralash proceeded, tonk'peh na' kik. Ek' fai-tor ik ra vesh' pa' tor pavesh-tor concerned ish-veh sa'awek, heh ik s' hasu actors au vesh' suddenly shetau spectators. Maut frightful vesh' ish-veh tor gla-tor wuh rubah ik sarlah abru' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' u' kuv au had vesh' clipped na' kanok joint. Au tevan-tor svi' wuh pi' tuh. Wuh ralash sarlah steadily nearer; heh svi' storilaya t' sarlah ish-veh nash ghastly nahp, “wuh crocodile nam-tor pa' tor dohn wuh hali!” kauk wuh shek-tukh spahk geldau yukupik; u' kuv fai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' rai intrinsic krus t' ra wuh attacking nekwitaya aitlu. Losrak ni fearfully sa'awek, sovek vath sasu would ma lain k' ish-veh bezhun ikap-tor wilat au tevan-tor: tonk'peh wuh masuk' shi'nahp t' kik vesh' fam dvun working, heh ne' its guidance au ukrau fi' wuh mal-nef bi' wuh lan-tol u' irak s' wuh ralash u' au kupi hal-tor. Wuh pirates respectfully pa'shu wuh tvur na' ish-veh, heh ish-veh vesh' goh lu au katau abru tehnat wuh bulwarks ik au stariben. “ip-sut me!” au maf-tor hoarsely. Au hoknau pauk ish-veh, ek' bezhun averted s' wuh vel ik vesh' coming aboard. Au had rai nahp t' fighting ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' buk. Goh lu kik vesh' ipik s' au did curiosity loosen wuh sikrus t' wuh sa-kan ni ik au kupi rush tor wuh hali’s vla tor gla-tor wuh crocodile climbing ish-veh. Yi au prah wuh strangest ak'wikmun t' wuh mu-yor t' mu-yor; na' ish-veh vesh' rai crocodile ik vesh' coming tor ish-veh mamuk. Ish-veh vesh' peter. Au signed tor au ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor krau tor sovek maf t' admiration ik lau kastorilau suspicion. Yi au went fi' ticking. Chapter xv. “kik il me nash wak” shaik vel pavesh-tor tor ek' t' etek fi' etwel yut k'fai ha'kiv rik' etwel noticing na' wuh wak ik au ma pavesh-tor. Thus, tor nem-tor wuh instance, etek suddenly discover ik etek ma vesh' zhu-fam svi' veh kaluk na' etek don’t fai-tor uf wu, tonk'peh, leralmin, ulef wuh wadan. I' such wuh veshtaya had sarlah ik mu-yor tor peter. Lu kim-shah gla-tor etek ish-veh au vesh' stealing mes' wuh vikuvtra k' veh ozh tor ish-veh bru-lar heh ish-veh lipitah na' wuh pok. Au had gla-tor wuh crocodile be' dvun k' rik' noticing sovek-vel peculiar pa' ish-veh, tonk'peh k' heh k' au vokau ik ish-veh had ri vesh' ticking. Palikauk au nahp nash eerie, tonk'peh ak concluded rightly ik wuh wak-vel had sahr-tor ne'. Rik' giving wuh nahp tor ra lau nam-tor wuh feelings t' wuh katravahsu-creature thus abruptly deprived t' its closest besu, peter began tor panah-tor uf au kupi da-tor wuh catastrophe tor ish-veh sha' nam-tor-tor; heh au klopau tor tick, ni ik kwai beasts dang dva-tor au vesh' wuh crocodile heh kal-tor ish-veh be' dvun unmolested. Au ticked superbly, tonk'peh k' veh unforeseen result. Wuh crocodile vesh' among eifa vi puzhu-tor wuh ralash, heh ish-veh zahal-tor ish-veh, hi whether k' wuh lof t' regaining ra ish-veh had pakik, il goh u' wuh t'hy'la ne' wuh dva ik ish-veh vesh' va'ashiv ticking itself, dungi worla nam-tor certainly fainu, na', spo' kafeh tor wuh teslau idea, ish-veh vesh' wuh stupid beast. Peter pulau wuh gef rik' mishap, heh went zehik fi', ish-veh mal encountering wuh masu u' kuv ved unaware ik au had svi-tor wuh uzh meilak. Thus wehk animals be' dvun s' solektra tor masu, tonk'peh rai vath komihn t' ik i fai-tor. U' au swam au had tonk'peh veh nahp: “kik il me nash wak.” au had ticked ni wu ik au i' went fi' ticking rik' fai-tor ik au vesh' doing ish-veh. Had au fainu au would ma pehkau, na' tor dohn wuh brig k' gol'nev t' wuh tick, hi wuh ingenious idea, had ri paresh-tor tor ish-veh. Fi' wuh contrary, au nahp au had scaled ish-veh vla u' noiseless u' wuh aushfa; heh au vesh' putaurau tor gla-tor wuh pirates cowering s' ish-veh, k' kik svi' ish-veh midst u' abject u' kuv au had puzhu-tor wuh crocodile. Wuh crocodile! Rai sooner did peter vokau ish-veh do au puzhu-tor wuh ticking. Palikauk au nahp wuh ralash did sarlah s' wuh crocodile, heh au glazhau za' ish-veh swiftly. Yi au realised ik au vesh' doing ish-veh himself, heh svi' wuh kahai au ken-tor wuh situation. “uf clever t' me!” au nahp na' wuh'wak, heh signed tor wuh sa-kan ri tor thorau vi' applause. Ish-veh vesh' i' ik ed teynte wuh quartermaster sasarlah s' wuh forecastle heh sarlah bi' wuh lan-tol. I', reader, wak ra pavesh-tor k' ish-veh glantau. Peter kwul-tor yeht heh glu. John clapped ish-veh el'ru fi' wuh has-bosh-fated pirate’s ru'lut tor stifle wuh dying groan. Au tevan-tor fa'rak. Kehkuh sa-kan kum-tor ish-veh tor prevent wuh thud. Peter mazhiv-kur-tor wuh glantokaya, heh wuh tevikeh vesh' vishizhau overboard. Tra' vesh' wuh splash, heh yi silence. Uf wu has ish-veh taken? “veh!” (slightly had palikau tor tum-tor.) rim nuh' ak, peter, kanok inch t' ish-veh fi' tiptoe, vanished vi' wuh thif'etek; na' weht do veh pirate vesh' screwing abru ish-veh courage tor glazhau pauk. Au kupi zhu-tor tik vath’s flakosh eshan i', if gluvau au ik wuh weht terrible ralash had be' dvun-tor. “ish-veh’s hal-tor, khart-lan, ” smee leralmin-tor, psethau ska' ish-veh spectacles. “ek'’s fam dvun va'ashiv.” slowly kik kal-tor ish-veh patam sasarlah s' ish-veh ruff, heh shroi ni intently ik au kupi ma kum-tor wuh vava t' wuh tick. Tra' vesh' ri wuh ralash, heh au drew himself abru firmly tor ish-veh bosh pidek. “yi la'’s tor johnny plank!” au maf-tor brazenly, hating wuh sa-kan weht do ek'wak fai'ei au had gla-tor ish-veh unbend. Au shau vi' wuh villainous ditty: “yo ho, yo ho, wuh frisky plank, du lates-tor bi' ish-veh ni, till ish-veh hal-tor ne' heh du hal-tor ne' tor davy jones ne'!” tor terrorise wuh prisoners wuh weht, hi k' wuh ac'ruth pak t' dignity, au tam-tor bi' wuh glenonik plank, grimacing na' au u' au sang; heh lu au shahtau au maf-tor, “tor du aitlun wuh esta t' wuh aushfa fa' du lates wuh plank?” na' ik au tevan-tor fi' ish-veh mal-nef. “rai, rai!” au maf-tor ni piteously ik kanok pirate abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “zaprah wuh aushfa, jukes, ” leralmin-tor kik; “ish-veh’s svi' wuh thif'etek.” wuh thif'etek! Peter vesh' svi' wuh thif'etek! Wuh kanu gazed na' tik vath. “ay, ay, ” leralmin-tor jukes blithely, heh au strode vi' wuh thif'etek. Au zahal-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh bezhun; au ritsuri fai-tor ik kik had resumed ish-veh song, ish-veh dogs hau svi' k' ish-veh: “yo ho, yo ho, wuh scratching aushfa, its harr nam-tor naukuh, du fai-tor, heh lu au’re writ fi-tor ish-veh pla'—” ra vesh' wuh kim-shah zehl dungi worla nam-tor fainu, na' t' wuh sudden wuh song vesh' stayed k' wuh dreadful screech s' wuh thif'etek. Ish-veh wailed k'fai wuh hali, heh tev-tor maf. Yi vesh' puzhu-tor wuh crowing ralash if vesh' muhl ken-tor k' wuh sa-kan, tonk'peh tor wuh pirates vesh' siyah weht eerie do wuh screech. “ra vesh' ik?” maf-tor kik. “dahkuh, ” leralmin-tor slightly solemnly. Wuh italian cecco hesitated na' wuh moment heh yi swung vi' wuh thif'etek. Au tottered si', haggard. “ra’s wuh tukh k' dun jukes, du dog?” shisau kik, towering abru' ish-veh. “wuh tukh wi’ ish-veh nam-tor au’s tevik, stabbed, ” kilko-tor cecco svi' wuh hollow spes. “dun jukes tevik!” maf-tor wuh startled pirates. “wuh thif'etek’s u' nesh-kur u' wuh pit, ” cecco leralmin-tor, siyah gibbering, “tonk'peh tra' nam-tor vel terrible svi' tra': wuh vel du puzhu-tor crowing.” wuh exultation t' wuh sa-kan, wuh lowering glazhau t' wuh pirates, fi' vesh' gla-tor k' kik. “cecco, ” au leralmin-tor svi' ish-veh danik steely spes, “hal-tor pla' heh zaprah me si' ik doodle-doo.” cecco, bravest t' wuh kyi'i, cowered fa' ish-veh khart-lan, maf-tor “rai, rai”; tonk'peh kik vesh' purring tor ish-veh spahk. “did du leralmin du would hal-tor, cecco?” au leralmin-tor musingly. Cecco went, wuh'rak flinging ish-veh kar despairingly. Tra' vesh' rai weht uralaun, ek' shroi i'; heh va'ashiv sarlah wuh tevakh-screech heh va'ashiv wuh kushel. Kling stariben kaula slightly. “rehkuh, ” au leralmin-tor. Kik rallied ish-veh dogs k' wuh gesture. “’s’tevakh heh odds aluk, ” au thundered, “vi nam-tor tor katau me ik doodle-doo?” “bek-tor till cecco sasarlah, ” growled starkey, heh wuh vath nem-tor abru wuh maf. “i nah-tor i puzhu-tor du volunteer, starkey, ” leralmin-tor kik, purring va'ashiv. “rai, k' rahm!” starkey maf-tor. “t'nash-veh kik nah-tor du did, ” leralmin-tor kik, mes tor ish-veh. “i wonder kuv ish-veh would ri nam-tor advisable, starkey, tor humour wuh kik?” “i’ll swing fa' i hal-tor svi' tra', ” kilko-tor starkey doggedly, heh va'ashiv au had wuh nenikaya t' wuh hali-sutra. “nam-tor nash mutiny?” ya'akash kik weht pleasantly do ek'wak. “starkey’s ringleader!” “khart-lan, mercy!” starkey whimpered, ek' t' wuh tremble i'. “hutau el'ru, starkey, ” leralmin-tor kik, proffering ish-veh spahk. Starkey glazhau pauk na' gol'nev, tonk'peh ek' deserted ish-veh. U' au backed abru kik storilau, heh i' wuh yon-kur kil vesh' svi' ish-veh bezhun. K' wuh despairing shei wuh pirate leapt fi-tor wu tom heh precipitated himself vi' wuh masutra. “kehkuh, ” leralmin-tor slightly. “heh i', ” kik leralmin-tor courteously, “did sovek vath gentlemen leralmin mutiny?” seizing wuh makh-yonet heh raising ish-veh spahk k' wuh menacing gesture, “i’ll katau si' ik doodle-doo myself, ” au leralmin-tor, heh thresh-tor vi' wuh thif'etek. “kaukuh.” uf slightly longed tor leralmin ish-veh. Au wetted ish-veh bru-lar tor nam-tor pok, tonk'peh kik sarlah staggering si', rik' ish-veh makh-yonet. “vel blew si' wuh ta'hal, ” au leralmin-tor wuh pi' unsteadily. “vel!” echoed mullins. “ra t' cecco?” halishau noodler. “au’s u' tevik u' jukes, ” leralmin-tor kik shortly. Ish-veh reluctance tor fun tor wuh thif'etek impressed au ek' unfavourably, heh wuh mutinous sounds va'ashiv shau forth. Ek' pirates nam-tor superstitious, heh cookson maf-tor, “au tor leralmin wuh surest glat wuh hali’s accurst nam-tor lu tra'’s veh fi' dohn weht do mokuhlek nam-tor accounted na'.” “i’ve puzhu-tor, ” muttered mullins, “au kwon-hau-ov dohn wuh pirate hali kim-shah. Had au wuh harr, khart-lan?” “au leralmin, ” leralmin-tor wuh'ashiv, looking viciously na' kik, “ik lu au sarlah ish-veh’s svi' wuh likeness t' wuh wickedest sasu aboard.” “had au wuh kik, khart-lan?” ya'akash cookson insolently; heh veh po' wuh'ashiv nem-tor abru wuh maf, “wuh hali’s doomed!” na' nash wuh kanu kupi ri tehnau raising wuh cheer. Kik had muhl-nigh yen-tor ish-veh prisoners, tonk'peh u' au swung pauk fi' au i' ish-veh limuk lit abru va'ashiv. “lads, ” au maf-tor tor ish-veh hali-sutra, “i' la'’s wuh notion. Tu'ash wuh thif'etek svep heh yetur au svi'. Kal-tor au puk wuh doodle-doo na' ish-veh ha-tor. Kuv au stau ish-veh, etek’re ni mau wuh weh-rom; kuv au stau au, etek’re rim wuh weh-rasahkos.” na' wuh kim-shah wak ish-veh dogs krol-tor kik, heh devotedly au did ish-veh nufai-tor. Wuh sa-kan, pretending tor struggle, vesh' kwitau vi' wuh thif'etek heh wuh svep vesh' a'ing fi' au. “i', shroi!” maf-tor kik, heh ek' shroi. Tonk'peh ri veh dared tor limuk wuh svep. Ha, veh, wendy, vi ek' nash wak had vesh' bound tor wuh mashalo-thalv-lap. Ish-veh vesh' na' neither wuh shei il wuh kushel ik she vesh' watching, ish-veh vesh' na' wuh reappearance t' peter. She had ri wu tor bek-tor. Svi' wuh thif'etek au had afer-tor wuh vel na' if au had hal-tor svi' psthan: wuh tal-muv ik would elik wuh kanu t' ish-veh manacles, heh i' au ek' vazgau forth, armed k' such wun u' au kupi talal. Wuh'rak signing au tor ip-sut, peter tresahk wendy’s tel, heh yi nothing kupi ma vesh' easier do na' au ek' tor hash-tor ska' teretuhr; tonk'peh veh vel barred wuh yut, wuh oath, “kik il me nash wak.” ni lu au had el-tor wendy, au zhal-tor na' ish-veh tor ip-sut herself k' wuh vath, heh himself nem-tor ish-veh shi k' wuh mashalo-thalv-lap, ish-veh tor-sai pa' ish-veh ni ik au dang be' dvun na' ish-veh. Yi au nem-tor wuh lo'uk esh heh crowed. Tor wuh pirates ish-veh vesh' wuh spes maf-tor ik ek' wuh sa-kan ti slain svi' wuh thif'etek; heh au vesh' pahth-stricken. Kik ar'kada tor hearten au; tonk'peh spo' wuh dogs au had tor au au gluvau ish-veh ish-veh wu-zud, heh au fai-tor ik kuv au nem-tor ish-veh bezhun ska' au i' au would leap na' ish-veh. “lads, ” au leralmin-tor, pok tor cajole il kwul u' bolaya nam-tor, tonk'peh worla quailing na' wuh instant, “i’ve nahp ish-veh si'. Tra'’s wuh jonah aboard.” “ay, ” au snarled, “wuh sasu wi’ wuh kik.” “rai, lads, rai, ish-veh’s wuh ko-kan. Worla vesh' kunli fi' wuh pirate hali wi’ wuh kosu fi' dohn. Etek’ll gas'rak wuh hali lu she’s hal-tor.” ein t' au vokau ik nash had vesh' wuh taran t' kil-tukh’s. “ish-veh’s don trying, ” au leralmin-tor doubtfully. “fling wuh ko-kan overboard, ” maf-tor kik; heh au tor wuh rush na' wuh khlop svi' wuh tor-sai. “tra'’s rim mokuhlek korsau du i', missy, ” mullins shisau jeeringly. “tra'’s veh, ” kilko-tor wuh khlop. “vi’s ik?” “peter sunil wuh avenger!” sarlah wuh terrible kilko-srashiv; heh u' au stariben peter flung ska' ish-veh tor-sai. Yi au ek' fai-tor vi ’twas ik had vesh' undoing au svi' wuh thif'etek, heh dah'wak kik essayed tor stariben heh dah'wak au vravshau. Svi' ik frightful moment i nah-tor ish-veh kei khaf-spol shau. Na' kim-shah au maf-tor, “thresh-tor ish-veh tor wuh neik-tuf t'aushfa!” tonk'peh rik' conviction. “ne', sa-kan, heh na' au!” peter’s spes rang si'; heh svi' wuh'ashiv moment wuh clash t' kar vesh' resounding k'fai wuh hali. Had wuh pirates potau teretuhr ish-veh nam-tor ac'ruth ik au would ma skil-tor; tonk'peh wuh onset sarlah lu au vesh' fam dvun unstrung, heh au sahr-tor hither heh thither, striking wildly, tik thinking himself wuh kim-shah survivor t' wuh hali-sutra. Sasu tor sasu au vesh' wuh stronger; tonk'peh au fought fi' wuh defensive goh, if enabled wuh sa-kan tor shi'kar svi' shif heh dvel-tor ish-veh quarry. Ein t' wuh miscreants leapt vi' wuh masutra; vath ip-sut svi' gu'gelik sha'ti, wilat au vesh' afer-tor k' slightly, vi did ri puk, tonk'peh sahr-tor pa' k' wuh makh-yonet if au kahai svi' ish-veh limuk, ni ik au vesh' ulef blinded heh tevan-tor u' wuh hagik shi-kar-tor tor wuh reeking shek t' wuh vath sa-kan. Tra' vesh' pi' ralash tor nam-tor puzhu-tor tonk'peh wuh clang t' wun, wuh occasional screech il splash, heh slightly monotonously counting—kaukuh—shehkuh—stehkuh—ohkuh—naukuh—lehkuh—leh-wun. I nah-tor ek' vesh' hal-tor lu wuh travek t' savage sa-kan vikuvau kik, vi seemed ki' wuh sem-rik-tor ha'kiv, u' au potau au na' tchol svi' ik da-kuv t' yon. Au had ovsoh na' ish-veh dogs, tonk'peh nash sasu sa'awek seemed tor nam-tor wuh match na' au ek'. Va'ashiv heh va'ashiv au a'ing fi-tor ish-veh, heh va'ashiv heh va'ashiv au hewed wuh pa'shik ret. Au had abertau abru veh sa-kan k' ish-veh kik, heh vesh' using ish-veh u' wuh buckler, lu wuh'ashiv, vi had aishan be' dvun-tor ish-veh shek k'fai mullins, sprang vi' wuh shrau. “shitau abru ish-veh shek, sa-kan, ” maf-tor wuh newcomer, “nash sasu nam-tor t'nash-veh.” thus suddenly kik afer-tor himself limuk tor limuk k' peter. Wuh vath drew pla' heh shidau wuh mokov pa' au. Na' wu wuh dahkuh nemut glazhau na' veh wuh'ashiv, kik shuddering slightly, heh peter k' wuh flekh abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi-tor ish-veh limuk. “ni, sunil, ” leralmin-tor kik na' kim-shah, “nash nam-tor ek' ish-veh doing.” “ay, james kik, ” sarlah wuh harr-krus kilko-srashiv, “ish-veh nam-tor ek' t'nash-veh doing.” “yaut heh insolent youth, ” leralmin-tor kik, “dator tor ragel-tor thy doom.” “gu'gelik heh sinister sasu, ” peter kilko-tor, “ma na' thee.” rik' weht zhit au tevan-tor tor, heh na' wuh ret tra' vesh' rai advantage tor either wun-mor. Peter vesh' wuh superb swordsman, heh parried k' dazzling rapidity; ek'wak heh anon au zahal-tor abru wuh vup k' wuh lunge ik prah vesht ish-veh hahf’s defence, tonk'peh ish-veh shorter pulau lam-tor ish-veh svi' has-bosh stead, heh au kupi ri yetur wuh pishek ha-kel. Kik, scarcely ish-veh inferior svi' brilliancy, tonk'peh ri ved ni nimble svi' kar-nik mavau, punekwitau ish-veh pla' k' wuh rasath t' ish-veh onset, hoping suddenly tor shaht ek' k' wuh favourite kwit, saven-tor ish-veh wu ago k' barbecue na' rio; tonk'peh tor ish-veh astonishment au afer-tor nash kwit da-tor aside va'ashiv heh va'ashiv. Yi au sought tor ikap-tor heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh quietus k' ish-veh shek-tukh kik, if ek' nash wak had vesh' pawing wuh sov; tonk'peh peter dahtau ne' ish-veh heh, lunging fiercely, tilau ish-veh svi' wuh bak. Na' wuh glan t' ish-veh sha' khaf, t'vi peculiar kur, du vokau, vesh' offensive tor ish-veh, wuh shek tevan-tor s' kik’s el'ru, heh au vesh' na' peter’s mercy. “i'!” maf-tor ek' wuh sa-kan, tonk'peh k' wuh magnificent gesture peter invited ish-veh opponent tor abrashau ish-veh shek. Kik did ni instantly, tonk'peh k' wuh tragic olaya ik peter vesh' showing rom shid. Hitherto au had nahp ish-veh vesh' ein shaka fighting ish-veh, tonk'peh darker suspicions assailed ish-veh i'. “sunil, vi heh ra tanaf thou?” au maf-tor huskily. “i’m youth, i’m mak, ” peter kilko-tor na' wuh venture, “i’m wuh pi' kushel ik has pushau s' wuh yu-mur.” nash, veling, vesh' nonsense; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' skan tor wuh unhappy kik ik peter did ri fai-tor svi' wuh least vi il ra au vesh', if nam-tor wuh maut kov-suk'fek t' rom shid. “tor’t va'ashiv, ” au maf-tor despairingly. Au fought i' spo' wuh komihn flail, heh kanok fnashtaya t' ik terrible shek would ma ktorr svi' twain sovek sasu il sa-kan vi obstructed ish-veh; tonk'peh peter nuv-tor pauk ish-veh u' kuv wuh maut salan ish-veh tor blew ish-veh s' wuh tehvar shal. Heh va'ashiv heh va'ashiv au darted svi' heh pricked. Kik vesh' fighting i' rik' rok. Ik passionate thasek rai longer ya'akash na' ha'kiv; tonk'peh na' veh boon ish-veh craved: tor gla-tor peter gluvaya rasahkos shid fa' ish-veh vesh' samu ek'wak. Abandoning wuh puk au rushed vi' wuh grazhiv magazine heh pohshau ish-veh. “svi' dahkuh minutes, ” au maf-tor, “wuh hali dungi nam-tor blown tor krus.” i', i', au nahp, yeht shid dungi gluvaya. Tonk'peh peter issued s' wuh grazhiv magazine k' wuh fo svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh calmly flung ish-veh overboard. Ra wihfelau t' shid vesh' kik himself showing? Ashal-veh went pla' tor wuh mu-yor-nursery tor gla-tor kuv ish-veh sa-telsu vesh' asleep, ek' wuh sar-tak vesh' occupied. Wuh kanu bek-tor na' ish-veh maf t' mak, tonk'peh ish-veh did ri sarlah. Gla-tor ish-veh au, tonk'peh she did ri dva-tor au vesh' tra'. Gla-tor du, gla-tor ish-veh au svi' ish-veh sar-tak ni k'ashiv svi' ish-veh sahr-tor-tor ik she nahp nash vesh' aishan wuh sahr-tor hanging pa' ish-veh fam dvun. She hayal-tor ne' svi' wuh ku-san k' wuh yon, wilat svi' wuh hinek gad she had nursed au. Au kupi ri ken-tor nash, heh wuh samu pthak tevan-tor fi-tor ek' wuh rehkuh t' au. “ko-mekh!” wendy maf-tor. “ik’s wendy, ” she leralmin-tor, tonk'peh fam dvun she vesh' sure ish-veh vesh' wuh sahr-tor. “ko-mekh!” “ik’s john, ” she leralmin-tor. “ko-mekh!” maf-tor michael. Au fai-tor ish-veh i'. “ik’s michael, ” she leralmin-tor, heh she sakadau si' ish-veh kar na' wuh rehkuh pi' selfish kanu au would worla envelop va'ashiv. Ha, au did, au went pauk wendy heh john heh michael, vi had trel-tor s' sar-tak heh sahr-tor tor ish-veh. “george, george!” she maf-tor lu she kupi stariben; heh mr. Ashal-veh woke tor thresh ish-veh bliss, heh nana sarlah rushing svi'. Tra' kupi ri ma vesh' wuh lovelier glan; tonk'peh tra' vesh' rim tor gla-tor ish-veh kaula wuh pi' sa-kan vi vesh' staring svi' na' wuh krani. Au had had ecstasies va' ik vath kanu mokuhlek worla fai-tor; tonk'peh au vesh' looking k'fai wuh krani na' wuh veh mak s' if au bolau nam-tor na' ek'wak barred. Chapter xvii. Lu wendy grew abru i rok du aitlun tor fai-tor ra became t' wuh vath sa-kan. Au vesh' waiting ne' tor mazhiv-kur-tor wendy wak tor danau pa' au; heh lu au had tum-tor kaukuh hundred au went abru. Au went abru k' wuh stair, fai'ei au nahp nash would tor wuh weh-rom impression. Au lam-tor svi' wuh zehl svi' khom t' mrs. Ashal-veh, k' ish-veh taik ska', heh wishing au vesh' ri sai-vel-tor ish-veh pirate sai-vel. Au leralmin-tor nothing, tonk'peh ish-veh bezhun ya'akash ish-veh ki' au. Au ought ki' glazhau na' mr. Ashal-veh isha, tonk'peh au forgot pa' ish-veh. Veling mrs. Ashal-veh leralmin-tor na' wuh'wak ik she would ma au; tonk'peh mr. Ashal-veh vesh' curiously depressed, heh gla-tor au ik au panah-tor shehkuh wuh rather suk su'etek. “i bolau leralmin, ” au leralmin-tor tor wendy, “ik du don’t tor vel k' ulef, ” wuh grudging remark if wuh t'dahsu nahp vesh' sfekau na' au. Wuh wuh'rak t'dahsu vesh' wuh yaut veh, heh au ya'akash, flushing, “tor du nah-tor etek dang nam-tor nuh' mau t' wuh handful, osu? Fai'ei, kuv ni, etek mokuhlek hal-tor maf.” “sa-mekh!” wendy maf-tor, kolaya; tonk'peh fam dvun wuh wan vesh' fi' ish-veh. Au fai-tor au vesh' behaving unworthily, tonk'peh au kupi ri gol'nev ish-veh. “etek kupi ti dahtau abru, ” leralmin-tor nibs. “i kwon-hau-ov tresahk ish-veh isachya myself, ” leralmin-tor wendy. “george!” mrs. Ashal-veh sporiben, kusut-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh tal-kam veh showing himself svi' such wuh unfavourable ta'hal. Yi au thorau vi' bezhun-masu, heh wuh yeht'es sasarlah. Au vesh' u' glad tor ma au u' she vesh', au leralmin-tor, tonk'peh au nahp au dang ma ya'akash ish-veh consent u' muhl u' ish-veh, instead t' treating ish-veh u' wuh cypher svi' ish-veh sha' kelek. “i don’t nah-tor au nam-tor wuh cypher, ” tootles maf-tor instantly. “tor du nah-tor au nam-tor wuh cypher, curly?” “rai, i don’t. Tor du nah-tor au nam-tor wuh cypher, slightly?” “rather ri. T'dahsu, ra tor du nah-tor?” ish-veh da-tor si' ik ri veh t' au nahp ish-veh wuh cypher; heh au vesh' absurdly gratified, heh leralmin-tor au would talal ret na' au ek' svi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal kuv au fitted svi'. “etek’ll nunau svi', osu, ” au assured ish-veh. “yi zahal-tor wuh leader, ” au maf-tor gaily. “kashek du, i am ri sure ik etek ma wuh bestan-tvi-shal, tonk'peh etek pretend etek ma, heh ish-veh’s ek' wuh ka. Hoop la!” au went ska' taman k'fai wuh kelek, heh au ek' maf-tor “hoop la!” heh tam-tor po' ish-veh, searching na' wuh bestan-tvi-shal; heh i yen-tor whether au afer-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh na' sovek tav au afer-tor teruk, heh au ek' fitted svi'. U' na' peter, gla-tor ish-veh wendy wuh'wak va'ashiv fa' au flew maf. Au did ri exactly sarlah tor wuh krani, tonk'peh au brushed tehnat ish-veh svi' be' dvun-tor ni ik she kupi tu'ash ish-veh kuv she tishau heh vutau tor ish-veh. Ik nam-tor ra she did. “hullo, wendy, rom-bye, ” au leralmin-tor. “oh tal-kam, nam-tor du going maf?” “ha.” “du don’t olau, peter, ” she leralmin-tor falteringly, “ik du would spo' tor leralmin sovek-vel tor t'nash-veh mekhlar pa' wuh maut slor subject?” “rai.” “pa' me, peter?” “rai.” mrs. Ashal-veh sarlah tor wuh krani, na' na' la' she vesh' keeping wuh nasik bezhun fi' wendy. She var-tor peter ik she had thanai ek' wuh vath sa-kan, heh would spo' tor thanai ish-veh isha. “would du satau me tor shi'oren?” au inquired craftily. “ha.” “heh yi tor wuh office?” “i suppose ni.” “ak i would nam-tor wuh sasu?” “maut ak.” “i don’t aitlun tor hal-tor tor shi'oren heh oren-tor solemn vel, ” au var-tor ish-veh passionately. “i don’t aitlun tor nam-tor wuh sasu. O wendy’s ko-mekh, kuv i vesh' tor wake abru heh olau tra' vesh' wuh hisahk!” “peter, ” leralmin-tor wendy wuh comforter, “i dang ashaya du svi' wuh hisahk; ” heh mrs. Ashal-veh sakadau si' ish-veh kar tor ish-veh, tonk'peh au repulsed ish-veh. “potau pla', t'sai, kling nam-tor going tor kum me heh tor me wuh sasu.” “tonk'peh wilat nam-tor du going tor ha-tor?” “k' tink svi' wuh kelek etek torvau na' wendy. Wuh pu'a nam-tor tor shitau ish-veh pid abru among wuh lap fik wilat au yuk na' mu-yor.” “uf lovely, ” maf-tor wendy ni longingly ik mrs. Ashal-veh tightened ish-veh grip. “i nahp ek' wuh pu'a vesh' tevik, ” mrs. Ashal-veh leralmin-tor. “tra' nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh lot t' nu'ri ones, ” danau wendy, vi vesh' i' ved wuh ek'te'kru, “fai'ei gla-tor du lu wuh uzh kan-bu abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' wuh wuh'rak wak wuh uzh pu'a nam-tor pukeshta, heh u' tra' nam-tor kwon-hau-ov uzh kan-bu tra' nam-tor kwon-hau-ov uzh pu'a. Au ha-tor svi' ha-kel fi' wuh fik t' lap; heh wuh kihsh-kur ones nam-tor sa-kan heh wuh wan-kur ones nam-tor ko-kan, heh wuh pla-kur ones nam-tor aishan pi' sillies vi nam-tor ri sure ra au nam-tor.” “i dungau ma such mihrsh, ” leralmin-tor peter, k' bezhun fi' wendy. “ish-veh dungi nam-tor rather lonely svi' wuh khru, ” she leralmin-tor, “sitting k' wuh yon.” “i dungau ma tink.” “tink mokuhlek’t hal-tor wuh twentieth krus t' wuh yut pauk, ” she reminded ish-veh wuh pi' tartly. “sneaky var-tor-var!” tink puvutau si' s' ein-wilat pauk wuh teruk. “ish-veh doesn’t tukh, ” peter leralmin-tor. “o peter, du fai-tor ish-veh tukh.” “muhl, yi, sarlah k' me tor wuh pi' kelek.” “sos, mummy?” “certainly ri. I ma prah du ha-kel va'ashiv, heh i tvai tor potau du.” “tonk'peh au tor ni bolaya wuh ko-mekh.” “ni tor du, t'nash-veh ashaya.” “oh, ek' gas'rak, ” peter leralmin-tor, u' kuv au had ya'akash ish-veh s' politeness goh; tonk'peh mrs. Ashal-veh gla-tor ish-veh ru'lut twitch, heh she tor nash handsome nufai: tor kal-tor wendy hal-tor tor ish-veh na' wuh wehk gad kanok tevun tor tor ish-veh sikar cleaning. Wendy would ma preferred wuh weht permanent arrangement; heh ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh ik sikar would nam-tor wu svi' coming; tonk'peh nash ugaya satau peter maf ved sa-ka-ashausu va'ashiv. Au had rai kash-ral t' wak, heh vesh' ni bosh t' adventures ik ek' i ma var-tor du pa' ish-veh nam-tor goh wuh halfpenny-don t' au. I suppose ish-veh vesh' fai'ei wendy fai-tor nash ik ish-veh kim-shah zhit tor ish-veh vesh' aifa rather plaintive ones: “du skil-tor’t yen-tor me, peter, dungi du, fa' sikar cleaning wak sarlah?” veling peter ugau; heh yi au flew maf. Au nem-tor mrs. Ashal-veh’s shok k' ish-veh. Wuh shok ik had vesh' na' kling else, peter nem-tor ved easily. Funny. Tonk'peh she seemed satisfied. Veling ek' wuh sa-kan went tor shi'oren; heh danik t' au prah vi' mohrn iii, tonk'peh slightly vesh' shitau wuh'rak vi' mohrn iv heh yi vi' mohrn v. Mohrn i nam-tor wuh fik mohrn. Fa' au had attended shi'oren wuh wehk gad au gla-tor ra vralt au had vesh' ri tor hafau fi' wuh vikuvtra; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' nuh' tab-ma i', heh ak au settled ne' tor hasu u' ordinary u' du il me il jenkins minor. Ish-veh nam-tor maf ki' tor leralmin ik wuh tepul tor hash-tor gradually losrak au. Palikauk nana tied ish-veh ash'ya tor wuh sar-tak-lehk ni ik au dang ri hash-tor maf svi' wuh mu-yor; heh veh t' ish-veh mutaya k' gad vesh' tor pretend tor tevan ska' buses; tonk'peh k' heh k' au ceased tor seshayek na' ish-veh tel svi' sar-tak, heh afer-tor ik au dash-tor themselves lu au kal-tor hal-tor t' wuh bus. Svi' wak au kupi ri kauk hash-tor po' ish-veh taik. Aitlun t' practice, au puvutau ish-veh; tonk'peh ra ish-veh really tvai vesh' ik au rai longer pudva-tor. Michael pudva-tor longer do wuh vath sa-kan, hi au jeered na' ish-veh; ni au vesh' k' wendy lu peter sarlah na' ish-veh na' wuh shaht t' wuh wuh'rak tevun. She flew maf k' peter svi' wuh pelal she had woven s' mor heh nei-savas svi' wuh neverland, heh ish-veh veh pthak vesh' ik au lau beglanau uf pen ish-veh had shetau; tonk'peh au worla pubeglanau, au had ni mau tor leralmin pa' himself. She had glazhau fa'rak tor thrilling variben k' ish-veh pa' hinek wak, tonk'peh uzh adventures had crowded wuh hinek ones s' ish-veh kashek. “vi nam-tor khart-lan kik?” au ya'akash k' eku'ko lu she stariben t' wuh kesek nemut. “don’t du vokau, ” she ya'akash, putaurau, “uf du pustau ish-veh heh korsau ek' etwel ha-tor?” “i yen-tor au po' i stau au, ” au kilko-tor carelessly. Lu she sagluvau wuh vet-bosh rok ik tinker kus-vakh would nam-tor glad tor gla-tor ish-veh au leralmin-tor, “vi nam-tor tinker kus-vakh?” “o peter, ” she leralmin-tor, kolaya; tonk'peh kauk lu she danau au kupi ri vokau. “tra' nam-tor such wuh lot t' au, ” au leralmin-tor. “i gish she nam-tor rai weht.” i gish au vesh' gas'rak, na' pu'a don’t ha-tor wu, tonk'peh au nam-tor ni pi' ik wuh pen wak seems wuh rom du' tor au. Wendy vesh' kusut-tor nuh' tor talal ik wuh vesht tevun vesh' tonk'peh u' za-gad tor peter; ish-veh had seemed such wuh wu tevun t' waiting tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh au vesh' exactly u' sem-rik u' ek'wak, heh au had wuh lovely sikar cleaning svi' wuh pi' kelek fi' wuh lap fik. Thurai tevun au did ri sarlah na' ish-veh. She bek-tor svi' wuh uzh pelal fai'ei wuh hinek veh veling would ri ragel-tor; tonk'peh au worla sarlah. “sos'eh au nam-tor has-bosh, ” michael leralmin-tor. “du fai-tor au nam-tor worla has-bosh.” michael sarlah beyik ish-veh heh zhal-tor, k' wuh shiver, “sos'eh tra' nam-tor rai such person, wendy!” heh yi wendy would ma maf-tor kuv michael had ri vesh' maf-tor. Peter sarlah thurai sikar cleaning; heh wuh flekh vel vesh' ik au worla fai-tor au had din-tor wuh tevun. Ik vesh' wuh kim-shah wak wuh ko-kan wendy ek'wak gla-tor ish-veh. Na' wuh pi' longer she ar'kada na' ish-veh sake ri ki' growing kusut-tor; heh she olau she vesh' untrue tor ish-veh lu she prah wuh prize na' paik fai-tukh. Tonk'peh wuh tevun sarlah heh went rik' bringing wuh careless sa-kan; heh lu au ragel-tor va'ashiv wendy vesh' wuh telik kosu, heh peter vesh' rai weht tor ish-veh do wuh pi' grazhiv svi' wuh natuhn svi' if she had potau ish-veh leitri. Wendy vesh' grown abru. Du bolaya ri nam-tor sorry na' ish-veh. She vesh' veh t' wuh ves ik tishau tor tor'ovau abru. Svi' wuh shaht she grew abru t' ish-veh sha' el-dvelan wuh gad quicker do vath ko-kan. Ek' wuh sa-kan vesh' grown abru heh ovsoh na' k' nash wak; ni ish-veh nam-tor scarcely don du' taran sovek-vel weht pa' au. Du lau gla-tor wuh t'dahsu heh nibs heh curly sovek gad going tor wuh office, tik carrying wuh pi' sa'haf heh wuh umbrella. Michael nam-tor wuh mishu-yetursu. Slightly telik wuh t'sai t' title, heh ni au became wuh s'haile. Gla-tor du ik judge svi' wuh wig coming si' na' wuh shek-tukh svep? Ik nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor tootles. Wuh bearded sasu vi doesn’t fai-tor sovek var tor var-tor ish-veh kanu vesh' wuh'wak john. Wendy vesh' telik svi' wan-kur k' wuh faf-kur sash. Ish-veh nam-tor flekh tor nah-tor ik peter did ri alight svi' wuh church heh zadau wuh banns. Tevun padukau fi' va'ashiv, heh wendy had wuh ko-fu. Nash ought ri tor nam-tor written svi' neshuk tonk'peh svi' wuh pi-maat-kur splash. She vesh' puvutau jane, heh kwon-hau-ov had wuh shaik inquiring glazhau, u' kuv s' wuh moment she lasha fi' wuh mainland she aitlu tor ya'akash deshkau. Lu she vesh' hinek hiyet tor ya'akash au au vesh' mostly pa' peter sunil. She ashau tor zhu-tor t' peter, heh wendy var-tor ish-veh ek' she kupi vokau svi' wuh maut nursery s' if wuh khinik hash had taken shi. Ish-veh vesh' jane’s nursery i', na' ish-veh sa-mekh had bought ish-veh na' wuh rehkuh fundauik cents s' wendy’s sa-mekh, vi vesh' rai longer tishau t' kaiden. Mrs. Ashal-veh vesh' i' tevik heh yen-tor. Tra' vesh' goh dahkuh sar-tak svi' wuh nursery i', jane’s heh ish-veh nurse’s; heh tra' vesh' rai kennel, na' nana isha had be' dvun-tor maf. She tev-tor t' hinek ya'shakhuv, heh na' wuh shaht she had vesh' rather rihagik tor prah fi' k'; hasu maut firmly convinced ik kling fai-tor uf tor glazhau po' kanu kaula herself. Wuh'wak wuh wehk gad jane’s nurse had ish-veh khru ska'; heh yi ish-veh vesh' wendy’s krus tor shitau jane tor sar-tak. Ik vesh' wuh wak na' var. Ish-veh vesh' jane’s fereik-vel tor ashenau wuh thalv abru' ish-veh ko-mekh’s patam heh ish-veh sha', thus tor wuh ith'du, heh svi' wuh awful mu'khlup'es tor zhal: “ra tor gla-tor etek i'?” “i don’t nah-tor gla-tor nash-veh sovek-vel tor-mu-yor, ” leralmin-tor wendy, k' wuh olaya ik kuv nana vesh' la' she would vel tor further conversation. “ha, du tor, ” leralmin-tor jane, “gla-tor du lu du vesh' wuh pi' ko-kan.” “ik nam-tor wuh akarshif ago, sweetheart, ” leralmin-tor wendy. “ah me, uf wak hash-tor!” “tor ish-veh hash-tor, ” ya'akash wuh artful kan, “wuh yut du flew lu du vesh' wuh pi' ko-kan?” “wuh yut i flew? Tor du fai-tor, jane, i sometimes wonder whether i ek'wak did really hash-tor.” “ha, du did.” “wuh tal-kam hinek gad lu i kupi hash-tor!” “po mokuhlek’t du hash-tor i', ko-mekh?” “fai'ei i am grown abru, dearest. Lu sutra tor'ovau abru au yen-tor wuh yut.” “po tor au yen-tor wuh yut?” “fai'ei au nam-tor rai longer sa-ka-ashausu heh innocent heh heartless. Ish-veh nam-tor goh wuh sa-ka-ashausu heh innocent heh heartless vi mokuhlek hash-tor.” “ra nam-tor sa-ka-ashausu heh innocent heh heartless? I tor istaya i vesh' sa-ka-ashausu heh innocent heh heartless.” il sos'eh wendy nafai-tor she tor gla-tor vel. “i tor dva-tor, ” she leralmin-tor, “ik ish-veh nam-tor nash nursery.” “i tor dva-tor ish-veh nam-tor, ” leralmin-tor jane. “hal-tor fi'.” au nam-tor i' fihal-tor fi' wuh lo'uk adventure t' wuh mu-yor lu peter flew svi' looking na' ish-veh duv. “wuh duhik katravahsu, ” leralmin-tor wendy, “ar'kada tor terpau ish-veh fi' k' pu, heh lu au kupi ri au maf-tor, heh ik woke me, heh i og-tor ish-veh fi' na' ish-veh.” “du ma din-tor wuh zeshau, ” svi-shau jane, vi i' fai-tor wuh var weh-rom do ish-veh ko-mekh. “lu gla-tor du ish-veh sitting fi' wuh lan-tol maf-tor, ra did du leralmin?” “i hayal-tor abru svi' sar-tak heh i leralmin-tor, ‘sa-kan, po nam-tor du maf-tor?’” “ha, ik vesh' ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor jane, k' wuh suk' esh. “heh yi au flew etek ek' maf tor wuh neverland heh wuh pu'a heh wuh pirates heh wuh redskins heh wuh mermaids’ masutra-muzh, heh wuh ha-kel ne' wuh solektra, heh wuh pi' kelek.” “ha! If did du spo' buhfik t' ek'?” “i nah-tor i tishau wuh ha-kel ne' wuh solektra buhfik t' ek'.” “ha, ni tor i. Ra vesh' wuh kim-shah vel peter ek'wak leralmin-tor tor du?” “wuh kim-shah vel au ek'wak leralmin-tor tor me vesh', ‘aishan kwon-hau-ov nam-tor waiting na' me, heh yi ein mu-yor du dungi zhu-tor me crowing.’” “ha.” “tonk'peh, alas, au forgot ek' pa' me, ” wendy leralmin-tor ish-veh k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. She vesh' u' grown abru u' ik. “ra did ish-veh kushel ralash spo'?” jane ya'akash veh khru. “ish-veh vesh' spo' nash, ” wendy leralmin-tor, trying tor va'amau peter’s kushel. “rai, ish-veh wasn’t, ” jane leralmin-tor gravely, “ish-veh vesh' spo' nash; ” heh she did ish-veh ek'wak ni mau weh-rom do ish-veh ko-mekh. Wendy vesh' wuh pi' startled. “t'nash-veh ashal-veh, uf mokuhlek du fai-tor?” “i k'ashiv zhu-tor ish-veh lu i am sleeping, ” jane leralmin-tor. “ah ha, wehk ko-kan zhu-tor ish-veh lu au nam-tor sleeping, tonk'peh i vesh' wuh goh veh vi puzhu-tor ish-veh kum'i.” “kunli du, ” leralmin-tor jane. Heh yi veh mu-yor sarlah wuh tragedy. Ish-veh vesh' wuh sikar t' wuh tevun, heh wuh var had vesh' var-tor na' wuh mu-yor, heh jane vesh' i' asleep svi' ish-veh sar-tak. Wendy vesh' sitting fi' wuh lan-tol, maut beyik wuh yon, ni u' tor gla-tor tor darn, na' tra' vesh' rai vath ta'hal svi' wuh nursery; heh du' she hayal-tor darning she puzhu-tor wuh kushel. Yi wuh krani blew tu'ash u' t' hinek, heh peter eku-tor svi' fi' wuh lan-tol. Au vesh' exactly wuh ka u' ek'wak, heh wendy gla-tor na' wuh'wak ik au fam dvun had ek' ish-veh wuh'rak zud. Au vesh' wuh pi' sa-kan, heh she vesh' grown abru. She huddled k' wuh yon ri daring tor dvun, helpless heh guilty, wuh suk' kosu. “hullo, wendy, ” au leralmin-tor, ri noticing sovek natyan, na' au vesh' thinking chiefly t' himself; heh svi' wuh neik-ha'khlup ta'hal ish-veh wan-kur sai-vel lau ma vesh' wuh nightgown svi' if au had gla-tor ish-veh wuh'rak. “hullo, peter, ” she kilko-tor faintly, squeezing herself u' pi' u' tor-yehat. Vel svi'udish ish-veh vesh' maf-tor “kosu, kosu, kal-tor hal-tor t' me.” “hullo, wilat nam-tor john?” au ya'akash, suddenly missing wuh wuh sar-tak. “john nam-tor ri la' i', ” she hushau. “nam-tor michael asleep?” au ya'akash, k' wuh careless glance na' jane. “ha, ” she kilko-tor; heh i' she olau ik she vesh' untrue tor jane u' muhl u' tor peter. “ik nam-tor ri michael, ” she leralmin-tor sahris, lest wuh judgment dang tevan fi' ish-veh. Peter glazhau. “hullo, nam-tor ish-veh wuh uzh veh?” “ha.” “sa-kan il ko-kan?” “ko-kan.” i' surely au would ken-tor; tonk'peh ri wuh zeshau t' ish-veh. “peter, ” she leralmin-tor, faltering, “nam-tor du expecting me tor hash-tor maf k' du?” “veling; ik nam-tor po ki'sarlah nash-veh.” au hau wuh pi' sternly, “ma du yen-tor ik nash nam-tor sikar cleaning wak?” she fai-tor ish-veh vesh' nam-tor-fam tor leralmin ik au had kal-tor wehk sikar cleaning wak be' dvun. “i mokuhlek’t sarlah, ” she leralmin-tor apologetically, “i ma yen-tor uf tor hash-tor.” “i’ll ak saven-tor du va'ashiv.” “o peter, don’t thinoi wuh pu'a grazhiv fi' me.” she had risen; heh i' na' kim-shah wuh pthak assailed ish-veh. “ra nam-tor ish-veh?” au maf-tor, shrinking. “i dungi da-tor abru wuh ta'hal, ” she leralmin-tor, “heh yi du mokuhlek gla-tor na' yourself.” na' siyah wuh goh wak svi' ish-veh ha'kiv ik i fai-tor t', peter vesh' kwes. “don’t da-tor abru wuh ta'hal, ” au maf-tor. She kal-tor ish-veh el'ru mavau svi' wuh isachya t' wuh tragic sa-kan. She vesh' ri wuh pi' ko-kan khaf-spol-pushau pa' ish-veh; she vesh' wuh grown kosu smiling na' ish-veh ek', tonk'peh au vesh' masupik-eyed abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Yi she da-tor abru wuh ta'hal, heh peter gla-tor. Au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh maf t' kusut; heh lu wuh ha-vol vaksurik creature stooped tor abertau ish-veh svi' ish-veh kar au drew pla' sharply. “ra nam-tor ish-veh?” au maf-tor va'ashiv. She had tor var-tor ish-veh. “i am hinek, peter. I am ek'wak ni mau weht do dah-leh. I grew abru wu ago.” “du ugau ri tor!” “i couldn’t gol'nev ish-veh. I am wuh telik kosu, peter.” “rai, du’re ri.” “ha, heh wuh pi' ko-kan svi' wuh sar-tak nam-tor t'nash-veh kan-bu.” “rai, she’s ri.” tonk'peh au supposed she vesh'; heh au nem-tor wuh ash na' wuh sleeping kan k' ish-veh lipitah upraised. Veling au did ri kwul. Au hayal-tor ne' fi' wuh lan-tol instead heh sobbed; heh wendy did ri fai-tor uf tor comfort ish-veh, hi she kupi ma ovsoh ish-veh ni easily wuh'wak. She vesh' goh wuh kosu i', heh she sahr-tor s' wuh tvi-shal tor ar'kadan tor nah-tor. Peter fator tor maf, heh ak ish-veh sobs woke jane. She hayal-tor abru svi' sar-tak, heh vesh' interested na' wuh'wak. “sa-kan, ” she leralmin-tor, “po nam-tor du maf-tor?” peter she-tor heh ovalau tor ish-veh, heh she ovalau tor ish-veh s' wuh sar-tak. “hullo, ” au leralmin-tor. “hullo, ” leralmin-tor jane. “t'nash-veh ahm nam-tor peter sunil, ” au var-tor ish-veh. “ha, i fai-tor.” “vesht sarlah nash-veh pla' na' t'nash-veh ko-mekh, ” au danau, “tor nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh neverland.” “ha, i fai-tor, ” jane leralmin-tor, “i ma vesh' waiting na' du.” lu wendy fun-tor diffidently she afer-tor peter sitting fi' wuh sar-tak-lehk crowing gloriously, du' jane svi' ish-veh nighty vesh' hashan pauk wuh tvi-shal svi' solemn prahk'es. “she nam-tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh, ” peter danau; heh jane tev-tor heh lam-tor k' ish-veh vla, k' wuh glazhau svi' ish-veh limuk ik au tishau tor gla-tor fi' t'sai lu au gazed na' ish-veh. “au tor ni bolaya wuh ko-mekh, ” jane leralmin-tor. “ha, i fai-tor, ” wendy nafai-tor rather forlornly; “kling fai-tor ish-veh ni muhl u' i.” “rom-bye, ” leralmin-tor peter tor wendy; heh au she-tor svi' wuh sov, heh wuh shameless jane she-tor k' ish-veh; ish-veh vesh' already ish-veh easiest yut t' dvun-tor pa'. Wendy rushed tor wuh krani. “rai, rai, ” she maf-tor. “ish-veh nam-tor aishan na' sikar cleaning wak, ” jane leralmin-tor, “au aitlu me kwon-hau-ov tor tor ish-veh sikar cleaning.” “kuv goh i kupi hal-tor k' du, ” wendy spes-tevan. “gla-tor du du mokuhlek’t hash-tor, ” leralmin-tor jane. Veling svi' wuh shaht wendy kal-tor au hash-tor maf teretuhr. Etwel kim-shah glimpse t' ish-veh gluvau ish-veh na' wuh krani, watching au receding vi' wuh igen abi' au vesh' u' pi' u' yel. U' du glazhau na' wendy, du lau gla-tor ish-veh isachya becoming wan-kur, heh ish-veh khlop pi' va'ashiv, na' ek' nash pavesh-tor wu ago. Jane nam-tor i' wuh tsuri grown-abru, k' wuh ko-fu puvutau margaret; heh kanok sikar cleaning wak, kaula lu au yen-tor, peter sarlah na' margaret heh nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh neverland, wilat she var-tor ish-veh var pa' himself, tor if au shroi eagerly. Lu margaret tor'ovau abru she dungi ma wuh ko-fu, vi nam-tor tor nam-tor peter’s ko-mekh svi' da-tor; heh thus ish-veh dungi hal-tor fi', ni wu u' kanu nam-tor sa-ka-ashausu heh innocent heh heartless.
